1.1 UKkutt8wongash Jeremiah wunnaumonuh Hilkiah, sephausuen ut Anathoth, ut wutohkit Benjamin.
1.2 Ukkutt8wonk Jehovah peyaónuk ut ukkesukodtumut Josiah wunnaumonuh Ammon Judae ketass8t nabo nishwe kodtumwae nanawunnuadt.
1.3 Peyuam8 wonk ut ukkesukodtumut Jehoiakim wunnaumonuh Josiah Judae ketass8t: nô pajeh wehqshik nabo nequtte kodtum8m Zedechiah wunnaumonuh Josiah Judae ketass8t, nô pajeh missinóhkonae monchanónat Jerusalem, ut napanna tahshe nepâuzsaut.
1.4 Neit wuttinn8waonk Jehovah nuppeyaónukqun, n8wau,
1.5 Asq kahkenawahenoun ut menogkusseet, k8wahenup, kah asquam sohham8an wutch ôontomukqut, k8neetupanatamwáhenup, kah kukkehtimunup kukquoshodtumwaenúuneat en wutohtimoinnahtu.
1.6 Neit nussip, Woi Lord Jehovah nuttónteóh ket8hkon, newutche nen Peisses.
1.7 Qut Jehovah nuttugqun, n8wóhkon, nen peisses, newutche piṣh kuttom wame uttoh ánan8mun, kah uttoh áne ann8nun, piṣh kussin.
1.8 Wabesuontamúhkon wuskesuk8óash: newutche k8weetomsh, k[u]ppohquohwhununat, wussin Jehovah.
1.9 Neit Jehovah summagunum wunnutcheg, kah mussinnum nutt8n, kah Jehovah nuttugqun, kusseh nupponam nukkutt8wongash ut kutt8nut.
1.10 Naish, yeu kesukok kenanawunnumwahesh wutohtimóneash, kah ketass8tam8ongash, kodohchâbuhkohhamunat, kah soqunnumunat, kah pagwatauunat, kah kepuhkonat, weekuhkonat, kah ohteuhkonat.
1.11 Nano, wuttinn8waonk Jehovah nuppeyaónuk, n8wau, Jeremiah te[a]gwas kenaum? kah nussip, nunnaum Almonuntugque souobpunk.
1.12 Neit Jehovah nuttugkup, k8nenaum; newutche nukkenuppéhteo nukk8tonk ussenat.
1.13 Kah wuttinn8waonk Jehovah nahohtôeu nuppeyaonuk n8wau, teagwas kenaum? kah nussip, nunnau wussue ohkuk, kah wuskesuk nogwohteau nanummiyeu.
1.14 Neit Jehovah nuttinuk, wutch nummiyeu mahcuk piṣh pohqusheau ut wame wadohkitcheg ohkeit.
1.15 Newutche kusseh, n8wehquetum wame nanumie tahs8tam8e teateashiyeuongash, wussin Lord, kah nag piṣh peyaog, kah nag piṣh nishnoh pasuk ponam wutappuonk ahhut petutteamuk ut Jerusaleme squontamut, kah ayeuuhkonitue wame pummenutonganit, nahut weenu, kah ayeuuhkonittue wame Judae keitotanash.
1.16 Kah nukket8hkontam n8sittum8ongash, ayeuuhkonittue nagoh, pa[p]aume wame ummatchseonganooash neg ohquanumukqueaneg, kah chikohsumauwáog weetemungquok o[n]kotagig manitt8og, kah wowussittumwog nehenwonche wunnutchegane anakausuonganooash.
1.17 Newutche puttukquobpinoush kusseg, kah neepaush, kah nag us wame ne anan8nun: chepshúhko[n] ut wuskesuk8wóut, ishkont kuss8quttahwhush ut anaquabhettit.
1.18 Newutche kusseh, yeu kesukok kutogqhesh pummeneutausue keitotanat, & brasse pummeneutongash ayeuuhkonittue mamusse ohke, ayeuuhkonittue Judae ketass8tamwog, ayeuuhkonittue wussontimóm8uh[,] ayeuuhkonittue wussephausueneum8uh, kah ayeuuhkonittúe ohkee missinninnúog.
1.19 Kah nag piṣh kutayeuhkonukquog, qut matta piṣh kussohkunkk8og: newutche k8wettomsh wussin Jehovah, kuppohquohwununat.
2.1 NAno wuttinn8waonk Jehovah nuppeyaonuk n8wau,
2.2 Monchish, kah mishont8ash ut wehtauogkut Jerusalem, n8wash, yeu wussin Jehovah, kummehquanumouṣh, k8skenúe womoausuonk, k8weetauânumwae womoausuonk, asuhkiean ut touohkomukqut, ut mat ohteuhkausue ohkeit.
2.3 Israel wunneetupanatamweyeuop ut Lordut, kah ukk[a]keneumunne pénaeetuonk: wame neh mahchipwónukqutcheh piṣh matchenehéoog, machuk piṣh nukkuhkongquog wussin Jehovah.
2.4 N8tam8k wuttinn8waonk Jehovah, woi wek Jakob, kah wame teateashiyeuonga[s]h ut wekit Israel.
2.5 Yeu wussin Jehovah, teagwe matcheseonk k8sh8wóog nunnámteunk, waj nô8sukoihettit, kah asuhkomwog tahn8cheyeuuk, kah tahn8cheyeu8og?
2.6 Kah matta n8wo8og, uttiyeu woh Jehovah noh kohkuhk8unukqueog wutch Egypte ohkeit? noh pannuppe sagkompagunogkup touohkomuk, papashpe touushinne kah pasohthegane ohkit, papashpe kunkohteadteáeu kah nupp8ongane onkauohtáe ohkeit, papashpe ohke, ne matta howan woh panupwushog, kah uttoh matta howan wadohkeg.
2.7 Kah kuppas8unumw8 ut misségene ohkeit, meechinat ne meechummúonk, kah ne noh adt wunnegit: qut petutteáog, kenishketeomwop nutohke, kah kutunkquontam8wáhtomw8 nutohtóonk.
2.8 Sephausuenuog matta n8wo8og, uttiyeuoh Jehovah? kah neg weoggehheoncheg naumatuonk, nag matta n8wahik8og: Pastorsog wonk nuppann[e]setunkquog, kah quoshodtumwaenuog, quoshodtumwog nashpe Baaloh; kah asuhkomwog niṣh matta wadchiéhettégish.
2.9 Newaj, ashpumme keket8kauunog, wussin Jehovah, kah keneechan8óog wunneechan8oh nukkeket8kauóog.
2.10 Newutche paumhkash Chittimme munnuhhanaṣh, kah naish, kah ann8teamsh en Kedar, kah menuhke natwontaṣh, kah naiṣh ne nnák.
2.11 Sun wutohtimóin ôsowunáog ummanitt8m8oh, qut onch neg matta manitt88og? qut nummissinninnúmog ôs8wunnumwog wussohsum8ongan8, ne matta nompe wutcheihetteg.
2.12 Yeu chepshontam8k, woi kesukquog, kah mishu wabesek, kah mishe touussinok, wussin Jehovah.
2.13 Newutche nummissinninnumog usseog neesinaṣh machukiṣh: nag nutohquanumukquog nen pâmachúane tohkekomue, kah nag wunnehthamóog wônogquash, poksháe woonogquaṣh ne matta woh ohtan8g nippe.
2.14 Sun Israel wuttinneumun? sun noh missináe neetu? tohwutch mukk8kinit?
2.15 Wuske qunnon8og mishont8wae mehnehte[a]og, kah mahchumwéhtôog ohke: ukkeitotanaṣh chikohtaaṣh, matta wutohkeina[t].
2.16 Wunnaumonuh wonk Noph kah Tahapanes, nag pohquenumwog kuppuhkuk8e chetuhquab.
2.17 Sunnummatta yeu kuppaudtauònas kuhhog, waj ohquánumadt kum-Manitt8m Jehovah, sagkompágunukquean en mayut?
2.18 Kah yeuyeu toh|kutussen ut Egipte mayut, wuttattamunat wunnippeaṣh Sihor? asuh toh kutussen ut Assyriae mayut, wuttattamunat sepupogquaṣh?
2.19 Nehenwonche kummatcheseonk piṣh kussasamatuhhuk, kah kutt8nequssinn8wongaṣh piṣh kutáushk[ó]mukqunaṣh: newutche wahteaush, kah naish, ne matchit kah weesogkon kenukkenònat Jehovah kum-Manitt8m, kah n8wabesuonitteáonk matta ohtáno kuhhogkat, wussin Lord Jehovah ayeuteaunit.
2.20 Newutche nôadt nuppohquetahwhomp keyoakum, kah nuppaskukkomup keneepissuongaṣh, kah kussip, matta nuppannesu: nanwiyean kah nanwun8dsquaosean nishnoh kussohkôi, kah nishnoh ut ashkuhquamut.
2.21 Qut onch kutohtekônunup wunnégenne weenomwussippog, papannuppe wunnamuhkut[é]e wuskannem: uttoh kuttin neit quinnuppein nano matchékinne penoe weenomwussippog en nuhhogkat.
2.22 Newutche uttohkônogque kukkitsumwin nashpe nitre, kah kumm8chekiyimunat sope, onch kummatcheseonk kuhkinneasin ut anaquabeh wussin Lord Jehovah.
2.23 Uttoh woh kuttin unn8won, matta nunnishkhetteoh, matta nutasuhkauoh Baalim? naish kummay ut 8noikoiyeuut, wahteaush uttoh aséan: ken kenupshae dromedary papaumwushadt ummayash.
2.24 Touohkomukque asse, nukkodchu touohkomuk, assanómau wabanoh tapeneogish, tapeneog howan ukqushkinuh? wame neg natinneahwhoncheg, matta sauwunâou wuhhogkuh, ut wunnepâuzsómut piṣh wunnamheouh.
2.25 Nanawehteoush kusseet matta mokkussinnohhôsin8ut, kah kukquttunk wutch kuhkutt8nat: qut kussip, na matta annoósuonganinno, matchaog, newutche n8womon penuowhteaog, kah nag m8hche nutasuhkauóog.
2.26 Neane komm8towaen akodchik namehit: nene Israel wek akodchum8, nag ukketass8tam8m8uh, wussontimom8uh, kah wussephausueneum8uh, kah ukquoshodtumwaenúm8uh.
2.27 Adtamwéhettit weehquanunk ken n8sh[ú]n: kah qussuk, keneechansup; newutche|n[a]g nukquinnuppinumunkquog uppusquan8, qut matta wuskes[u]k8: qut wuttaméhpunáhettit, piṣh n8waog, omohkish kah wadchâninnean.
2.28 Qut uttiyeug kummatt8mog neg kezheácheg? neg omohkehettich, woh neg wadchanukquean w[a]dtaméhpunáon: newutche na adtahshik kukkeitotanash, ne wuttinniinneau kummanitt8mog woi Judah.
2.29 Tohwaj keket8kieóg? kenaau wame kuppanneséhtayimw8 wussin Jehovah.
2.30 Tahn8che nuttogkom keneech[â]n8oog, nag matta attumunum8og sasamatahwhuttuonk: nehenwonche kuttogkodtegan8 mahchipp8 kukquoshodtumwaéneumog, onauh pagwohteae qunnono[u].
2.31 Woi pometuonk, naish wuttinn8waonk Jehovah, sun nuttouohkomuk8imis ut Israel? pohkenâe ohke? tohwutch nummissinninnúmog n8wahettit, nenawun nussontimôumun, matta wonk kuppeyaónunómun?
2.32 Sun woh peenomp wanánatam 8nhogk8unaṣh, asuh weetauwadteaénin wuthogqunnumaongaṣh? qut onch nummissinninnúmog n8wanánumuk ánu[ā]nittu kesukkodtaṣh.
2.33 Tohwutch m8sittahhaman kummay natinnehamunat womonittuonk? newaj wonk kuhk8tomauadt matchet8wog kummayaṣh.
2.34 Ut sissippoe kuthogk8wonganit wonk namehteauun wusqueheonk kuttummunge mat woskhúog: matta nummiskom8un keme natinteaon, qut ut wame yeush.
2.35 Onch kuttinn8wam, newutche matta n8woskhuwoh, wunnamuhkut ummusquanitteaonk piṣh qushkemo wutch nuhhogkat: kusseh, kukkeket8hkoush, newutche kussim, matta nummatchesu.
2.36 Tohwaj m8cheke papaumsháan kutôs8wunumunat kummayash? ken wonk piṣh kutakodchawahik Egypt, neane akojheup Assyria.
2.37 Nux, pish kussohwéhtau, kah kenutchegash ohtag kuppuhkukqut: newutche Jehovah pogketam kuppabahtantamóongaṣh, kah nish matta pish k8niéhikk8unáṣh.
3.1 NOOwaog, wosketomp pogkenont ummittamwussoh, kah noh nukkonont, kah mittamwussit onkatog, sun woh wonk noh en qushkeu: sunnummatta ohke woh mishe nishketeauun? qut ken kenanwun8dsquáus monaog womónadcheg: qut onch quinnuppish en nuhhogkat, wussin Lord.
3.2 Tohshiniṣh kuskesukquash en qunuhqui ayeuonganehtu, kah naish uttoh kittin matta k8weepámutteanás: ut mayut kutaskwhonóog, onatuh Arabian ut touohkomukqut, kah kenishketeop ohke, nashpe kenanwun8dsquaôsuongaṣh, kah nashpe kummatcheseongaṣh.
3.3 Newaj sokanonaṣh kogkôunumuk, kah kutogque pehtùquom nanwu[n]8dsquoôsuenuut, kussekeneam akodchinat.
3.4 Sunnummatta yeu wutch kummauunnitteiyeu, n8sh, ken n8skenue nanawunnuaenéum?
3.5 Sun piṣh nagwutteánum ummusquantamóonk, sun piṣh wunnagwutteánumun pajeh wohkukquoshik? kusseh, kussip kah kutussep machukish neahunukukqunnittean.
3.6 Jehovah wonk nuttugkup, pamontog Josiah ketass8t, sun kenaum uttoh asit asóeposue Israel? noh kukkuhq[e]u en nishnoh kussohkôi wadchu, kah ut agwe nishnoh askunkquomut, kah na wuttit nanwun8dsquaôsin.
3.7 Kah nussip mahche yeush wame usseit, quinnuppish en nuhhogkat: qut noh matta qushkeu, kah wunass8muwae weetompassuin Judah wunnaumun.
3.8 Kah nunnaumunah, aquompak, wutche wame newaj omponcheposue Israel mamussit, nuppogkenóp, kah nuttinninnumauop pogkenittue wussukwhonk: qut onch wunass8muwae weetikkusquoh Judah, matta wabeseupoh, qut monchup, kah nanwun8dsquaausip wonk.
3.9 Kah niyeup, nashpe mataunchemoe, wunnanwun8dsquaosuonk, nishketeauop ohke, kah mamussup qussukquanash kah wehquanunkquamaṣh.
3.10 Qut onch wame yeush, wunass8muwáe weetompasu Judah, matta quinnuppu en nuhhogkat nashpe mamusse wuttah, qut eiantukiyeue, wussin Jehovah.
3.11 Kah Jehovah nuttugkup, assôeposue Israel anue sampwe ogquanumau wuhhogkuh, onk wunass8muwáe Judah.
3.12 Monchish kah yeush wahteauwahuaṣh kut8wongaṣh nogque nanumiyeu, kah n8wash, qushkiṣh ken asôepôsue Israel, n8wau Lord, matta ken8konkaúun8mw8 nummusquantam8onk: newutche nummómonaneteam, wussin Jehovah, matta nunnagwutteánum8 nummusquanittam8onk.
3.13 Webe samp8ash kummatcheseonk, kuppanneséhtáu Jehovah kum-Manitt8m; kah kusseáhham kummayash en penuwohteaut, ut agwe nishnoh ashkuhquamut, kah matta ken8sweetam8mw8 n8wadtauatonkqussuon, n8wau Lord.
3.14 Qushkek, woi asôep8sue mukkiog, wussin Lord, newutche k8weetauómunumw8: kah keneemununumw8, pasuk en pasuk otanat, kah kenehneesinunnénaôont, kah pish kuppas8unumw8 Zion.
3.15 Kah kittinnumauunumw8 pastorsog neaunak nuttah, neg sohkom8nukqueog wahteauonk kah wohwohtam8onk.
3.16 Kah piṣh n$nih, muttaán8óg, kah nanom8naóg ut ohkeit: yeush ut kesukodtash n8wau Jehovah, nag matta piṣh wonk n8wo8og, 8n8wae wut-arkum Jehovah: matta piṣh waantam8un, matta pish mehquontam8un, matta pish nátauwohtau8un, asuh matta piṣh wonkusséin.
3.17 Na ahquompak piṣh hettamwog Jerusalem, wutass8tamappuonk Lord, kah wame wutahtimoneaṣh en piṣh miyaém8aṣh, en 8wesuonganit Jehovah, en Jerusalem: kah matta piṣh wonk asuhkom8og uppehchuánumwe matche wuttahhou.
3.18 Yeush ut kesukodtash wek Judah, piṣh weechaáog wek Israel, kah nag piṣh mo[à]e peyaog wutch nánumohkit, en ohkit numauogkup k8sh8wóog wutche ohtóonk.
3.19 Qut nussip, uttoh woh kuttin kenugke ponunu[n] mukkiésut, kah kittinninnumauunat wunne ohke, wunne wutohtoongan8 mataànukeg wutohtimoneash? kah nussip, piṣh kuttehenneh, n8sh, kah matta piṣh kenukkoss8h.
3.20 Wunnamuhkut, neane mittamwussin wunass8muwáe nukkonont wessukeh, netatuppe kuttin wunass8muwae unnehhinneau, woi wek Israel wussin Jehovah.
3.21 Wadtauatonkqussuonk n8tunkup ut qunuhqui ayeuonganéhtu, mauonk, kah uppeantam8ongash wunneechanoh Israel: newutche woónkitteauog ummayeu, k[a]h nag wannanumaog Lord um-Manitt8m8h.
3.22 Qushkek kenaau asouhp8sue mukkiog, kah piṣh nunneetskehteoh kutasôep8suongan8oash: kusseh kuppeyaónunumun, newutche ken Jehovah num-Manitt8mun.
3.23 Wunnamuhkut tahn8che wadchanittuonk annoontamun wutch wadchuut, kah wutch mataánukish wadchuash, wunnamuhkut, ut Jehovah num$Manitt8mut wadchanaongan8 Israel ohteau.
3.24 Newutche akodchuonk mahcheteo wutanakausuongan8 n8shunônog, wutch n8skenúunneanónut: uffloksum8ash, kah wutheardsum8ash, wunnaumonauh kah wuttôn8uh.
3.25 Nussepsinumun nutogkojchuwonganunónut, kah nutchepshaonganun nunnuhkuhkonkumun: newutche nummatcheneheómun Jehovah num-Manitt8muh: nenawun kah n8shunonog, wutch n8skenúunneanónut pajeh yeu kesukok, kah matta n8sweetam8mun 8wadtautatonkqussuonk Jehovah num-Manitt8mun.
4.1 QUshkean, woi Israel, wussin Jehovah, qushkish en nuhhogkat, kah am[a]unuman kenishkeneunkquodt8mash wutch anaquabeh, neit matta piṣh kutontsappu.
4.2 Kah piṣh kutchadchekeyeuwam, Lord pomantog, ut wunnamuhkutéyeuuk, wut wussittum8onganit, kah ut sampweusseonganit, kah wutohtimóneash piṣh wunánumáog wuhhogkauh, ut wuhhogkat, kah ut wuhhogkat piṣh woweenauwaog.
4.3 Newutche Jehovah yeu wuttinnon Judae, kah Jerusaleme wosketompuh, anaskham8k kenukkonohkomuk8, kah tanohketéhteók asinnekôusséhtu.
4.4 Quôshquss8k kuhhogkaóog en JEhovahut, kah amaunum8k woskechee wuttahh8wae kodtuhquabeyeu, kenaau Judae wosketompaog, kah wadohkitcheg Jerusalem, ishkont nummusquanitteaonk ogque sohham8m8 n8taut, kah chikohteau ne woh mat howan ontham8g, wutche kummatcheseongan8oash.
4.5 Wahteauwahuwak ut Judah, kah n8tamwáhuwak ut Jerusalem, kah n8wak, puhpéquagk ut ohkeit: mishont8wak, miyaegk, kah n8wak, moek, kah ontuh pummenutausue keitotanéhtu.
4.6 Neepattau8k muttauákinash nogque Zion, menehketeau8k, pitchinnoéhteok, newutche nuppaudto machuk wutch nanumiyeu, kah mishe paguanuonk.
4.7 Qunnonou kuhkuhqueu wutch ukkuppiyeumut; kah noh pagwanont gentilsoh appu mayut: sohham wutch wutayeuonganit, wttauwushitteauunat kutohke, kah kutotanáoash piṣh mahchim8ash, matta wutohkeinat.
4.8 Yeu wutche, puttukquobpussuontam8k man8tionak, mau8k, kah 8n8k, newutche wutunkque musquanitteaonk Jehovah matta qushkemun8 wutch kuhhogkanónut.
4.9 Kah piṣh nnih ne kesukok, wussin Jehovah, ketass8t wuttah piṣh nupp8m8, kah wuttahhou sontimoog kah sephausuenuog piṣh chepsheau, kah quoshodtumwaenuog piṣh monchanatamwog.
4.10 Neit nussip, woi Lord Jehovah, wunnamuhkut, kummishe yeug as8kekomâog missinninnuog, kah Jerusalem, kussip, piṣh k8nohteamw8, qut togkodteg missigquonont keteahogkou
4.11 Na ahquompak piṣh unnôog yeug missinninnúog, kah Jerusalem, ponkque wuttin wutch qunuhqui ayeuonganit, ut touohkomuk, en nogque wutton8óont nummissinninnúmog, matta páuunontusseneat, asuh pahketeàuunat.
4.12 Pokkodche wuttin, wutch yeush ayeuongash, piṣh nuppeyaónuk: yeuyeu wonk nutayeuuhkonittue kut8kontamauóog wussittumoonk.
4.13 Kusseh, noh piṣh ogque kuhkuhqueu matohqshit, kah wutchariotsumash piṣh onatuhyeuash pemsquaut: wuthorsesumoh anue kenupshaog onk neg wompsikukquaog: missi nutonkapunnaongan8, newutche nummatchhetteamun.
4.14 Woi Jerusalem, kutchishittaush kuttah, wutch matchetowonganit, onk woh k8wadchanit: toh utt8che piṣh tahn8che kuttenantam8ongash kutappehtunk?
4.15 Newutche wadtauatonkqussuonk wahteauahuau wutch Dan, kah n8tamwahuwau onkapunáonk wutch Ephraimme wadchuut.
4.16 N8tamwáhuk wutohtimóneash, kusseh, ayeuuhkonittue wahteauwahuk Jerusalem, askuhwheteaenuog 8mwog nôadtit wutohtimoneat, kah ayeuuhkonittue mishont8waontamwog Judae keitotanash.
4.17 Onatuh nanwohkontogig ohteuk wutayeuuhkontamuneau waeénu: newutche ayeuuhkonittue nutcheketunk, wussin Jehovah
4.18 Kummay kah kutusseongash, kuppautunkqunash yeush, yeu kummatcheetowonk newutche wesogkon, newutche mussishin kuttahhut.
4.19 Nunnogkus, nunnogkus, nutonkquomom ut nuttahhut, nuttah mishont8wau ut nuttinnómiyeumut, n8nanum chequnappin, newutche ken8tamup, woi nukketeahogkou, ummishont8waonk monopuhpeg, ayeuteáont8waonk.
4.20 Paguanuonk asuhkaue pagwanuonganit mishont8wóm8, newutche mamusse ohke matchehteauun: kenuppe neekash matchehteauunash, kah nutonkwonganog kenuppe.
4.21 Toh utt8che woh nunnaumun muttaag, kah n8tamunat monopuhpékque mishont8waonk?
4.22 Newutche numissinninnúmog mattammag88og, matta n8wahik8og, nag as8tue mukkiog, kah matta wohwohtam8og: waantamwog matchesenat, qut wunnesenat matta wahteau8og.
4.23 Nukkehkeneamup ohke kah kusseh, matta kuhkénauwéhteósin8, kah monteagwuninno: & kesukquosh, & mat wequaiyeuméog.
4.24 Nukkehkinneamup wadchuash, & kusseh, nag nunnukshaog, kah wame wadchuash keme ontohtaash.
4.25 Nummomunneamup kah kusseh na matta wosketompaun8, kah wame kesukque puppinshasog wussem8og.
4.26 Nummonunneamup, kah kusseh, mishummeechume ayeuonk touohkomukqueyeu8, kah wame nish keitotanaṣh pohquetahhamunaṣh ut anquabit Jehovah, kah nashpe ummishe musquantamôonk.
4.27 Newutche yeu wussin Jehovah, mamusse ohke piṣh touwushin, qut onch matta n8wame mohtupanôog.
4.28 Yeu 8ch pish ohke mauun, kah kesukquash wohqut pish m8iyeuaṣh: newutche nussin, nuppogkodtantamun, & matta nutaiuskoianatam8, & matta nukqushkinnum8un.
4.29 Mamusse keitotan piṣh wusseem8 wutche ummishont8waongan8 horsesoh na8mukqutcheg kah wadohtompéitcheg, nag piṣh petutteaog kuppáhtu, kah piṣh tohk8tauaog kussampskôiyeuut: nishnoh keitotan piṣh ahquontamun, kah matta wosketomp wutaiyéin.
4.30 Kah matchéhenumuk, toh piṣh kutussen? tokonogque kuthogqunneat waneemsquag, tohkonogque gold k8n8whósuohtineat, tohkonogque kenenekinum8e wussukhumunat kuskesuk, tahn8che piṣh k8nekuhhog, womonukqueanig piṣh kussekanunkquog, piṣh kukkodtinneánukquog.
4.31 Newutche nutogquesittamup wuttauatonkqussuonk mittamwossis kodtauwekheont, kah ogque wutonkquommom8onk noh weske neechadt, 8wadtauatonkqussuonk wuttaunoh Zion, noh mawémont wuhhogkuh, noh sepaginuk wunnutchegash, n8wau, missi nutonkapunnáonk yeuyeu, newutche nukketeahogkou sauwunum wutche nushehteaenúog.
5.1 AH[a]úhsukque u[s]ishunk ut pannuppe Jerusaleme toumáogquehtu, kah yeuyeu naum8k kah wahteau8k, kah nuttinneohteagk na$ut mishe ayeuonganehtu: woh naméheadt wosketomp, noh asein wussittum[ò]onk, kah piṣh nutahquontamwòntamun
5.2 Kah tohkônogque wussinneau, Lord pomantog, wunnamuhkut pann8wae chadchekeyeuwaog.
5.3 Woi Jehovah, sunnummatta kuskesukquash ohtano wunnamuhkuteyeuuk? nag kuttogkomóog, qut nag neuantam8og, nag kummahtupanòog, qut sekeneamwog attumunumun sasamatawhuttuonk, nag anue menehketeoog wuskesuk8oaṣh onk ne qussuk, sekenamwog qushke[u].
5.4 Newaj n8wau, wunnamuhkut yeug matchekuog, as8tuog, newutche mat wahteau8og umm[a]y Jehovah; asuh 8sittum8onk um-Manitt8m8oh.
5.5 Nutauon masugkenukeg, kah nag nukken8naog, newutche neg wahteauog ummay Jehovah, kah 8sittum8onk um-Manitt8m8uh: qut yeug papannuppe pokqshanáog yoakoh, kah paskúhkomwog kenepsuongash.
5.6 Newaj piṣh qunnonou wutch touohkomukqut pagwanon, kah wunnonkquae mukquoshim piṣh ummatchhheuh; Leopard piṣh askuhhum ukkeitotanáoaṣh: nishnoh pasuk na waj sohhog piṣh sokshanau, newutche uppanneseonganoaṣh monaaṣh, kah wutasôep8suongan88aṣh nano m8naaṣh.
5.7 Uttoh woh kuttin yeu ahquontamauunun: kummukkiésumwog nutohquanumunk, & chadchekeimáog neh mat manitt8enégeh: nag wamepwuhheog, neit mamussuog, & miaweog ut nanwun8dsquasenuog wek8ôut
5.8 Nag tatuppeyeu8og sohkom8nae horsesut nompoáeu, nishnoh pasuk kogkeahchewánumau ummittamwussoh weetatteamungoh.
5.9 Sunnummatta yeush pish nunnátauwohtauòunaṣh, wussin Jehovah, kah sunnummatta piṣh kukketeahogkou ann8tauòntam8 yeu ânak wutohtimoin?
5.10 Kuhkuhquegk uppummeneutonganit, kah pagwohteagk, qut ahque wámeneán8k, amaunumau wutonkk8asuongaṣh, newutche nish matta wuttaiheaṣh Jehovah.
5.11 Newutch wek Israel, kah wek Judah, ayeuuhkonittue ahche n8nass8mukquog wussin Jehovah.
5.12 Pann8waheáog Jehovah, kah n8waog, noh matta, kah machuk matta piṣh nunnuhkukkongk8mun, kah matta piṣh naum8mun togkodteg kah muhshagquodt.
5.13 Kah quoshodtumwaenuog piṣh wabanu8og, kah wuttinn8waonk matta appehtunk8og: yeu piṣh unneheóneau.
5.14 Newaj yeu n8wadt Lord God ayeuuhteanit, newutche yeu kutt8onk kussinneau, kusseh nuttinn8waongaṣh nunn8taúhteam ut kutt8nut, kah yeug missinninnuog wuttuhqunnú8og, kah piṣh ummahchipwunneuh.
5.15 Kusseh, kuppaudtauunumw8 wutohtim[ó]in wutch nôadtit, woi wek Israel, wussin Lord: ne menuhki wutohtimóin, ne kehchiyeue wutohtimóin, neg ukkutt8wongan8 mo wahteau8un, kah matta k8wohtam8 uttoh an8wahettit.
5.16 Uppetan[o]nou ne pohquohshine wenohke, nag wame menuhkesuenúog.
5.17 Kah nag pish meechwog kukkepenum8onk, kah kuppetukqunnunk, ne woh kenaumonog kah kuttaunog meechhetteup: pish m8whóog kuf-flocksumoh, kah kut-herdsumoh: nag piṣh mahchipp8og k8weenomwussippogquash, kah figsuhtugquash: nag piṣh matcheketeauog pummeneutausue kukkeitotanaṣh, uttoh adt pabahtantaman, nashpe togkodteg.
5.18 Qut onch ut yeush kesukkodt[a]ṣh wussin Lord, matta kutóshkoméh[e]n8mw8.
5.19 Kah pish n$nih, piṣh n8waog, tohwutch yeush wame unnéhenog Lord num-Manitt8mun? neit pish nag kenamp8hamauóog; neane ohquanumeógkup, kah k8wowussumómw8 pen8e mánitt8og ut kutohk8wóut, ne kuttattuppe piṣh wuttinneumuhkauóneau pen8wohteaog, ut ohkeit ne matta wadtiheéóg.
5.20 Yeu wahteauwáhuwagk ut wekit Jakob, kah n8tamwahuagk ut Judah, n8wagk,
5.21 Yeu n8tam8k yeuyeu, woi mattammag8weógish missinninnuog, kah matta wohwohtam8gig, neg wuskesukqutcheg qut matta naum8og, neg wohtauogkutcheg, kah matta n8tamóog.
5.22 Sun matta k8wabesúonumw8 wussin Jehovah? sun matta kenunukushomw8 ut anaquabeh, noh wanohtunk nagunt wutche kuhkuhheg ut ketahhannit, nashpe michemohtae kuhk8waonk, matta woh anùwushómun8, kah tôhkonogque wuttugk8moh 8wahwáabpénin, qut onch matta sohkom8uneau, tôhkonogque mishont8wóneau, qut onch matta wutaneukom8uneau?
5.23 Qut yeug missinninnuog ontsogquéhtamwutteaháog, kah cheketamwutteahaog: ontsogquehtamwog kah moncheog.
5.24 Kah matta n8wawog ut wuttahh8wout, yeuyeu qushontuh Jehovah num-Manitt8mun, noh sokenonteadt, negonáe kah maumachish ut wutaquompiyeumut: kenanawehteunkqun kuhquttum8e kepenum8e weekaṣh.
5.25 Kummatcheseonganooaṣh yeuṣh wutamaunumunáoaṣh, kah kummatcheseonganooaṣh kukkushpâdtamunk8 wanegukish.
5.26 Newutche ut kenugke nummissinninnumog, matchetoweenuog wáhsháog: nag unnaskwheteaog noh wânashont ahpehanoh[,] ponaog ápehanoh, puttawhôog wosketompuh.
5.27 Onatuh wadshiùhquneg numwabhettit psuksesog, ne ne numwohteau wekuwoont as8kekodteam8onk, ne waje nag mussugkenhettit, kah weenauweetuog.
5.28 Nag nano wunogk8og, wunampamukqussuog, nux paumuhkomwog wutusseongan8oash matchet8wog, matta wussittumoog pissaumatuonk, uppissaumatuonk touies, qut onch wunayeuog: kah wussampiyeum qunauwahikquit matta 8sittum8uneau.
5.29 Sun matta woh yeush n8ch nátauwahuwaunash wussin Jehovah? sunnummatta woh nukketeahogkou ann8tantam8 yeu ának wutohtimóin?
5.30 Monchanatamwéyeu8k kah úhquejishánumukquok ne ussen yeu ut ohkeit.
5.31 Quoshodtumwaenuog pann8wae quoshodtumwog, kah sephausuenuog nánawunnuwáog nag nashpe, kah missinninnùog womontamuneau ne n$niyeuut: kah toh woh kutussemw8 ut wohkukquoshik.
6.1 WOi kenaau wunneechanoh Benjamin, moek k8seemunneaut wuch nashaue Jerusalem, kah puhpequohto8k monopuhpeg ut Tekoa: kah ponam8k kuhkinneasue n8teau ut Beth-haccerem, newutche machuk nogquodt wutch nanummiyeu kah mishe paguanuonk.
6.2 Nutogquéheop wutta[u]noh Zion tapeneunkqussit kah wanegit mittumwossis.
6.3 Nanaushepsaenùh weeche uf$flocksumóuh pish uppeyonóuh: pish nag ayeuuhkonittue 8wéenikomukquonóuh: nag pish nishnoh pasuk tanadtupp8og ut wutayeuonganit.
6.4 Ayeuuhkonittue quagwoshwunum[ó]k matómpog: omohkek, kah kuhkuhquehtuh puhshaquadt: missi nutonkapunnaonganun, newutche kesukod paumushóm8, newutche wunnonkquae onkauóhteau sepagkém8.
6.5 Omohkek, neepoushádtuh, kah pagwatauuttuh ummishikkomukquash.
6.6 Newutche yeu wussinah Lord ayeuteanit, kouéhtham8k mehtugquash, kah ayeuuhkonittue pogkétinómukquae wadchukok Jerusalem, yeu keitotan woh nadtauahtómuk: noh mamusse sunukkuhchahh8waonk wunnashomut ohteau.
6.7 Neane tohkekom sohham8teunk wunnippem, neweyane sohwhôkon ummatcheseonk, chekeusseonk kah mukk8kinnuwáonk nish n8tamunaṣh ut wuhhogkat: neuantamóonk kah n8chumwuttahwhuttuongaṣh nagwutteohtaaṣh anaquabeh.
6.8 Kuhk8tomaúununach, woi Jerusalem, ishkont nukketeahogkou kenukkonuk, ishkont kuttauwushinnewahesh, ohke ne matta wadohkeémuk.
6.9 Yeu wussin Jehovah ayeuuhteaunit, nag piṣh pannuppe mukkupushquaog Israelle sekqshoncheg, onatuh weenomwussippog: ogque ompontinuṣh kenutcheg en man8taut noh máwuneadt weenominneaṣh.
6.10 Howan woh k6on8nog, kah âmómog, onk woh n8tamwog? kusseh, wehtauogk8 matta quoshqussausin8, kah n8nanumóog kuhkeitamun: kusseh, wuttinn8waonk Jehovah ogquontamwog ashpunâmut: matta wuttapeneam8uneau.
6.11 Newaj numwabetunkqueh ummusquantam8onk Jehovah: nussauunum kogkôunumunát: nussokanumauóneau mukkiog poquadchit, kah ummoeu mukkinneongan8out wuskenuog, newutche wessukkiin weeche mittamwussoh piṣh neemunau, kutchise weeche noh mahtauntog.
6.12 Kah wekuóash pish quinnuppem8ash en onkatoganit, kah weeche wutohtekonoash kah ummittamwuss8oh moeu: newutche nussummagunum nunnutcheg ut wadohkitcheg ohkeit wussin Jehovah.
6.13 Newutche wutch peississit pajeh noh masugkenuk, nishnoh pasuk n8suhkom hohchewontamóonk: kah wutch quoshodtumwaenúut, pajeh sephausuenúut, nishnoh pasuk pann8wae ussu.
6.14 Meeshane neetskehteóog wonk woskeheaongan8 wuttaun8uh nummissinninnúmog, n8waog, Wunohteagk, wunohteagk, matta wunohteaonganin8g.
6.15 Sun nag akodchuog ussehettit unkqueneunkquok? matchaog, matta akodchuog, kah onteauog pen8quoshun, newaj pish penusháhettit kenugke nag panushoncheg, uttoh adt natauwáheog, pish kepshaog wussin Jehovah.
6.16 Yeu wussin Jehovah, neepo8k maikontu, káh naum8k kah nat8tomwehteag kah nukkone mayash, uttiyeu wunneguk may, kah ne pomushagk, kah pish kenampteomw8 keteahogkoune anwosin8onk: qut nag n8waog matta ne nuppomushaunan.
6.17 Kah wonk nupponaskqhukqueogig, n8wahettit, kuhkeitam8k monopehpegane wadtauatonqussuonk: qut nag n8waog matta nukkeiketam8unan.
6.18 Newutche n8tam8k kenaau wutohtimoneash kah wahteau8k woi mukkineonk, uttoh ánag ut kenugke nagoh.
6.19 N8tash woi ohke, kusseh nuppaudtoh machuk yeu ut ayeuonganit, wuttenantamog meechummuongash, newutche matta kuhkeitam8og nukkutt8wongash, asuh nuttinnaumatuonk, qut uppogketamuneau.
6.20 Teag wutch weetemungquok peyogque wutch Sheba? kah weekemungquoke weekinaskq, wutch n8adtut wutohtimoneat kutchikohtae mag8onganoash matta tapeneunkquottinn8ash, kah kussephausuongan8oash matta weetemungquottin8ash ut nuhhogkat.
6.21 Newaj yeu n8wadt Jehovah, kusseh, nupponam togkussittassunoonk ut anaquabhettit yeug missinninnuog, kah wut8shineunk kah wunnaumoninneunk pish moae uppenushadtamuneau: weetatteamunganin kah weetompoh pish paguanog.
6.22 Yeu wussin Jehovah kusseh missinninnuog 8mwog nanumohkit, kah missi wutohtimoin pish tahshinumun sussippoe ohkeit.
6.23 Nag pish kogkonaog ohtompeh kah qunuhtug: nag onkapunohteaenu8og, kah wanne ummonaneteaonganeog: wuttauatonkqussuonk ogque mishotn8wau mehtahhannit, kah nayeumukquog horsesoh: ogque wunappuog ayeuuhkonukquean, woi wuttaunoh Zion.
6.24 N8tamumunnomup woweenodtumoonk, nunnutcheganunonash nano n8chumwiyeuash, kah mishonkquómom8onk nuttohqunukumun kah ogque onkquommomm8onk muttamwossis kodtauweekheont.
6.25 Sohham8teòk en ohteahkonit, kah pomusháhte[ó]k may$ut, newutche wuttogkodteg matwau, kah wabesuonk waéenu.
6.26 Woi wuttaunoh nummissinninnumog puttukquobpissuwontamók man8tiônak, kah pummuquáish pukqukontu: ogquohpâusish mauwemat kenukquttegheon, ahche wesogkone maumuttam8onk, newutche matchehuwaénin teanuk pish kenuhkuhkongqun.
6.27 Kutogque ponush qunuhquikomukqut, kah wonkônous ut kenugke nummissinninnumut; onk woh k8wahteoh, kah kukqutchteoh ummayeu.
6.28 Nag wame onkquanittamwe ontsogquehtamog, kehkomuwae pomusháog: neg wompohshog kah misséhchuog, neg wame anuskuwanùog.
6.29 Popotowegaṣh chikohtaash, mahmuttattag mohtutteau ut n8taut: sôbossumwaen tahn8ch sâbohsôsu, newutche matchet8wog matta amaunóog.
6.30 Nishke silver wosketompaog piṣh wuttehenóneau, newutche Lord uppogkenuh.
7.1 WUttinn8waonk ne paômukqut Jeremiah wutch Jehovahut, n8wau,
7.2 Neepaush ussquontamut wekit Jehovah, kah naut yeu wahteauwahuash kutt8wonk, kah n8waṣh, n8tam8k wuttinn8waonk Jehovah, wame kenaau Judaéog, neg petutteacheg yeush usquontamaṣh, wowussumónat Jehovah.
7.3 Yeu wussin Jehovah ut ayeuteaunit, um-Manitt8moh Israel, onchteo8k kummayeuoaṣh, kah kutusseonganuoaṣh, kah yeu k8to[n]kéhinuneau ayeuonk.
7.4 Pabahtantam8hteók pann8wae kutt8wongaṣh, n8w[a]og, wut-templeum Jehovah, wut-templum Jehovah, wut-templum Jehovah yeush.
7.5 Newutche papannuppe oncheteaôg kum$mayeuóaṣh, kah kutusseongan8óaṣh; papannuppe usseog wussittumóonk nashauwe wosketomp, kah weetatteamunguh.
7.6 Matta sunukkutchahôóg pen8wot, touwies, kah sekousq, kah matta seaham8óg mat woskehuwáe musqueheonk yeu ut ayeuonganit, kah matta asuhkauôog onkatogig manittoog, wutch k8woskhetteaongan8.
7.7 Neit yeu k8tohk[e]hinuneau ayeuonk, ut ohkeit ne anumauogkup k8sh8oog micheme kah micheme.
7.8 Kusseh kuppab[a]htantamumw8 pann8wae kutt8wongash, nish matta woh wadchiyeumukish.
7.9 Sun kukkomm8tomw8, kenushteomw8, kah kummamussimw8, kah kuppann8wae chadchekeyeuomw8, kah kutchikossumauómw8 weetemungquok Baal, kah kutásuhkauomw8 onkatogig manitt8og, neg matta woheogig.
7.10 Kah sun kuppeyomw8, kah keneepomw8 anaqu[a]beh yeu ut wetuómut, ne as8weetamuk wutche n8wesuonk, kah kussimw8, nuppohquoahwhunnitteamun ussenat wame yeush nishkeneunkquokiṣh?
7.11 Yeu weetu ne as8wetamuk wutche n8wesuonk, sun ne 8wekineau mukk8kinnuwaenuog ut anaquabeog? kusseh, nen nunnaumun wussin Jehovah.
7.12 Qut yeuyeu unk nutáyeuonganit ne ohtagkup Shiloh, uttoh negonne ponamomp n8wesuonk, kah naum8k uttoh ánteau wutche ummatcheseongan8 nummissinninnumog Israel.
7.13 Kah yeuyeu newutche k8wame yeush ussenáoaṣh anakausuongaṣh, wussin Jehovah, kah kukken8numwop, nompoáeu omohkéon, kah kódt8kôon, qut matta ken8tamómw8, kah k8wehkomunumwop, qut matta kenamp8hamomw8:
7.14 Newaj unnehteau yeu weetu, ne as8wetamuk wutche n8wesuonk, ne pabuhtantamóg, kah ayeuonk ne anumauogkup kenaau kah k8sh8óog, ne ánteauomp Shiloh.
7.15 Kah kussohwhôkôunumw8 wutch anaquabeh, neane sohwohteaomp wame kematt8oóg, mamusse Ephraime wuskannem.
7.16 Newutche peantamwanshúhkon yeug missinninnuog, kah ahque tahshinumwansh mauonk asuh peantamóonk, kah ahque nag ken8tamwansh en nuhhogkat, newutche matta ken8tauun8.
7.17 Sun matta kenaum8 toh ussehettit ut Judae keitotanehtu: & ut Jerusaleme taumaogquehtu?
7.18 Mukkiesog mukkinnumwog wuttuhqunaṣh, kah wut8shineunk m[o]utt[à]numwog, kah mittamwussissog tuttuhpunumwog ayimauwónat petukqunegaṣh wutche keichissonkusq kesukqut, kah sokenumauónat wuttattamoe mag8ongaṣh ut onkatoge manitt8h, woh numm8m8squehikqunnaóut.
7.19 Sun nag numm8m8squehikquog, wussin Jehovah? sunnummatta m8m8squeheauóog wuhhogkauh, chepshonat ut nehenwonche wuskesuk8óut.
7.20 Newaj yeu n8wadt Lord Jehovah, kusseh, nummusquantam8onk kah nummishe musquantam8onk pish sokanumun yeu ut ayeuonganit, ut wosketompaut, kah ut puppinashimwut, kah ut ohteuhkóne mehtugqut, kah ut ohkee meechummuonganit, kah pish chikohteau, kah matta pish ontham8un.
7.21 Yeu wussin Jehovah ayeuteaunit um-Manitt8moh Israel, ponam8k kutchikohtae mag8ongan8oash, en kussephausuongan8out, kah meech8k weyaus.
7.22 Newutche matta nukken8nomp k8sh8woog, kah matta nutann8noog ne kesukok pas8og wutch ohkit Egypt, papaume chikohtae mag8ongash, asuh sephausuongaṣh.
7.23 Qut yeu nutann8nonah, nussip, n8swehtam8k n8wadtauatonkqussuonk, kah nen piṣh kum-Manitt8mw8, kah kenaau piṣh nummissinninnúmog, kah pomushagk wame mayut ne ánunn8nunóg, onk woh k8niyimw8.
7.24 Qut nag matta n8tam8og, kah matta ahchúsittam8og, qut pomusháadtamwog ut matche metahh8wae kogáhquttuonganit, kah pittuanum8onganit, kah nag as[ô]ushaog, kah matta kutchittohshau8og.
7.25 Nadteuh ne kesukok k8sh8wóog sohhamwehettit wutch ohkit Egypt, nô pajeh yeu kesukok, n8wame ann8nomp en kuhhogkaut quoshodtumwae nuttinninnúmog, asekesukokiṣh, nompoáeu omohkeonish, kah ann8nogish.
7.26 Qut onch matta nukkeihketunk8og, asuh nutahch[ú]wusṣittonk8og, ut nag menehkehteôog wusṣittuppukan8, ánue ne matchesúmaog 8sh8oh.
7.27 Newutche wame yeush kutt8wongash pish kuttinnonáoash, qut nag matta ken8tunk8og, pish wonk k8weehkomôog, qut matta kenamp8hamunk8og.
7.28 Qut pish kuttinóog, yeu wutohtimoin matta n8swetam8gig 8wadtauatonkqussuonk Jehovah um-Manitt8m8uh, kah matta attumunum8 sasamatuhwhuttuonk: wanamuhkutéyeuuk nehtauun, kah tummesumun wutch wutt8n8wóut.
7.29 M8sumush woi Jerusalem, kah pogketash[.] kah maumatash ut qunuhqueu ayeuonganéhtu[;] newutche Jehovah uppogketamun, kah nukkodtum ne m8squantog pometuonk.
7.30 Newutche wunneechanoh Judah matcheseoh ut anaquabeh, wussin Jehovah; nag ponumwog wunnishkeneunkquodt8m8ash, wetuómut ne [à]hettamuk wutch n8wesuonk, nishketeauunat.
7.31 Kah nag ayimwog qunuhqui ayeuongash ut Tophet, ne ohtag wut8n8ohkôiyeumut wunnaumonuh Hinnom, chikoswónat wunnaumonáuh kah wuttaun8uh n8taut, ne matta anann8nog, asuh peyaumun8 nuttahhut.
7.32 Newutche kusseh, kesukodtash peyaum8, wussin Lord, matta pish wonk hettam8unat Tophet, asuh wut8n8uhkoiyeum wunnaumonuh Hinnom, qut sheteae 8nóuhkôi, newutche nag pish posekinóog ut Tophet, nô pajeh mat momishkán8g.
7.33 Kah wuhhogkauh yeug missinninnúog piṣh ne ummechuongan8 kesukque puppinsháog, kah wutche ohkee puppinashimwog, kah matta pish howan wutáma8hkauoh.
7.34 Neit nutchéqunapéhteoh wutch Judae keitotanaṣh, kah Jerusaleme taumáogquehtu, weekontamwe wadtauaonkqussuonk, wussentomwaen 8wadtauatonkqussuonk, kah weetauwadteáen 8wadtauatonkqussuonk: newutche ohke piṣh tauwushin.
8.1 NA ahquompag, wussin Jehovah, nag pish sohh8wuttauog wuskonash Judae ketass8tamwog kah wuskonoash wussontimom8oh, kah wuskon8ash sephausuenuog, kah wuskon8aṣh quoshodtumwaenuog, kah wuskon8aṣh wadohkitcheg JErusalem, wutch 8weenohkéenóut.
8.2 Kah nag pish wussephamunáoaṣh anaquoshik nep[á]uz, kah nanepaoushadt, kah wame kesukque kenauwameonk neh womonáhetticheh, kah neh wadtinninneumuhkauwáhetticheh, kah neh asuhkauáhetticheh, kah neh natinneawáhettiche, kah neh wâsumáhetticheh: niṣh matta piṣh mukkinum8unaṣh, asuh posekinum8unaṣh, niṣh piṣh annohkeyeu8aṣh ut wosket ohkit.
8.3 Kah nupp8onk piṣh pepenauau ánue onk ne pomantamóonk, nashpe neg wame seqshoncheg yeu ut matcheteatashiyeuonganit, neg ashqushoncheg ut wame ayeuonganehtu uttoh ann8kauog, wussin Jehovah ayeuteaunit.
8.4 Nano piṣh kuttinnóog, yeu wussin Jehovah, sun nag woh penushaog, kah matta omohkéog? sun woh amaeu, kah matta qushkeu?
8.5 Tohwaj yeug Jerusaleme missinninnúog assôep8shettit, nashpe machemohtag assôep8suonk? menuhkenumwog as8kek[ó]dteam8onk, sekeneamwog qushkenat.
8.6 Nukkeiketamup, kah n8tamup, qut nag matta sampwe n8wa8wog, wanne howan aiuskoiantam8 ummatcheseonk, anowadt, toh nutussen? nishnoh pasuk en quinnuppu ummayut, neane horse quogqueit en ayeuuhkonat.
8.7 Nux kesukque Stork wahteau kuhquttume wutútt8cheiyeum, kah wuskuhwhunan, kah ta[nu]ag, kah maméshashques kuhkinneasuog, ne woh utt8che peyahettit: qut nummissinninnḿog matta wahteau8og 8sittum8onk Jehovah.
8.8 Uttoh kittin n8wónean n8waantamumun, kah wuttinnaumatuonk Jehovah n8wetomukqun? kusseh, wunnamuhkut tahn8che wutáyimun, uppennum8uh Scribsog tahn8cheyeu8.
8.9 Waantamwog akodchuog, chepshaog kah tohqun[ó]og, kusseh, nag pogketamwog wuttinn8w[á]onk Jehovah, kah teagwe waantamóonk apehtunkqhettit?
8.10 Newaj mag8 ummittamwuss8uh en onkatoganit, kah wutohteuhkón8ash en nag woh ohtunkeg: newutche nishnoh pasuk wutch peississit pajeh masugkenuk n8swuhkom hohchewontamoonk, wutch quoshodtumwáenuut pajeh sephausuwáenuut, niṣh$noh pasuk pann8wae usseu.
8.11 Newutche nag meshanne neetsketuog woskeheaongan8 wuttaun8oh nummissinninnúmog, n8waog, wunohteagk wunohteagk, matta wunohteaonganin8g.
8.12 Sun nag akodchuog nishkeneunkquok ussehettit? matchag, wanneh mo akodchuog kah matta pen8quosho8og, newaj piṣh penusháhettit kenugke neg panushoncheg, ne adt8che nadtauwáhet piṣh penuhkonog wussin Jehovah.
8.13 Wunnamuhkut nag piṣh nummahtupanóog wussin Jehovah, matta piṣh weenomininno wenómwussippog, asuh figsash ut figsuhtugqut, kah wunnepog piṣh uhp8teau: kah piṣh áninnumauogish, piṣh uppaumukongqunáoash.
8.14 Tohwutch chequnappeog? miyáek, kah petutteadtuh pummenútausue keitotanahtu, kah naut chequnapitteuh, newutche Jehovah num-Manitt8mun, kutchequnaphikqun, kah k8tattamwáhikqun weeswee[e]pog, newutche nummatcheneheomun Jehovah.
8.15 Nukkenompadtamumun wunohteaonk, qut matta wunnegininn8, kah wunnáyeue aquompi kah kusseh wuttamehpunáonk.
8.16 Chequttumhettit horsesog mo wuttissittauog Dan: mamusse ohke nunnuksinea[u] wadauatonkqussue nehnehteanit ummenuhkeseumoh, newutche peyaog, k[à]h mahchep8og ohke, kah wame ne noh ohtag, keitotan kah wame neg nag wadohkitcheg.
8.17 Newutche kusseh nutann8n ask8kog kah kokatricesog ut kenugke kenaau, neg woh mat monehtauwooncheg, kah neg piṣh kussogkepak8óog, n8wau Lord.
8.18 Ayeukonittue tapene[á]uwontamun ohquanumoonk, nuttah nupp8m8 ut nuttinnómiyeumut.
8.19 Kusseh 8wadtauatonkqussuongane mauongan8 wuttaun8oh nummissinninnúmog, newutche neg wadohkitcheg nôadtut wutohtimóneat: sunnummatta Jehovah appu Zion? sunnummatta ukkehtass8tamomoh apehtunk8? tohwutch nag m8m8squehettit nashpe wuttinnukontunkanouh, kah nashpe penowe tahn8cheyeugish [j]
8.20 Kepenum8onk pámsheau, nepun wohkukquoshin, kah matta n8wadchanitteamun.
8.21 Newutche woskeheaongan8 wuttaun8oh nummissinninnúmog, n8woskhit numm8es: chepshaonk nuttohqunuk.
8.22 Sunn$na$matta balmun8 ut Gilead? sun$na$mat ponaskétuwosuenúun8? tohwaj mat uppomantam8ongan8 wuttaun8oh nummissinninnúmog, mat keteohtaómun.
9.1 WOi napehnont nuppuhkuk nippeyeu88, kah nissuppegwe tohkekommú8k nuskesukquash: onk woh nummau kesukodae kah nukkonae, wutche nashoncheg wuttaun8oh nummissinninnúmog.
9.2 Napehnont ohtau ut touohkomuk, pomushaenuog ukkoueongan8, onk woh nunnukon nummissinninnúmog, & woh nutámaéhtauóog: newutche nag wame mamussuwaenuog, ummóeongan8 wanass8muwácheg.
9.3 Kah nag ogque wutunkkinnumw8weenanú8 ohtompe, pann8wonat: qut nag matta wutt8wehtamóog wutch wánamuhkutéyeuuk ut ohkeit: newutche ohhontseog w[u]tch machuk en machukut, kah matta n8wáhik8og wussin Jehovah.
9.4 Nunnukqussek wutch nishnoh wosketomp weetatteamungoh, kah pabuhtánumúhteok howae weemattin: newutche nishnoh 8weemattin 8wománumoh, kah nishnoh weetatteamunganin, kekómuwae pomusheau.
9.5 Kah nag as8kekomáog nishnoh weetatteamungan8oh, kah matta eyeu wunnamuhkutéyeuuk, kuhk8t[u]mwontamwog weenannú pann8wonat, kah sauwunnaog wuhhogkauh matchesenat.
9.6 K8tohtuonk ohteau nôeu as8kekodteam8onk, nashpe as8ke[k]odteam8onk sekeneamwog n8wahikqunnaóont wussin Jehovah,
9.7 Newájeh yeu n8wadt Lord ayeuteaunit, kusseh, nag nummáhtuppaswóog, kah nukqutchheaog: newutche toh woh nuttinneh wuttaun8oh nummissinninnúmog.
9.8 Weenan8 onatuh kôuhquodt pámemuk, as8kekodteám8eyeum8: how[a]n wunohteae ken8nau weetatteamungoh ut wutt8nut, qut wuttahhut wutaskwhónuh.
9.9 Sunnummatta woh yeush n8ch natauwahuwáunash, wussin Jehovah? sun matta woh nukketeahogou an8tantàm8 yeu ânag wutohtimóin?
9.10 Wutche wadchuash nunnemunum mauonk kah maumuttam8onk, kah wutch touohkomukque ayeuonk maumuttam8onk, newutche nag mahchukkissuog, ne waj matta howan nah paumukáuonk, kah woh mo wosketompaog n8tam8og 8wadtauatonkqussuongan8 neetassuog, naneeswe kesukque puppinshasog, kah puppinashimwog, wussem8og kah monchasháog.
9.11 Kah nunnanomwonkquadtoh Jerusalem, kah dragonsog wek8, kah nuttauushitteoh Judae keitotanash, matta wutohkeinat.
9.12 Howan noh waantog yeu woh wohtog, kah howan noh wutt8n Jehovah kôn8nukqut, onk woh 8wahteauwáhuwon tohwaj ohke mahchum8g; kah ogque mahtutteau touohkomuk, matta howan ukqushkodteáunat?
9.13 Kah Jehovah n8wau, newutche ohquanumaog nuttinnaum[á]tuonk, ne ponamon anaquabhettit, kah matta n8sweetamóog n8wadtauatonkqussuonk, kah matta ne pomusháuneau.
9.14 Qut nag asuhkomwog nehenwonche metahh8wae uppehtuánum8ongan8; kah Baalim, ne 8sh8oh kuhk8tomungqhetteup.
9.15 Newutche yeu wussin Jehovah ayeuteaunit um-Manitt8moh Israel, kusseh, nag nussohkom8unoog, yeug missinninnúog wormw8d, kah n8tattamweheoog weeswe.
9.16 Nusseahwhóog wonk kenugke pen8wotheáut, nag asuh 8sh8oh matta waheáhettegeh: kah nutas[ù]hkaue n8sukqunôog togkodteg, nô pajeh nummohtupp[á]nonaóont.
9.17 Yeu wussin Lord ayéuteaunit, natwontam8k, kah wehkomok maumuttamwe mittamwossissog, onk woh nag peyaog kah wehkom nohtôe maumuttogig, onk woh peyaog.
9.18 Kah kenupshahettich, kah maumuttamwanshikqutteuh, onk woh kuss8ksuppégwoshómun, kah woh sohwutchúan nippe wutch kuskesukqunónut.
9.19 Newutche wuttauatonkqussue maumuttam8onk wutch n8tamun Zion, uttoh kittin matchehetteanan? nummishe chepshómun, newutche nu[n]nukkodtumumun ohke, newuthe nutayeuonganunonash nuppogkenukumun.
9.20 Qut onch n8tam8k wuttinn8waonk Lord, woi kenaau mittamwossissog, kah kuhtauog88ash attumunumhettich wutt8ne wuttinn8waonk, kah kuhk8tamok kuttaun8wóog maumuttamun, kah nishnoh pasuk weetatteamungoh, maumuttam8onk.
9.21 Newutche nupp8onk pajeh kuhkúhqueu nukkenogkunnégunó[u]t, kah petutteom8 nummishekomukqunónut, tummehtahwhonát mukkiog wutch poquadchit, kah wuskenúog toumáogquehtu.
9.22 Ket8kash, yeu wussin Lord, nupp8e wuhhogkáuh wosketompaog piṣh ogque penushaog an[n]óhkeit m8sohteuhkónit, kah ogque wunnukquttinutchánit kepenumwain, kah matta pish howan ummukkinum8unash.
9.23 Yeu wussin Lord, waantamwaen ahque woweenoaj ut 8waantam8onganit, kah menuhkesuen, ahque woweenóaj ut ummenuhkesuonganit, weenauwetuen woweenoáhkitch ut 8weenauaweetuonganit.
9.24 Qut noh waeenoadt, yeu$ut waeenoaj, noh n8wohwohtunk, kah n8wahik, nen Jehovah[ú]8, asee womoausuonk, wussittumoonk kah sampweusseonk ut ohkeit, newutche yeush nuttapeneaumunash wussin Jehovah.
9.25 Kusseh, kesukodtash peyom8ásh, n8wau Jehovah, nussasámatahwhônaóont wame neg quosqusaúsitcheg, kenugke matta quosqussausegig.
9.26 Egypt, kah Judah, kah Edom, kah wunneechanoh Ammon, [h]ah Moab, kah wame neg aongkoue apitcheg, neg ayitcheg touohkomuk: newutche wame yeush wutohtimoneaṣh matta quosqushôsin8aṣh, kah wame wek Israel matta quosqushausuwutteahou8og.
10.1 NOOtam8k kutt8onk ne Jehovah ánukqueog, woi wek Israel.
10.2 Yeu wussin Jehovah, nehtuhtam8hteogk ummayou penuohteaog: kah chepshontam8hteogk kesukque kuhkinneasuongaṣh, newutche pen8wohteáog niṣh wutchepshontamunnáoaṣh.
10.3 Newutche wuttinniyeuongan8oaṣh tahn8cheyeu8aṣh: newutche pasuk tummehtam mehtug wutch touohkomuk, (wunnutchegane anakausuonk anakausuwaen) nashpe togkunk.
10.4 Nag wunnohh8suog nashpe silver kah gold, kah ummenuhketunaoaṣh nashpe kenunkwhongaṣh, kah hammersaṣh woh mo ontohtáun8ut.
10.5 Ogque samp8kompauog palmuhtugqut, qut matta ket8kau8og: neg woh kenunóog, newutche matta pomushauóog: qushûhteógk, newutche mo woskéhuwówog, asuh woh mo 8nénehuóog
10.6 Newutche matta howan ku[ttin]unkou woi Jehovah, kummissugken, kah k8wesuonk mishe menuhki.
10.7 Howan woh mat quoshuk8an woi wutohtimóune ketass8t? newutche wutchayeum8 kuhhogkat: newutche ut kenugke wame wutohtimóune waantamwog, kah ut wame wutass8tam8ongan8out, wanne howan kuttinnunk8.
10.8 Qut papannuppe puppinashumóog kah as8tuog: nunneukontunk tahn8cheeyeu kuhk8tomwehteaonk.
10.9 Sepagenumwe silvere kodchuhkiyeuaṣh wutaaunaṣh Tarshish, kah gold wutch Uphaz, wutanakausuonk anakausuwaen kah sabasumwaenin wunnutcheg: 8nôagk kah purple wuthogk8un8oaṣh, niṣh wame wutanakausuongan8 nehtoe anausuenúog,
10.10 Qut Jehovah wunnamuhkutée Manitt88, noh pomantamwae God, kah machemapit ketass8t[:] musquantog, ohke piṣh nunnksheau, kah wutohtimoneaṣh matta piṣh tapenumóog appuwontamun ummishe musquantam8onk.
10.11 Yeu woh nag kuttinoneau, manittoog neg matta kesteo8gig kesukquaṣh kah ohke, neg piṣh pagwanuog wutche ohkeit, kah wutch agwe yeush kesukquaṣh.
10.12 Noh nashpe ayikup ohke ummenuhkesuonk, noh menuhketeau muttaok mashpe 8waantam8onk, kah sepágenumup kesukquaṣh nashpe 8waantam8onk.
10.13 Máhshant8adt, muttáununkquodt nippeaṣh ut kesukqut, k[á]h waabeteau óuwan ushpem8ut, wutch weekqshik ohke: ukkutshamwunéhteau nashpe sokanon, kah sohh8wunau waban8h wutche wunnompak8une komukqut.
10.14 Nishnog wosketomp puppinashim88 ut 8wahteauonganit: nishnoh sôbassumwaénin chepshau nashpe nukkeukontunk: newutche wussabassumwe nunneukontunkoh pann8waeyeu8, kah matta wunnashaonganéoh.
10.15 Nag tahn8cheyeu8og, kah panneusseae anakausuongaṣh, nadtauwahit pish matcheheóog.
10.16 Wutchippiyeum Jakob matta nah tatuppéin8: newutche noh kakenauwehteunk wame teanteoqussiniṣh, kah Israel wutohtauongane souobpunk, Jehovah ayeuteanit ne 8wesuonk.
10.17 Miy[á]numók maumachiaṣh wutch ohkeit, woi wadohkéan wonkon8sinit.
10.18 Newutche yéu wussin Jehovah, kusseh, nuss8wompagunuh pasukqut wadohkitcheg ohkeit, k[á]h nukquequenauánumwahheóog, onk woh ne wuttinne nemehtinneau.
10.19 Missi nutonkapunáonk wutche n8woskkitteáonk, nunn8chumwetáhwhutteaonk uhqueneunkquodt, qut nussip, wunnamuhkut yeu onkquanumóonk, kah m8che mos nummuk8ammattamun.
10.20 Neek matchehteauun, kah nuppémuneóhtanaṣh wame poskisháaṣh: nummukkiesumog nussohwehtunkquog, kah nag matta appeog, kah matta wonk howan nussépagunumunk8 nek, kah n8nohtunkoh nutunkwheganuh.
10.21 Newutche Pastorsog puppinashimweyeu8og, kah natinnewho8og Jehovah: ne$waj matta piṣh wunnihettit, kah wame uf-flockum piṣh seáhwhóog.
10.22 Kusseh, aunchem8kae wadtauatonkqussuonk peyom8, kah mishe wogkouéonk wutch nanumohkit, touushinnúwáhtinat Judae keitotanaṣh, kah dragonnekommukquaṣh.
10.23 Woi Lord, n8wahteoh ummay wosketomp matta wunnehenwoncheiyeum: mat ohtano wosketompaut, noh paumushadt, sampwutteauunat wuttaunehtuongash.
10.24 Woi Jehovah, sasamatahwheh, qut nashpe wussittumóonk, matta ut kummusquanittam8onganit, ishkont mat toh kuttintuppehu.
10.25 Sokenumau kummusquanitteaonk pen8wohteaut neg matta wahikk8uneg, kah wutteateashiyeuongan8wóut neg matta wehquetum8gig k8wesuonk, newutche mahchipp8og Jakoboh, kah umm8hwhóuh, kah ummahtupanóuh, kah tauushit[t]eauwahtoog wutayeuonk.
11.1 WUttinn8waonk ne pauhônukqut Jeremiah wutch Jehovahut, n8wau,
11.2 N8tam8k yeush wunn8wae kutt8wongash, kah ken8nok Judae wosketompaog, kah wadohkitcheg Jerusalem
11.3 Kah nag us, yeu wussin Lord Jehovah ut Israel, matánumunach noh matta n8sweetam8g yeush wunn8wae kutt8wongash.
11.4 Nish ann8nokkupash k8sh8wóog, ne kesukok sohh8wunog wutch Egypt, wutch missitchuogke sab[a]ssum8onganit, an8waon, n8swetam8k, n8wadtauatonkqussuonk, kah nish ussek, wame neanann8nunóg: neit pish kenaau nummissinninnúmog, kah nen piṣh kum-Manitt8m8.
11.5 Onk woh nutussem chadchekeyeuwaonk, ne chadchekéimogkup k8sh8wóog, aninnumauónat ohke ne taumogok sogkodtunk kah hony, ne âunag yeu kesukok: neit nunnamp8hamuk kah nussip, ne n$naj woi Jehovah.
11.6 Neit Lord nuttugkup n8tamwáhuash wame yeush kutt8wongash ut Judae keitotanehtu, kah Jerusaleme taumáogquehtu, n8wash, n8tam8k yeush wunn8wae kutt8wongash kah nish ussek.
11.7 Newutche nummenuhke chekeimomp k8showóog, ne kesukok sohh8wunog wutch Egypt, pajeh yeu kesukok, n$nompoae omohkeon, kah chadchekeyeuwaon, an8waon, n8swehtam8k n8wadtauatonkqussuonk.
11.8 Qut nag mat nosweetamóog, kah matta ahch8sittam8og, qut nishnoh pasuk pomushau ummatchetahhae wuttenantam8onganit: newaj nuhkunumauog wame yeu wunn8wae kutt8wongash, ne ánan8nog ussenat: qut nag matta wutussenáoash.
11.9 Kah Lord nuttinnuk, nushehteáuss8waonk namehteauun ut kenugke Judae wosketompaog: kah kenugke wadohkitcheg Jerusalem.
11.10 Nag qushkéog en ummatcheseongan8wòut negonne 8sh8uh, neg sekeneogig n8tamunat nuttinn8waongash: kah asuhkauáog onkatogek manitt8h, wowussumonat: Israelle wetu, kah Judae wetu nag pohquenumwog n8n8waonk, ne ayimauogkup 8sh8uh.
11.11 Newaj yeu wussin Lord, kusseh, nunnuhkinnumauóog machuk, ne matta pish tapenumohetteg pohquohhamunat, kah tôhkonogque pish nummauunnitteunkqunneau, matta pish nunn8tau8og.
11.12 Neit Judae keitotanash kah wadohkitcheg Jerusalem pish moncheog, kah mauunnitteauâog manitt8oh neh anumauáhetticheh weetemungquok, qut nag matta pish papaquanne 8wadchanuk8oh, wuttaméhpun[à]hettit.
11.13 Newutche ne âdtahshik kukkeitotanash ne kum-manitt8mog, woi Judah, kah ne âdtahshik Jerusaleme toumaogquash k8nahtómw8 altarash en ne akodchuwéyeu8k, altarsash ne adt chikkohsumuk weetemungquok en Baal.
11.14 Newutche peantamwanshuhkon yeug missinninnuog, kah tahshinnumwanshuhkon mauonk asuh peantamoonk: newutche matta pish nunn8tauoog maunnitt[t]eaihettit wutch wuttamehpunaonk.
11.15 Noh womonog, teag wutch appit neekit, mahche manishquaâsit m8náoh? kah wunneetupanatamwe weyaus kuppaumuhkunk: matcheseanish, kummiskouantam.
11.16 Lord kutussowenuk askuh[u]kquame olivuhtug, wunnegen, kah wunnummeechummu: nashpe mishe wogkouee mishont8waonk wutchikkossumun, kah wuttuhqunash pohqshaash.
11.17 Newutche Jehovah ayeuteaunit, noh ahteuhkonukquean, ayeuuhkonittue kukken8tamunk machuk wutch ummatchitt8m Israelle weetu, kah Judae weetut, ne ayeuuhkonittue aseaunshehettit wuhhogkauh, numm8m8sqhikqunnaoont, aninnumauahetticheh weetemungquok Baaloh.
11.18 Kah Jehovah n8wahteauwahikqun, kah n8wahteauun; neit kenaitussip wutusseonganóoash.
11.19 Qut nuttatuppeyeuup Lamb, asuh ox, noh pas8ut nushonat, kah matta n8wahteau8h ayeuuhkonittue natwontamunkquog tashipinanittuongash, n8wahettit, nehtauudtuh mehtug nashpe ummeechummuonk, kah tummehtáhwhontuh wutch wutohtuout pomontogig, onk woh 8wesuonk matta wonk mequontam8un.
11.20 Qut woi Jehovah ayeuteaunit, ken sampweusseáe wussittuman, ken quajheadt mutt8[u]nussog, kah metah: naumwáhe nag kutann8tauwaongan8, newutche k8wahteauwáhesh nuppissaumatuonk.
11.21 Newaj yeu n8wadt Jehovah papaume Anathothe wosketompaog, neg áchuwehteunkig kuppomantamóonk, n8wahettit, quoshodtuhkon ut 8wesuonganit Lord, onk woh mo kenupp8 nashpe nunnutcheganun.
11.22 Newutche yeu wussin Jehovah ayeuteaunit, kusseh, nag nussasamatahwhóog: wuskennuog piṣh nupwog nashpe togkodteganit, wunnaumonáoh kah wuttaun8oh pish nupwoh nashpe mahshagquodt:
11.23 Kah matta piṣh ushqushau8og, newutche nunnuhkinnumau machuk ut Anathothe wosketompaog, nadtauwáheáe ukkodtum8m8.
12.1 KUssampweusseaénu, woi Lord, keket8kauunon, qut kéket8kauwunnittei papaume k8sittum8ongaṣh: tohwaj ummay matchetou wunayeum8uk? tohwaj wame nag wanaihettit ahche wanassúm8wáe ussécheg?
12.2 Nag kutohtukónunk, nux, nag 8wadchabuk8og: nag neetuog, nux meechummu8og: ken kuppas8cheyeu8 wutt8n8wóut, kah kinnau8sukom wutt8unuss8uh.
12.3 Qut ken woi Jehovah, k8waheh, kenáip, kah kukqutchteóp nuttah en kuhhogkáiyeu: ogque sohwhun sheepsut wutche nashaongan8, kah quagquashweáh wutche paguwanittue kesukod.
12.4 Toh utt8che piṣh ohke mau8m8, kah wame ohteuhkonée herbsaṣh ohp8taaṣh, wutche ummatcheseongan8 neg na wadohkitcheg? puppinashimwog mahtsúog, kah psukesuk, newutche nag n8waog matta piṣh naum8 n8wohkukquóiyeumun.
12.5 Weechepohtómussoh mohtissita[h]shoncheg, kah nag sauunukquéan, neit toh woh kittin nunnôohkônon horses? kah wunohteáe ohkeit, ne pabuhtantamun, sauwunukquean, neit uttoh woh kittinheoh tômogkok ut Jordan?
12.6 Newutche kemattog, kah k8sh wek, wutass8muwae kittinhukquog; nux, wehkomáog monanutcheh kutásuhkunkqunat: wunnamptauúhkon, tôhkonogque k8wówunónukumukqunat.
12.7 Nunnukkodtum nek: nunnukkodtum nutohtóonk: neh nuttah womononcheh, noh nummagun wunu[n]tchegan8wout ummatwomoh.
12.8 Nutohtóonk tatuppeyeu8 ut nuhhogkat qunnonou$ut, nutayeuuhkonittue mishont8anumunk newaj sekeneam.
12.9 Nutohtóonk tatuppeyeu8 ut nuhhogkat chohchohkésue psuksesut, waéene psuksesog wutayeuhkonóuh: peyunk, miyaek kenaau wame ohteakône puppinashimwog nónche mahchep8k.
12.10 Monaog pastorsog pagwadtóog n8wenominneohteuk, nag tahtaskuhkomwog nutchippiyeum agwe wusseetowóut: n8ne chippáiyeum wuttauushine touohkomukquhkóneau.
12.11 Wuttauushitteauuneau, kah tâuushik nummauunnitteunkqun, mamusse ohke tauushitteáuun, newutche matta howan upponam8un wuttahhut.
12.12 Matchehteauwaenúog nuhkuhkomwog wame qunuhqui ayeuongaṣh papashpe touohkomukqut: newutche wuttogkodteg Jehovah piṣh pagwohteom8, wutch weekqshik ohke, onk ya$en aongkoue: wanne weyaus piṣh wunohteómun8.
12.13 Ohkehteopanneg wheatash qut nag pish kepenumwog asinnekoussoh: ponaog wuhhogkauh onkquommamwunneat, matta wutchienat, kah nag pish akodchuwontamwog k8chiyeuonkan8oash newutche wutunkque musquanitteaonk J[é]hovah.
12.14 Yeu wutayeuuhkonittue unnon Jehovah wamé nummatchetowé weetatteamungoh, neg masinukeg oht[ó]onk ne ohtauaheog nummissinn[n]inneumoh Israel, kusseh nag, nukkodtinoog wutch wutohkeout, kah nukkodtinum week Judah wutch nag kenugke.
12.15 Kah pish n$nih, mahche kodtinog, pish nukqushkem kah pish nukkitteamonteanumoog, kah wonk nuppas8 nish$noh wosktomp ut wutohtoônganit, kah nish$noh pasuk ut wutohkeit.
12.16 Kah pish n$nih nag menuhke kodnetuhtauwehettit ummayeuoash nummissinninnumog, chadchekeyeuonat nashpe n8wesuonk (Jehovah pomantam, neane kuhk8tomauwahettit nummissinninnumoh chadchekeyeuonat nashpe Baal) neit pish weekitteaog ut nasháuwe nummissinninnumut.
12.17 Qut matta nosweetamohetteg, pish nuppapukquané kodtinnumun kah pagu[á]tauun ne wutohtimoin, wussin Jehovah.
13.1 YEu nuttugqun Jehovah, monchish, nanashweetash womponákinne puttukquobpus, kah ponsh kussegkonóhtugqut, kah ponam8hkon nippeit,
13.2 Neit nukquagquashwe[h]tamup puttugquobpus neaunag wuttinn8waonk Jehovah, kah nupponamu[n]ah nusségonohtugqut.
13.3 Kah wuttinnowaonk Jehovah nahohtôeu nuppeyaónuk, n8wop,
13.4 Nemunush puttugquobpus ne quagquoshwehtamop, ne ohtag kussegonohtogqut, kah neepaush, âush Euphrates, na$ut adtahtaush ut qussukquane wónogqut.
13.5 Neit nummonchip, kah nutadtahtauun ut kishke Euphrates, neanann8sit Jehovah.
13.6 Kah nnihyeup mahche m8chetikqunogkok, Lord nuttinuk, neepaush, àush Euphrates, kah na wuttinuh puttukquobpus, ne an8nop na$ut adtahtauunat[.]
13.7 Neit nuttomp Euphrates, ka[g] nukkuthamun, kah n8tinum puttukquobpus ne adt adtahtauomp, kah kusseh, puttukquobpus anit, matta toh unnompâmunkquodtinn8.
13.8 Neit wuttinn8wáonk Jehovah nuppeyaonuk, n8wau,
13.9 Yeu wussin Jehovah, yeu nuttinne matchehteauun uppehtuanumóonk Judah, kah ummishe pehtuanumóonk Jerusalem.
13.10 Yeug matcheetoe missinninnúog neg sekeneogig n8tamunat nuttinn8waongash, neg paumushácheg ut matche metahh8wae unnantam8onganit, kah ásuhkauóncheg onkatogeh manitt8h, nag wowussumonat, kah peantamauónat, nag pish tatuppeyeu8og yeu puttugquoppissinit, ne matta toh ánompâmukquodtin8g.
13.11 Newutche neane puttukquobpus ogquám8k wussegonóhtugqut wosketomp, ne nuttinne ogquamwehteauun nuhhogkat mamusse Israelle wek, kah mamusse Judae wek, wussin Jehovah, onk woh nag n8missinneumúneunk, kah wutch wesuonk, kah wutche waeenodtuonk, kah wutche sohsumóonk, qut nag matta n8tam8og.
13.12 Newutche pish unnádt yeu kutt8onk, yeu wussin Lord um$Manitt8moh Israel, nish$noh wisq pish numwohtauun wine, kah nag pish kuttugquog, sunnummatta nuppapannuppe wahteomun, nishnoh wisq piṣh numw[â]panau wine?
13.13 Neit piṣh nag kuttinóog, yeu wussin Jehovah, kusseh, pish nunnumwohtauóog wame wadohkitcheg yeu ohkeit, kehtass8tamwog neg apitcheg ut wutappuonganit David, kah sephausuenuog, kah quoshódtumwaénuog, kah wame wadohkitcheg Jerusalem, nashpe kogkeissippam8onk.
13.14 Kah nuppápashkuhkónunk, wut8shimóog, kah wunnaumonáuh moeu wussin Jehovah, matta nukkitteamonteanumoh, qut nag nuppaguanóog.
13.15 N8tam8k kah kuhkeitam8k, pittuanumúhteok, newutche Jehovah wussin.
13.16 Sohsum8wáheuk Jehovah kum-Manitt8m8, asquam papohkina[n]teagkup, kah asquam kusseet8ash ta[g]shinheug pohkenae wadchuuhkontu, kah nadtauwompadtamóg wequai, ukquinnuppinnumun en nupp8onk, wutonkauontomut, ukkúhpogke po[h]kináhko[n]
13.17 Qut matta n8tam8og, nukketeahogkou pish keme mau wutche kuppehtuánum8ongan8, kah nuskesukquaṣh piṣh mauée mau8m8aṣh, kah penutchuanash nussippegwash, newutche uf-flockum Jehovah missinae monchadtauun.
13.18 Us ketass8t, kah sonksquaut, hohpaheuk kuhhogkaoog, nummatappek, newutche k8puhkuhk88onk pish n8keem8, kutchetuhquabee sohsumoonk.
13.19 Sowaniyeue keitotanash pish kuppohhosuash kah mattá pish howan 8woshwunnum8unash, Judah pish missinnae monchanau, neg wame pish mamusse missinohko[n]unk.
13.20 Táhshinum8k kuskesuk8oash, kah nok neg wagig nanumiyeu, uttiyeu flock ne ut anumauunumuk, ne wanégik flock?
13.21 Toh pish kussim sasamatahhukquean, (newutché nag kukkuhk8tomauoog ummummugquompainneaout k8puhkuhqunneat) sunnummatta pish onkquanum8onk kutogque tohqunnumunat mittamwossis neechadt?
13.22 Kah n8waan ut kuttahhut, tohwutch yeush nuhkuhkiit, wutché mohsag kummatcheseonk kussissippoe hogk8onk waahsheau, kah kogquanash pôhshkohtaash.
13.23 M8adthogk8nas sun woh 8wompheuh wuttuhquab, asuh Leópard wutchohchohkesuongash? neit kenaau wonk woh k8nhukquneau, nag wutteae matcheseog.
13.24 Newaj ogquesewahhog sequékepenum8onganit, ne pamshunk nashpe touohkomukque waban.
13.25 Yeu kuttittanohkitteaonk, kukquthum8e chippiyeum nashpe neen, wussin Lord, newutche k8wannanumeh, kuppabuhtantam pann8waonk.
13.26 Newaj naumwahuwi kussissippoe hogk8 ut woskeche kesukqut, onk woh kúkkosuonk nogquodt.
13.27 Nunnaumup kummamussuongash, kah kukkogkeinw8dsquaongash, kah kenishkeneungque mánisquaôsuongash, kah kutuhquneunkquodt8mash, ut ohteuhkonue wádchuuhkontu: missi kutonkapunaónk woi Jerusalem, sun mátta pish kuppahkhetteoh? uttoh adt8che woh nnag?
14.1 WUttinn8waonk Jehovah, ne pauhônukqut Jéremiah papaume mahshagquodt.
14.2 Judah mau, kah 8squontamash mahchim8, m8esuog pajeh ohkeit, kah ummauonk Jerusalem kuhkuhquem8.
14.3 Kah ukkehtauwom8uh ann8naog uppeissesum8uh en nippekontu, nag peyaog pasahtheganehtu, kah mat namehteauoog nippe, nag qushkeog mahchayeue wishquadt nag akodchuog, kah chepshaog, kah puttogquequohh8og.
14.4 Néwutche ohke passohteaem8, newutche matta sokanonunn8 óhkeit, anaskhamwaenuog akodchuog, nag onkhumwog uppuhkuk88ash.
14.5 Nux, quenegq wonk neechau ut ohteuhkonit, kah wunnukkonuh, newutche matta moskehtuun8.
14.6 Kah touohkomukque assesog neneepattag qunuhqui ayeuonganéhtu, nag assonómáog waban onatuh dragonsog: wuskesuk88ash nupp8m8aṣh newutche matta moskehtuun8
14.7 Woi Jehovah, tôhkonogque nummatcheseonganunonaṣh n8wauwaónukqunnanonaṣh, ne ussish wutche k8wesuonk: newutche nutassôéhpósuonganunonaṣh monataṣh, kummatchenéhennumun.
14.8 Woi ken wutannoósuonk Israel, 8wadchanuwaénumoh wuttamehpunadt: tohwutch ya[n]éewéan penuwohteaut ut ohkeit, kah onatuh pomushaénin, noh quánupit nóquttukqunóhteat?
14.9 Tohwutch woh yanéeuwéan noh chepshont, onatuh menuhkesuen noh matta woh pohquohham8k? qut onch woi ken Jehovah nunnashómunonat kutap, kah nutuss8wénitteamun k8wesuonk, ahque nukóhsinan.
14.10 Yeu wuttinnon Jehovah, yeúh missinninnúh, yeuh wuttinne womantamuneau nanwiyin, matta quihtittam8og wusseet8oàsh, newaj Jehovah matta tapeneáwonk, yeuyeu mehquontam nag ummatcheseongan8oaṣh, kah natawóhtou ummatcheseonganooaṣh.
14.11 Neit Jehovah nuttinuk, peantamwanshúhkon yeug missinninnuog, wutche 8niyeuongan8.
14.12 Mat meetséhetteg matta nunn8tam8 ummauongan8, kah maghettit chikohtae mag8ongash kah mag8onk, matta nuttapeneauóog: qut nag nuppaguanóog nashpe togkodteg, kah nashpe mashagquod, kah nashpe pagwanúonk.
14.13 Neit nussip, woi Lord Jehovah, kusseh, quoshodtumwaenuog wuttinóuh, matta pish kenaum8m8 togkodteg, kah matta pish kummishagqunneów8, qut kuttinnumauunumw8 wunnamuhkutée wunohteáonk, yeu ut ayeuonganit.
14.14 Neit J[e]hovah nuttinuk, quoshodtumwaenuog pann8wae quoshodtumwog ut n8wesuonganit, matta nag nutann8nóog, kah matta nutann8konóog, kah matta nukken8noog; nag nukquoshae missohhamun8óog pann8wae monomansuonk kah mosinunkquodt, kah monteagwuninn8g, kah wuttahh8wae as8kekodteam8ongan8.
14.15 Newutche yeu wussin Jehovah papaume quoshodtumwaenúog neg quoshodtukeg ut n8wesuonganit, kah matta nutann8nóog, onch nag n8waog, togkodteg kah mahshagquodt matta pish yeu o[h]tano ohkeit, nashpe togkodteg kah mahshagquodt yeug quoshodtumwaenuog piṣh paguan8og.
14.16 Kah missinninnúog neh kohk8tomauwáhetticheh, nag piṣh sohw[e]ôkonunk ut Jerusaleme toumaogquehtu newutche mahshagquodt, kah togkodteg, kah matt piṣh howan uppósekinuh, asuh um̃ittamwuss8oh, asuh wunnaumonáuh, asuh wuttaun8oh, newutche nussókanónukk[ó]ntam ummatcheseongan8oaṣh.
14.17 Newutche yeu kutt8onk piṣh kuttinnóneau, nuskesukquaṣh nuhkonáe kah kesukodtae pomitchuaj nussippegwash, kah matta tahshéyeuitch: newutche peenompáe wuttaun8oh nummissinninnúmog, pokshanáog nashpe mishe pokshaonk, kah nashpe ahche unkqunneunkquodte togkodtuonk.
14.18 Sohhaman en ohteuhkonit, neit kusseh, náhshitcheg nashpe togkodteg; petutteaon otan, neit kusseh, neg mahchinacheg nashpe mahshagquodt: nux naneeswe quoshodtumwaen, kah sephausuwaen quinnuppuhkomwog ohkeit ne matta wahteauhetteg.
14.19 Sun ken papaquanne kuppogken Judah? sun kukketeahogkou uhquontam Zion? tohwutch togkomeog, kah matta n8neetskehuwaenúm8mun? natauwompadtamumun wunohteaonk, kah matta wunnegeninno, kah neetskehettue ahquompi, kah kusseh wuttaméhpunáonk.
14.20 Nussamp8womun, woi Jehovah, nummatcheseonganun, kah ummatcheseongan8 n8shunónog, newutche kummatchenéhenumun.
14.21 Ahque unkquanuminnean wutche k8wesuonk mishanontogkon kussohsumoe appuonk, mehquontaṣh: ahque pohquenumaiinnean k8n8waonganun.
14.22 Sun howae kenugke tahwunn8cheyeum8 Gentilsog, noh woh sokanonukôsit? asuh sun woh kesukquash sokanónitteam8ash? sunnummatta ken, noh woi Lord num-manitt8mun? ne waj pahtussuónunog, newutche wame yeush ken kesteauunash.
15.1 NEit Lord nuttinuk, tohkônogque Moses kah Samuel wunneepauun anaquabeh, onch nuttah matta ómun8 nogque en yeug missinninnuog: nag sohwhôteash wutch anaquabeh, kah sohhamwéhettich.
15.2 Kah piṣh n$nih, nag unnukquean, uttoh nuttin sohhamunán? neit piṣh nag kuttinóog, yeu wussin Lord, neg wadchiitcheg nushittuonganit, en nuppunát: kah neg wadchiitcheg togkodteganit, en togkodteganit, kah neg wadchiitcheg mahshagquodtut en mahshagqu[ó]dtut, kah neg wadchiitcheg missinnáiinneat, en missinnáinneat.
15.3 Kah nukkuhquttumauóog yauwechippaiyeuash, wussin Lord, togkodteg nushittinneat kah anumwog nehnekikôsineàt, kah kesukque puppinashasog, kah ohkee puppinashimwog en mahchipwunneat kah pagwohkonat.
15.4 Kah ontappehéoog, en wame ohkée as8tam8onganit, newutche Manasseh wunnaumonuh Hezechiah Judae ketass8t, wutche ne ásip ut Jerusalem.
15.5 Newutche howan woh kódtumonteanumukquean woi Jerusalem? kah howan woh kummauunnitteauwánshik, asuh howan woh páhchadt 8wahteauunat tôh aniyean.
15.6 Kutohquanumeh wussin Lord, kutassóushám: ne$waj summagunum nuhpit ayeuuhkonittue ken, kah kenushish, nussauunum aiuskoianatamunat.
15.7 Nag nuppáuanomóog nashpe pauunóntunk, ut ohkee squontaméhtu: nummukk8kinóog wunneechan8oh, nuppagwan nummissinninnúmog, newutche matta qushkéog wutch ummayeuóut.
15.8 Wussekousquóm8uh nano m8naoh en nuhhogkat onk ne ketahhanne nagunt: nunnuhkinnumauóog, ayeuuhkonittue wutókasin, wuskenuog, pohshuhqu[á]e mukk8kinnuaenúog: nukkenuppe quentamwaheon, kah wabesuonganú88k ut keitotanat.
15.9 Noh nesausuk tahsuoh neechadt mahchimm8, nupp8, wunnuppauzs8moh wayaoh ash kesuk88k: mahche akodchu kah chepshau, kah nag ashqshoncheg nupponoog togkodteganit, anquabhettit ummatwom8oh, wussin Jehovah.
15.10 Missi nutonkapunaonk, woi nokas, newutche keneekitteah penuanittue wosketomp, kah mekonteaenin ut mamusse ohkeit: matt[t]a nunnanamohkouehhuwoh ontsompadtamoonk, asah matta howan ontsompadtam8e nagoh kouhuk8, qut onch nish$noh pasuk nummatanumwe unnukquog.
15.11 Lord n8wop wunnamuhkut pish k8nenanumukqutteauunun matwau matche ahquompak, kah wuttamehpunae ahquompag.
15.12 Sun pish missehchuog poksheau nanumiyeue missehchuog, kah menuhkequog?
15.13 Kuttinneetuonk kah kenompakouunash, matta tahnoadtue nummag ut mukk8kinnuonganit, wutche wame kummatcheseongan8oash, en wame kussissippoiyeumut.
15.14 Kah kuppannupwushahush nashpe kummatwomog en ohkeit ne mo wahteauouan: newutche n8teau nashquneau ut nummusquanittam8onganit, ne pish chogohsukqueog.
15.15 Woi Jehovah k8wahteoh, mehquanumeh, kah natauwaheh, kah ann8tauwa[n]sheh waskhikqueoneg, amanehkon nashpe kussepepahtoonk: wahteaush, wutche ken nutchequnehtam auskontuonk.
15.16 Kukutt8wongash namehteauunash, kah nash nummeech[in]apash, kah kukkutt8onk kah nummoskouantamwahik n8weekontamwutteah[a]hik: newutche nuttissowes k8wesuonk, woi Jehovah um-Manitt8m8uh ayeuhteaog.
15.17 Matta nutappeup ummoeongan8ont momontohsuenuog: kah matta n8weekontam8p: nunnussappip newutche kenutcheg: newutche kenumwohtoh jishontamoonk.
15.18 Tohwutch nagwutteohtag nutonkquomom8onk? kah nunn8chumweteawutteaonk matta neetskehteauouun sekeneam8m8 neetkehteauunat? sun pish pannuppe kutogquanumeh pann8waenuut, ut nunohtae nippeut.
15.19 Newutche yeu n8wau Jehovah, qushkean, neit pish wonk kuppas8ush, kah pish keneepau anaquabeh kah amaunuman mahshoadtitcheg wutch kenugke nishkeneunkqussitcheg, pish kuttatuppeyeu nutt8nut: nag qushkehettich en kuhhogkaiyeu, qut n[á] en qushkehkon.
15.20 Kah kutayeuush pummenutohsue brasse wonkonous en yeug missinninnuog, kah nag pish kutayeuuhkonukquog, qut nag pish matta kussohkunk8og: newutche nen k8weetomsh k8wadchanukqunat, kah kuppohquohwhunukqunat, wussin Jehovah.
15.21 Kah kuppohquohwhunush wutch wunnutcheganit matcheetou, kah kummanouwhush wutch wunnutcheganit unkqueneunkqussit.
16.1 WOnk wuttinn8waonk Jehovah nuppeyaonuk n8wau,
16.2 Matta pish k8mittamwussissu, kah matta pish k8naumoniyeu asuh k8tauniyeu, yeu ut ayeuonganit.
16.3 Newutche yeu wussin Jehovah, papaume wunnaumoniinneunk, kah papaume wuttauneunk neg nekitcheg yeu ut ayeuonganit kah papaume okas8oh neh neekhukqhetticheh, kah papaume wut8shineunk waneechânukkônukquehetticheh yeu ut ohkeit.
16.4 Nag pish onkquommom8e nupwog, nag matta pish mauemóog, asuh matta pish posekinóog: qut nag pish tatuppeyeu8og anóhke ut woskeche ohkeit, kah nag pish mahchim8og nashpe togkodteg, kah nashpe mahshagquodt, kah wuhhogkauh ummeetsuongan8 kesukque puppinshaog, kah ohkée puppinashimwog.
16.5 Newutche yeu wussin Jehovah, petutteúhkon mauongane wetu[ô]mut, kah ahque aush ut maumuttamunat asuh mohkon: newutche nutamaunum n8nohteaonk wutch yeug missinninnuog, wussin Jehovah, womoausuonk kah monaneteaongash.
16.6 Naneeswe matikkenukeg kah papeissiṣsitcheg pish nupwog yeu ut ohkeit: matta pish posekinóog, kah wosketompaog matta pish ummauemouh, kah matta pish neekswóunáuh wuhhogkuh, asuh mukukkontupauóog.
16.7 Asuh matta pish wosketompaog nehneekinauoog maumuttamunat, taphe[ò]nat wuhhogkauh: asuh pish mat wosketompaog 8tattamwaheouh taphettue wuttattamwaitche wutche wut8shin, kah wutohkasin.
16.8 Wonk matta pish kuppetutteoh mishadtupp8e-kommukqut, nag weetappemónat, meetsinat asuh wuttattamunat.
16.9 Newutche yeu wussin Jehovah ayeuteaunit um-Manitt8moh Israel, kusseh, n8wohkukquoshitteóh, yeu wutch ayeuonganit ut anaquabeóg kah pomantamóg, pôáe wodtauatonkquossuonk, weekontamwe wadtauatonkqussuonk, 8wadtauatonkqussuonk wessentamwaénin, kah 8wadtauatonkqussuonk weetauwadteaénin.
16.10 Kah piṣh nnih wahteauwaheadt yeug missinninnuog wame yeush kutt8wongash, kah nag unnukquean, tohwaj Jehovah kutt8hkontog wame yeu mohsag machuk ayeuuhkone nenawun? kah teagwas nummatcheseonganun, asuh teagwas nummatcheseonganun, asuh teagwas nuppanneseonganun, ne ayeuhkonittue unnéhheungkut Jehovah num-Manitt8mun?
16.11 Neit nag piṣh kuttinnóog, newutche k8sh8oog nutohquanumuk, wussin Jehovah, kah asuhkauaog onkatogeh manitt8h, kah wuttinneumuhkauóuh, kah wowussumouh, kah nutohquanumukquog, kah matta nanawehheauóog nuttinnaumatuonk.
16.12 Kah nag anue matcheseúmaog k8sh8uh (newutche kusseh kutasuhkomumw8 nishnoh pasuk ummatchitteaháe unnántam8onk, onk woh nag mat nukkuhkeitonk8og)
16.13 Newaj sohwòhkónunóg yeu wutch ohkeit, en ohkeit ne mo wahteau8óg, asuh k8sh8óog: kah na piṣh kuttit wowussumóneau penowe manitt8og kesukodae kah nukkonae, kah na kuttit matta kitteamonteanumunn[n]eau.
16.14 Newutche kusseh, kesukodtash peyaum8ash wussin Lord, matta piṣh wonk unn8wáun, Lord pomantam noh sohh8wunomp wunnaumonuh Israel wutch Egypt.
16.15 Qut Lord pomantam noh sohh8wunomp wunnaumonuh Israel wutch nanumohkeit, kah wame ohketu uttoh an8hkauomp: kah piṣh wonk nuppas8óog wutohtuóut ne anumauogkup 8sh8oh.
16.16 Kusseh, nutann8n monacheg n8tamágwaénúog, wussin Jehovah, kah nag piṣh nah wunn8tamagquonóuh, kah nahohtoeu piṣh nutann8n monacheg adchaenúog, kah nag piṣh wutadchanóuh wutch nishnoh wadchu, kah wutch nishnoh wadchuém: kah wutch hassunónogqut.
16.17 Newutche nuskesukquash ohtaash wame ummayeuóut: niṣh matta adtahtâunóash wutch kuskesukqut: kah umm[at]ch[e]seongan8 matta adtahtôsin8 wutch nuskesukqut.
16.18 Kah negonne nutonkquadtantam ummatcheseonganoash, kah uppanneseongash papsku, newutche nishketeóog nutohke: n[à]g numwohtoog nutohtóonk nashpe nupp8e muhhogkunk jishanumukquokish kah unkqueneunkquokish.
16.19 Woi Jehovah nummenuhkesuonk kah n8wonkônous, kah nutushpho[u]áonk wuttaméhpunae kesukodtut, Gentilsog piṣh kuppeyaonuk wutch weehqshik ohke, kah piṣh n8waog, wunnamuhkut n8shunónog nompappéhtamwog pann8waongash, tahn8cheyeu8k, kah niṣh matta wadchiyeumukish.
16.20 Sun woh wosketomp ummanitt8muhkauau wuhhogkuh, kah nag matta manitto8og?
16.21 Newutche kusseh, pasukqut piṣh n8wahteauwaheoog: n8wahteauwahéoog nunnutcheg, nummenuhkesuonk, kah piṣh wahteauog nuttissowis Jehovah.
17.1 UMmatcheseonk Judah wussukwhósu nashpe moóshogque pen: kah nashpe wuhk8nuk diamond: ne kogóhksimun ut wuttahh8wae tableut, kah ut kutaltarume askonit.
17.2 Wunneechan8uh mehquantamunit wutaltarumooash kah ukkuppiyeum8oash kishke ashkunkquamut ut wadchuut.
17.3 Woi n8wadcheum ut ohteuhkonit, nummag wáme kittinneetuonk kah wame kenompakouunash mukk8kenittinneat, kah kukqunuhqui ayeuongash wutch matcheseonk pannuppe wame kussussippôiyeumut.
17.4 Kah ken pish matta kutappu ut kutohtoonganit ne anumauunomp, kah k8tinninneumuhkausuáhush ut kummatwomut, en ohkeit ne mo wahteáuoan: newutche kenashqunanum n8teau ut nummusquanittam8onganit, ne pish micheme chikohtag.
17.5 Yeu wussin Jehovah, matanumunach noh pabahtanumont wosketompuh, kah wahpittenteadt weyaus, kah noh wuttah amaehtauont Jehovah.
17.6 Newutche pish tatuppeyeu8 kunkohteadtag touohkomukqut, kah matta pish naum8 peyom88k wanegik, qut noh pish wutohtuontam kunkohteadtaeu ayeuongash ut touohkomukqut, ut salte ohkeit, kah matta wutohkein.
17.7 Wunnanumau wosketomp noh pabuhtanttanumont Jehovah, kah noh annaonont Jehovah.
17.8 Newutche noh pish tatuppeyeu8 mehtug ohketeamuk ut kishke nippeit, kah noh sepagodchabukkaem8uk ut kishke sepuut kah matta pish naum8, kussittau peyom8uk, qut 8neepog pish ashkoshqui, kah matta pish wuttamhik8 kunkohteadtae kodtum8, kah matta pish wohkukquoshininn8 tanneganit meechum.
17.9 Metah anue as8kekodteam8wontam onk wame teanteaguasinish kah unkqueneunkummatcheetou, howan woh 8wahteauun.
17.10 Nen Jehovah natinneuhkontam metah, nukqutcheh mutt8unussog, aninnumauonat nish$noh wosketomp neaunak ummayash, kah neaunak wutusseongane meechummuonk.
17.11 Onatuh pahpahkis ahtenásuk kah matta pwohkhôyeog: netatuppe noh weenauwekit qut matta sampwe, pish wunnukkodtumunash ut nashauwe ukkesukodtumut, kah ut 8wohkukquóiyeumut pish mattammagweyeu8.
17.12 Sohsumoe qunùhqueu appuonk wutch waj kutchissik ne nus-Sanctuarie ayeuonk.
17.13 Woi Jehovah, wutannoósuonguh Israel, wame neg ohquanumukqueáneg pish akodchuog, kah nag pahchaôsitcheg pish wusukwhosuog ut ohkeit, newutche nag nukkonáog Jehovah, noh tohkekommue pomantamwae nippe.
17.14 Neetskeheh woi Jehovah, kah pish nunneetskes: wadchaneh kah pish n8wadchanit: newutche ken waeenomog.
17.15 Kusseh, nag nuttugquog, uttiyeu wuttinn8waonk Lord? yeuyeu peyóm8utch.
17.16 Qut nen, matta nukken8natu Pastoreuuneat kutasukauununat, kah matta nukkodtantam8 unkqunneunkquodte kesukod, k8wahteóh: ne sohham8m8uk wutch nussisset8nut, ne sampwiyeup ut anaquabean.
17.17 OOwabesuonganehkon en kuhhogkat, ken nutannoósuonk ut matche kesukodtut.
17.18 Nag chepshahettich neg kodwoskehúkqueaneg, qut nen ahque chepshónti: nag quequénauánumwéhettich, qut nen ahque queuénauánumwuttei: núhkinumau matchik kesuk, kah nag pagwas nashpe papsku pagwanuonk,
17.19 Jehovah yeu nuttugqun, monchish kah neepaush 8squontam8out wunneechan8oh missinninnuog, uttoh adt Judae ketass8tamwog petutteahettit, kah ne waj sohhamwehettit, kah ut wame Jerusaleme squontamehtu.
17.20 Kah nag us, n8tam8k wuttinn8waonk Jehovah, kenaau Judae ketass8tamwog, kah wame Judah, kah wame wadohkitcheg Jerusalem, neg petutteacheg yeu ut squontaméhtu.
17.21 Yeu wussin Lord, nunnukqussek kuhhogkaóog, kah weasséhteogk sabboth$dayeu: asuh petukkodta8hteok ut Jerusalemeh squontamut.
17.22 Asuh sohh8wuttóhteók weanun wutch kekuóut sabboth$dayeu. Asuh toh usséhteok, qut wunneetupanátamwáhteó8k sabboth$day neánann8nogkup k8shuóog.
17.23 Qut nag matta wunosweetam8uneau, ásuh mat ahchusittamoog, qut nag chetauwussittippukoñaeog, onk woh mo n8tam8og asuh matta attumunum8og kuhk8tomoadtuonk.
17.24 Kah pish n$nih, menuhke kuhkeitieog wussin Jehovah, matta petukkodtau8unat weanun yeu ut kutotanae squontamut Sabbothdayeu, qut wunneetupanatamwahteo8k Sabboth$day, mat na$ut anakauseuinat.
17.25 Neit pish kehtass8tamwog, kah sontimoog petutteaog ut yeu otanae squontamtu appinneat wutappuonganit David, nayeumukquehettit chariotsash kah horsesog, nag wussontimom8uk Judae wosketompaog kah wadohkitcheg Jerusalem, kah yeu kutotan pish michemohteau.
17.26 Kah nag pish 8mwog Judae keiotanehtu, kah wutch ayeuonganehtu ut kishke Jerusalem, kah wutch Benjamine ohkeit, kah wutch mukoshquttaut, kah wutch wadchuuhkontu, kah wutch sowaniyeu, paudtauehettit chikohtae mag8ongash, kah sephausuongash, kah meetsue sephausuongash, kah incense kah padtauwehettit woweenodtumwe sephausuongash en wekit Jehovah.
17.27 Qut matta kukkéhtieog, wunn[é]etupanatamwahtinneat Sabbath$day, kah matta nayeutam8unat weanun, petutteahettit ut Jerusalemme squontamut Sabbathdayeu: neit pish nunnashqussum n8teau na$ut squontamash, kah pish mahchikkossum8m8 Jerusalemme mishikkomukquash, kah matta pish onthamm8un.
18.1 WUttinn8waonk ne pauhonukqut Jeremiah wutch Lordut, n8wau.
18.2 Neepaush kah w8msish en ohkuhkitteaen weékit kah na nuttit n8tamwahuwon nukkutt8wongash.
18.3 Neit n8womsip en ohkuhketeaen wekit, kah kusseh, wuttittannehteauun wheelut.
18.4 Kah wisq ne kezteunk wutch man8nskut, ne matchehteausu ut wunnutcheganit ohkuhqutteaenin: neit wonk ayim penowe wisq: uttoh an 8nontug ohukuhqutteaenin.
18.5 Neit wuttinn8wao[u]k Jehovah nuppeyaonuk, n8wau.
18.6 Woi Israelle week, sun woh mat kuttinhenn8mw8 neane yeuoh ohkuhketeanin wussin Lord, kusseh, neane man8nsk appit ut wunnutcheganit ohkuhketeaenin, ne kuttatuppe appinneau nunnutcheganit, woi Israelle wek.
18.7 Na utt8che unn8waon papaume wutohtimoin, kah papaume tahs8tamoonk, pohqunumunat, kah n8kenumunat, kah paguatauunat.
18.8 Tohneit ne wutohtimoin, ne ayeuuhkonittue kón8tam, quinnuppehettit wutch ummatchet8m8out, pish nutaiuskoiantam ne machuk ayeuuhkonittue ananumog.
18.9 Kah uttoh adt8cheyeu8g ne an8wi papaume wutohtimoin, kah papaume tahs8tamoonk, ayimunat, kah ohteuhkonat.
18.10 Matchesehettit ut anaquabeh, matta n8swehtam8hetteg n8wadtauatonkqussuonk, neit pish nutaiuskoiantam ne wanegik ne anogkup k8niyeuhhennumw8.
18.11 Newutche yeuyeu ehhoh, ken8s Judae wosketompaog, kah wadohkitcheg Jerusalem n8wash, yeu wussin Jehovah kusseh, kutayeuuhkonittue ayimauunumw8 machuk, kah kutayeuuhkonittue natwontamauonumw8 natwontamoonk: qushkek yeuyeu nish$noh pasuk wutch ummatche mayit, kah wunnehteo8k kummayeuoash.
18.12 Kah nag n8waog, matta annoósuonganun8: qut nutásukomumun nehenwonche natwontam8onganunonash, kah nish$noh pasuk nenawun nutussemun ummatche metahh8wae unnantam8onk.
18.13 Newutche yeu wussin Lord, nat8tamok yeuyeu kenugke penuwohteaog, howan noh n8tog ne ônagish Israelle penomp ussen ne onkquanumukquok.
18.14 Sun woh wosketomp nukkonau Lebanone k8noh, ne wóm8uk ohteahkone qussukquanit? asuh kussitchuáne sonkuppogash ne wam8uk pen8e ayeuonganit sun woh nukkodtumunash?
18.15 Newutche nummissinninúmog n8wanánumuk, nag chikohsumwog weetemungquok en tahn8cheyeu8uk, kah nah wuttogkussittahssumóuh ut ummayeuóut, wutch nukkóne mayut, pomushónat mayit nish mo wunnegenunogish.
18.16 Touwishinnuwóhtineat wutohkeyeu, kah michemohtae nuttohhentupantam8onk: nish$noh pasuk noh na paumshadt pish chepshau, kah nunnukkuhquoshau.
18.17 Nag nusseahwhóog onatuh nashpe wutchepwash ut anaquabit matwau: nunnahtinoog muppusk, qut matta muskesuk, wutonkapunáe kesukodtum8óut.
18.18 Neit nag n8waog, peyunk, ayeuuhkonittue natwontamauóntuh natwontam8ongash Jeremiah; newutche naumatuonk matta pish wannehheau wutch sephausuenuut, asuh kogáhquttuonk, wutch waantamwenuut, kah wuttinn8waonk wutch quoshodtumwaenuut: peyunk, togkommontuh meena[n], kah ahque tohhentupontammuttuh teagwe ukkutt8wonk.
18.19 Kuhkeihtah woi Jehovah, kah n8tash 8wadtauato[u]kqussuongan8 neg mekonukqueaneg.
18.20 Sun woh machuk onkquttantamun wanegik? newutche nag pasáhthamwog wutch nukketeahogkou: mehquontash nunneepop ut anaquabe[a]n, nag wunnee n8wanshánaoont, kah quinnuppenumunat kummusquantam8onk nag wutch.
18.21 Newutche p8nin wunneechan8oh ne mohshagquodtut, kah sohkenash 8sqheongan8 nashpe chekeushae togkodteg, kah ummittumwuss8oh amaunumauunach wunneechan8oh, kah sekousquainitch, kah 8wosketompóm8uh nushinach, kah wuskenúm8uh nushunaj mattompagwe togkodteg.
18.22 Mauonk n8tamunach wutch week8woont, tiadche nuhkinnumauadt m8chequshaoh, newutche nag pahsohthamwog nuttohqunukqunnaoont, kah adtahshaog appehanoh wutche nusseetash.
18.23 Qut woi Jehovah, k8wahteoh wame ukkogahquetuongan8 ayeuuhkonittue nen, nunnushikqunnaoont, ahque ahquontamau ummatcheseongan8, kah jishkhogkon, uppanneseonk wutch anaquabean, qut kepuhkonunaj ut anaquabean, unneh musquantaman.
19.1 YEu wussin Jehovah, monchish neemunush ahkuhqutteaenin wutohkee wisq, kah neemun kutchisog wutch missinninnuut kah kutchisog wutch sephausuenuut.
19.2 Kah en sohhom8k wut8nuhkoiyeumut wunnaumonuh Hinnon, ne ohtag ahhut petutteamuk chepwiyeue squontamut, kah naut wahteauwahuush kutt8wongash, nish pish anonish.
19.3 Kah n8wash, n8tam8k wuttinn8waonk Jehovah woi Judae ketass8tamwog, kah wadohkitcheg Jerusalem, yeu wussin Jehvoah ayeuteaunit um-Manitt8moh Israel kusseh, ne nuppaudtauun yeuut ayeuonganit, ne howan n8tog wuhtauogash pish nupp8m8ash.
19.4 Newutche nag nunnukkonukquog, kah penuwohteatoog yeu ayeuonk kah ne wuttit chikohsumauoneau weetemungquok penowe Manitto, neh matta nagumau asuh 8sh8oh, waheahettegeh, asuh Judae ketass8tamwog, kah wohtoog yeuut ayeuonganit mat woskehuwae wusqueheunk
19.5 Nag wonk ayimauwaog qunuhqui ayeuongash Baal, chikkoswonat wunnaumonaoh nashpe n8tau wutche chikohtae mag8ongash en Baalut, ne matta anunn8team8 asuh ân8wau, asuh matta anantam8.
19.6 Newutche kusseh, kesukodtash peyaum8, n8wau Jehovah, yeu ayeuonk matta pish wonk hettam8un Tophet, asuh wut8nouhkoiyeum wunnaumonuh Hinnon, qut nushehteae 8nouhkoi.
19.7 Kah tahnunn8cheahtauun ukkogahquttuonk Judah kah Jerusalem yeu ut ayeuonganit, kah nuppenushah[h]eoog anaquabenit ummatwom8uh, kah nashpe wunnutchegan8wout neg kodnushehteacheg, kah nupp8e wuhhogkauh nummeechumuhkauona[oh] kesukque puppinshasog, kah ohkee puppinashimwog.
19.8 K[a]h nuttauwushitteauun yeu otan, kah [n]ummeshonantamwahtea[n]un, nish$noh pasuk noh na paumshadt pish chepshau, kah ummeshanontamun, newutche wame unninneaongash naut.
19.9 Kah nummeechuwaheaog 8weyaus8 wunnaumonauh, kah 8weyaus8 wuttaun8oh kah nag pish meechwog nish$noh pasuk 8weyausum8 weetompuh, weenuhkomuk nannakompananuttimuk, uttohad ummatwom8uh, kah neg kodnushoncheg pish wunnanakompananouh.
19.10 Neit pish kuppohquetahham wisq ut anaquabhettit weechogqueaneg.
