19.11 Neit pish nag kuttinoog, yeu wussin Jehovah ayeuuhteaunit, ne nuttinne pohquenumun yeug missinninnuog, kah yeu keitotan, onatuh howan pohkshadtunk ohkuhquehteaen wisq, ne [w]atta woh wonk nompe wunnehteauomuk, kah nag pish upposekinouh, ut Tophet, Nô pajeh mat wuttape posekinausinneaoónt.
19.12 Yeu nuttinteauun yeu ayeuonk wussin Jehovah, kah en nag na wadohkitcheg kah nutogquehteoh wutotaneau Tophetut.
19.13 Kah Jerusálemme wetuomash kah Judae tahs8tamwog wekuoash pish ogque nishketeauunash Tophet: newutche wame wekuoash uttoh ut woskeche chikohsumauwahettit weetemungquok en wame kesukque kenauwameonk & sokanumauwaog wuttattamoe mag8ongash penowe Manitt8ut.
19.14 Neit Jeremiah 8m Tophet, uttoh Jehovah anan8nomp quoshodtamunat, kah neepau ut chippinnutongane wekit Jéhovah kah unnau wame missinninnuh.
19.15 Yeu wussin Jehovah ayeuteaunit, um[-]manitt8moh Israel kusseh, nunnuhkinnumau yeu keitotan kah ut wame wutotanamesash machuk ne ayeuuhkonittue ane kn8tam, newutche menehketeauog wussittippukan8oash, onk woh mo, n8tam8og nuttinn8waongash.
20.1 NEit Pashur wunnaumonuh Immer sephausuen noh kehche nanawunnuaenin wonk ut wekit Jehovah n8tam quoshodtuk Jeremiah yeush.
20.2 Neit Pashur togkomau Jerémiahoh quoshodtumwaenuh, kah upponuh stocksut ne ohtag ut Benjaminne qunuhqui squontamut, ne kishkohtag wekit Jehovah.
20.3 Kah nnih na wonk kesukok Pashur sohh8wunau Jeremiahoh wutch stocksut, neit Jeremiah wuttinuh Lord matta kuttehenuk8h Pashur qut Magoz$missabib.
20.4 Newutche yeu wussin Lord, kusseh, kutayimaush chepshaonk en kuhhogkat, kah en wame ketompaut, kah nag pish penushadtamwog nashpe wuttogkodtegan8 ummatwom8uh, kah kuskesukquash pish wunnaumun, kah nummag wame Judah en wunnutcheganit Babilone ketass8t, kah noh pish kummissinohkone monchanuk en Babilon, & noh pish wunnushoh nashpe togkodteg.
20.5 Nano, nummag wame ummenuhkesuonk yeu keitotan, kah wame wutanakausuonganooash kah wame ummishoade maumachiyeumash, kah wame wunnompak8un8oash Judae ketass8tamwog, nummagunash wunnutchegan8wout ummatwom8uh, neg pish mak8kinoncheg, kah pish neemunoog, kah uss8unoog Babilon.
20.6 Kah k[é]n Pashur, kah wame neg apitcheg kékit, pish missinno8og, kah ken pish kuppeam Babilon, kah na pish kuttit nuppun kah na pish kuttit posekinnitteam, ken kah wame ketompaog, neg pann8wae quoshodtumauadtcheg.
20.7 Woi Jehovah, kuppuhch8uneh, kah nuppuhch8unit, ken kutanue menuhkusumeh, kah kussohkos: asekésukokish nutahanehtont, nish$noh pasuk nutoontohkonuk.
20.8 Newutchen nádteuh kôdt8an, nummishont8wop, nummishont8wop, chekeeu usseonk kah mukk8kinnuwaonk newutche wuttinn8waonk Jehovah nutushpunanittean, kah asekesukokish nutahanehtont.
20.9 Neit nussip, matta wonk nummissohwhôh, asuh wonk nussu ut 8wésuonganit: qut wuttinn8waonk ut nuttahhut, tatuppeyeu8 nashqunáe n8taut, kuppuhhôsu ut nuskon$ut, kah nussauunumup kehchithon, kah matta nukkehchittohhou.
20.10 Newutche n8tamup nukkehkomukqunat monaog, wabesuonk waeenu, unnehtunkquodt, n8waog, kah nuttinnehtonkqunn8hteamun: wame neetompaog askuhhamwog nukk8qunukshaonk, n8waog, pagwodche woh ôsumau, kah woh kussohkauóun, kah woh kutann8tauóun.
20.11 Qut Jehovah n8weetomuk, onatuh mohsheunkqueneunkqussit: newaj piṣh waskhukqueoneg togkussittassunéhettit, kah nag piṣh matta sohkohseog, nag piṣh mishe akodchuog, newutche nag matta piṣh wunniyéog, nag ummicheme chepshaongan8 matta piṣh wunántam8un.
20.12 Qut, woi Jehovah ayeuteaunit, ken quajheadt sampweusseaénin kah kenaau mutt8unussog kah metah, naumutti kutann8tôsuonk nag ut: newutche en kuh[k]ogkat n8wohshinum nuppissau$matuonk.
20.13 Ket8humok Jehovah, waeenomók Jehovah, newutche pohquohwhunau ukketeahogkôunoh matcheku, wutch wunnutcheganit matcheseaen.
20.14 Matanumwe uttamunach ne kesukod adt neekeomp: ahque wunanittamunach ne kesukok n8hkas neechanukquéan
20.15 Mat[á]numwe ununach noh wosketomp, noh paudtaunchem8óno[n]t n8shoh, n8wadt, mukkutchouks keneekitteont, ahche wekontamwahikqun.
20.16 Kah noh wosketomp tatuppeyeu8itch keitotanaṣh nish Jehovah kepuhteajiṣh, kah matta aiuskoianatam8: kah n8taj mauonk nompoáeu, kah mishont8waonk puhshequadt.
20.17 Newutche matta nunnushhuk8 wutch ôontomukqut, asuh woh nokas n8weenohkeinneat, kah wutôontomuk woh nagwutteae n8wompikquoeuwónukqunat.
20.18 Tohwutch sohhamos wutch ôontomukqut, naumunat anakausuonk kah unkquanumóonk, onk woh nukkesukodtum akodchue pámsheau?
21.1 WUttinn8waonk ne pauhónukqut Jeremiah wutch Jehovahut, Zedekiah ketass8t ann8nont Pashur wunnaumonuh Melchiah, kah Zephaniah wunnaumonuh Maaseiah sephausuen, n8waog,
21.2 K8wehquetumoush nat8tamwontamaiinneam Jehovah (newutche Nebuchadnezzar Babylone ketass8t nummatompagúhkonukquog) tohneit Jehovah unnehikquéog neaunak wame ummonchanatamwe anakausuongaṣh, onk woh nutamaehtunkqun
21.3 Neit Jeremiah nah wuttinuh, yeu piṣh kuttinnoneau Zedekiah.
21.4 Yeu wussin Jehovah um-Manitt8moh Israel, Nukqushkinum kenauwameongaṣh ohtágiṣh ut kenutchegan8wóut, niṣh nashpe ayeuuhkónog Babylone ketass8t, kah Caldeansog, neg wéenuhkongqueógig ut poquadchit pummeneutunkanit, kah nummukkinóog ut noeu yeu keitotanat.
21.5 Kah nen wonk kutayeuúhkonumw8, nashpe summagunnumwe menutcheg, kah nashpe menuhki muhpit, musquantamwe kah chenauausue, kah mishe musquantamwe.
21.6 Kah nuttogkom neg apitcheg yeu keitotanat, naneswe wosketomp & pupinashim: nag piṣh nupwog nashpe mishe anninneaonk
21.7 Kah ompetag wussin Jehovah nummag Zedechiah Judae ketass8t, kah wuttinneumoh, kah missinninnuog, kah neg sekqshoncheg yeu otanat wutch enninneaonganit, wutch togkodteganit, kah wutch mashagquodtut, ut wunnutcheganit Nebuchadnezzar Babylone ketass8t, kah ut wunnutchegan8óut ummatwom8uh, kah ut wunnutchegan8óut neg kodnushoncheg, kah nah piṣh wuttogkomuh en kenag togkodteg matta piṣh owóhquánumuh, asuh ukkitteamonteanumoh, asuh monánumoh.
21.8 Kah piṣh kuttin yeug missinninnúog, yeu wussin Jehovah, kusseh, nupponam anaquabeog, pomantamóe may, kah nupp8e may.
21.9 Noh apit yue keitotanat, piṣh nashpe nupp8 togkodteganit, kah nashpe mahshagquodt, kah nashpe enninneaonk: qut noh sohhog kah agẃehtauont Caldeansoh, neg wéenuhkongqueógig, noh piṣh pomantam, kah uppomantamoonk pish ne tohqunuk.
21.10 Newutche ayeuuhkonittue ponam nuskesuk yeu otan wutche machuk, kah matta wutch wanegik, wussin Jehovah; kah piṣh aninnumauon en wunnutcheganit Babylone ketass8t, kah noh piṣh wutchikohsumun ut n8taut.
21.11 Kah papaume wek Judae ketass8t, n8wash, n8tam8k wuttinn8waonk.
21.12 Woi David wek, yeu wussin Lord, ussek wussittumóonk nompoáeu, kah pohquohwuttók noh mogk8kinit wutch wunnutcheganit noh magk8kinuadt, ishkont nummusquantam8onk ogque sohham8m8 n8taut, kah chikohteau, ne$waj howan woh mo ontham8k: newutche kummatche usseongan8oaṣh.
21.13 Kusseh, kutayeuuhkonṣh woi wadohkean 8nouhkôiyeuut, kah mukoshquttae qussukquanit, wussin Lrod, neg 8n8wacheg, howan woh ayeuuhkonukquean? asuh howan woh petutteadt nutáyeuonganunónut?
21.14 Qut kussasamatahwhunumw8, neánummeechumik kutusseongan8aṣh, wussin Jehovah: kah nunnashqunanum n8teau, ut wuttouohkomukkouóut, kah piṣh mahchekussum8m8 wame teanteáqussiniṣh, ut waéenu.
22.1 YEu wussin Jehovah, womsish en Judae ketass8t wekit, kah naut n8wash yeu kutt8wonk,
22.2 Kah n8wash, N8tash wuttinn8waonk Jehovah, woi Judae ketass8t, ken ápean wutappuonganit David, ken kah kuttinneumog, kah kummissinninnúmog neg petutteacheg yeuh squontamehtu.
22.3 Yeu wussin Jehovah, ussek wussittumóonk, kah sampweusseonk, kah pohquohwhus noh mak8kinit wutch wunnutcheganit magk8kinnúadt, kah matchenehuwáhte[ò]gk, chekéenéheúhteógk pen8wot, touwiés, asuh sekousq, asuh soksquohthádteok mat woskehuwae musqueheonk yeu ut ayeuonganit.
22.4 Newutche yeu wunnamu[h]kut usseóg, neit piṣh petukkon[e]au yeu ut squontamut, ketass8tamwog, appinneat wutappuonganit David, nayeumukqunat chariotsaṣh, kah horsesog, nagum kah wuttinneumoh, kah ummissinninnumoh.
22.5 Qut mata yeuṣh n8tam8og kut8wongaṣh, nutchadchekeyeuwam nashpe nen, wussin Jehovah, yeu weetu piṣh touushitteauun.
22.6 Newutche yeu Lord wuttittamun Judae ketass8t weekit, ken Gilead, ut nuhhogkat, kah uppuhkuk Lebanon, qut wunnamuhkut kuttouohkomukqúhkonuṣh, kah keitotanaṣh niṣh matta wadohteumukiṣh.
22.7 Kah kutayeuuhkonittue qu[a]gwoshwéhtamouṣh pagwohteaenuog, nisnoh pasuk ahtou wutauwohteaonk, kah nag piṣh tummehtahwhôog k8ne Cedarsum8uh, kah wuttinnuhkonáuh n8taut.
22.8 Kah monataṣh wutohtimoneaṣh piṣh paumuhkomwog yeu keitotan, kah nag piṣh unnaog nishnoh pasuk weetatteamungoh, tohwaj Jehovah yeu unnehteunk yeu missi keitotan?
22.9 Kah nag piṣh namp8hamwog, newutche nukkodtumwog 8n8waonk Jehovah um-Manitt8m8uh, & wowussumáog onkatogeh manitt8oh, kah wuttinneumuhkauóuh.
22.10 Mauemúhteogk napukeg, asuh maumuttamóunúhteógk; qut mishe mauunnitteaunsheuk noh moncheit, newutche matta piṣh wonk qushkeu, asuh naum8 ne adt neekit ohke
22.11 Newutche yeu wussin Lord papaume Shallum wunnaumonuh Josiah Judae ketass8t, noh nompe nanawunnuómont Josiahoh 8shoh, noh sohhog yeu wutch ayeuonganit, matta na piṣh wonk en qushku.
22.12 Qut piṣh na wuttit nuppunin uttoh adt missinohteahettit, kah matta piṣh wonk naum8 yeu ohke.
22.13 Missi wutonkapunaonk noh ayig weetu nashpe mat sampweusseonk, kah 8chambersaṣh nashpe wo[ô]nkagk, noh attumunuk weetatteamunguh wutanakausuonk, kah matta onkquatauonk, kah matta wutôadtúhkauoh wutanakausuonk.
22.14 Noh an8wadt nutayim mishe kehchikkomuk, kah mogke kishke chambersaṣh, kah wunnussum kenogkenegash, kah appuhquau chikkupoh, kah musquadtsôsu.
22.15 Sun woh kenanawunnuam newutche kutabpuhquomp chikkuppog? sunnummatta k8sh meetseis kah wuttattam8us, kah usseis wussittumóonk, kah sampweusseonk, neit 8niyeuwontamun?
22.16 Wussittum uppissaumatonk matcheku, kah quenauhikquit, neit 8niyeuhikqun; sunnummatta yeu n8wahetteaonk wussin Jehovah.
22.17 Qut kuskesukquaṣh kah kuttah webe wutch hahchewontamóonk, kah soksquadthamunat mat woskehuwae musqueheonk, kah sunukqutchahwhuttuonk, kah chekée ussenat.
22.18 Newutche yeu wussin Jehovah papaume Jehojakim wunnaumonuh Josiah Judae ketass8t, matta piṣh ummauemóuh, woi neemat, woi neetompas: matta piṣh ummauém8uh n8wahettit, woi lord, woi wussohsumóonk.
22.19 Piṣh posekinau ne posekinit asse, pamontonchimáhettit, kah sohwohteahettit en áongkoue Jerusaleme squontamehtu.
22.20 Kuhkuhquiṣh Lebanon, maush, kah mishont8aṣh ut Bashan, kah maush ut ôsukonganit; newutche wame womonadtcheg paguanóog.
22.21 Kukkinnonup wanniyéan, qut kussip, matta nunn8tam, yeu kuttinniyeuonk wutch k8skenuunneat, matta ken8swetam8unat n8wadtau[a]tonkqussuonk.
22.22 Waban piṣh mahchipp8 wame Pastorsoh, kah womonacheg piṣh missinoóog, wunnamuhkut piṣh neit kutakoj, kah piṣh kutchepsham wutch wame kummatcheseongaṣh.
22.23 Woi ken wadohkean Lebanon, wâdsháhteáan ut chikkupuhtukqut, uttoh piṣh kuttin wunneetupanatamwéin onkquommom8ongaṣh yeanâhkukkongquean, wutonkquommom8ongaṣh mittamwossis neechadt.
22.24 Pomantamon wussin Jehovah, Coniah wunnaumonuh Jehojakim Judae ketass8t tôhkonogque nompak8unnú8 ut nuttinohkôunit, onch na k8ch kodtinunun.
22.25 Kah kuttinnumaush ut wunnutchegan8w[ô]ut neg kodnushikqueaneg, kah en wunnutchegan8wout neg wuskesuk8 quohtaman, ut wunnutcheganit Nebuchadnezzar Babilone ketass8t, kah ut wunnutchegan8wout Caldeansog.
22.26 Kah kussohwhokonsh, kah kokas noh nekhikquean, ut onkatogke ohkeit ne mo adt nekean kah na pish kuttit nuppun.
22.27 Qut ohkeit na kodtantamwehettit en qushkenat na matta pish wuttin qushkeineau.
22.28 Sun yeuoh wosketomp Coniah sekeneauou pokshae nunnukontunkoh: sun noh wishquiyeu ne adt mat wekontam8onganun8g? tohwutch nag sohwohteaog, nagum kah 8skannemunneoh, kah pogketamwog en ohkeit ne matta wahteauhétteg[?]
22.29 Woi ohke, ohke, ohke[,] n8tash wuttinn8waonk Jehovah.
22.30 Yeu wussin Lord, wussukhamok yeuoh wosketomp, matta wunnechaneg wosketomp noh matta woh waniegk ut ukkesukkodtumut: newutche matta wosketomp 8m8oh 8skannemunit pish wunniyeoh: appinneat wutappuonganit David, kah nano nanawunnuadt ut Judah.
23.1 MIssi wutonkapunnaongan8 Pastorsog, neg pagwohteacheg kah seahwhoncheg wuttittanadtupp8ongan8 nusshepsumog wussin Jehovah.
23.2 Newutche yeu wussin Lord um-Manitt8m8uh Israel, ayeuuhkonittue Pastorsog neg assamoncheg nummissinninnumoh kusseahwhomw8 nufflockum, kah kutama8hkauoog, kah matta nag kenatauwaheoog, kusseh natauwahettue kupponamauonumw8 kummatche usseongan8oash wussin Jehovah.
23.3 Kah nummukkin sekqshoncheg ut nuf[-]flockumut wutchwame wutohtimoinash uttoh ann8hkauog, kah wonk nuppas8oog, ut wutchippinneutunkan8out, kah nag pish mishimmeechummuog, kah nano monaog.
23.4 Kah nuttahshinnumauoog nanashipsaenuog, neg pish sohkom8unoncheg, kah nag matta pish wonk wabeseog asuh chepshau8og, asuh matta pish waneteau8og pasuk8 wussin Jehovah.
23.5 Kusseh, kesukodtásh peyaum8ash wussin Lord, nutomohkinumau David sampweusseae wuttuhk, kah ketass8t pish nanawunnuau, kah pish wunayeu, kah pish usseu wussittumoonk kah sampweusseonk ut ohkeit.
23.6 Ut ukkesukodtumut Judah pish wadchanau, kah Israel pish wunayeu, kah yeu 8wesuonk ne pish ahen[l]t: JEHOVAH NUSSAMPWE USSEONGANIIN.
23.7 Newutche kusseh, kesukodtash peyaum8ash wussin Jehovah, nag matta pish wonk unn8wo8og, Lord pomantam noh sohh8wunomp Israélloh wutch ohkit Egypt.
23.8 Qut Lord pômantam, noh sohh8wunomp kah sagkompagunomp 8skannem Israelle week, wutch nanumohkeit, kah wutch wame wutohtimoneat uttoh ann8hkauog, kah nag pish ayeu[ô]g nehenwonché wutohkeyeuout.
23.9 Nuttah ut nuttinnomiyeumut pokshau newutche quoshodtumwaenuog, wame nuskonash nunnukshaash: nuttatuppeyeu kogkeussippamwaenuut (kah neaneyeu wosketomp aneukongquit wine) newutche Jehovah, kah wutche 8neetupa[n]atamwe unn8waongash.
23.10 Newutche ohke wunnumwapeneau mamussuénuog, newutche nashpe chadchekeyeuwaonk, ohke mau8m8, wunneayeuongash ut touohkomuk nunohtaash, kah wuttinniyeuongan8 matchit, kah wutchekeusseongan8 matta sampwan8.
23.11 Newutche naneeswe quoshodtumwaen kah sephausuwaen nishkeneungqussuog, nux, ut nekit namehteauun ummatcheseonk wussin Jehovah.
23.12 Newutche pish ummayou tatuppeyeu8 ut wuhhogkaout t8neque mayash ut pohkenahtu: nag pish kutchittoushaog, kah na$ut penushaog: newutche pish nuppaudtauoog machut natauwahae kodtum8m8 wussin Jehovah.
23.13 Kah nunnaum wutass8tuongan8 quoshodtumwaenuog ut Samaria: nag quoshodtamwog ut Baal, kah panneseaheaog Israelloh nummissinninnumoh.
23.14 Kah wonk nunnaum nishkeneunkquok ut Jerusaleme quoshodtumawenuut, mamussuog, pomushaog pann8wonganit, menehketeauog wonk wunnutchegan8oaṣh matchesecheg, onk matta howan woh qushku wutch ummatcheseonganit: nag wame tatuppeyeuog ut nuhhogkat Sodom, kah wadohkitcheg naut tatuppeyeu8og Gomorrah.
23.15 Newutche yeu wussin Jehovah ayeuteaunit papaume quoshodtumwaenuog, kusseh, nussohkom8un[ó]og wormw8d, kah 8tattamwaheóuh weesweeu nippe: newutche wutch Jerusaleme quoshodumwaenúog, eiantukeiyeuonk sohham8m8 en wame wutohtimóineat.
23.16 Yeu wussin Jehovah ayeuteaunit, n8tam8hteók ukkutt8ongan8oaṣh quoshodtumwaenuog, neg missohhamunkqueógig; nag tohken8cheáhik8oog: nag n8waog monomansuonk wutch nehenwonche wuttahh8wóut, kah matta wuch wutt8nut Jehovah.
23.17 Nag ash wuttinóuh neh sekeneunkqueaneh: Jehovah n8wau, piṣh k8nohteamw8, kah unnáog nishnoh pasuk8, noh ásuhkog nehenwonche wuttahh8wae unnantam8onk; wanne machuk piṣh kenuhkuhkongk8mw8.
23.18 Newutche howan neepauwit ukkogúhqutteam8onganit Jehovah, kah wahteunk, kah n8tog wuttinn8waonk? howan kahkinneasit ukkutt8wonk n8tog?
23.19 Kusseh, Jehovah uppemsquohhumoh sohham8m8 ut musquantam8onganit, unkqueneunkque pemsquoh, piṣh unkqueneunkque penushau ut uppuhkukqut matcheetou.
23.20 Ummusquantam8onk Jehovah matta piṣh qushkemun8, nô pajeh kestauunat, kah pakodche ussenat wuttahh8wae unnantam8ongaṣh: ut maumachiṣh kesukodtut, piṣh kuppannuppeyeue natwontamuneau.
23.21 Matta yeug nutann8nóog quoshodtumwaénuog, qut quogqueog: matta nag nukken8náog, qut nag quoshodtumwog.
23.22 Qut neepauwéhettis nukkogáhqutteam8onganit, kah n8tamwáheáhettis nummissinninnúmoh nuttinn8waongaṣh, neit woh nag qushk8panneg wutch ummatchemayyeuóut, kah wutch ummatcheseongan8óut.
23.23 Sun nen paswe Manit wussin Jehovah, kah matta nô|adt Manit?
23.24 Sun woh howan adtahshau wuhhogkuh, ut asampamukquodtut, onk woh mo nunnauoh wussin Jehovah? sunnummatta nunnumwohto8h kesuk kah ohke wussin Jehovah?
23.25 Nunn8tauomp toh quoshodtumwaenuog an8wahetteup, pann8wayeuongash quoshodtumwehettit ut n8wesuonganit, n8wahettit, nuttinnukquom, nuttinnukquom.
23.26 Toh utt8che piṣh yeu ohteau wuttahh8wout quoshodtumwaenuog, neg pann8waongash quoshódtukeg? nux, nag quoshodtumwog wuttahh8wae as8kekodteam8onganooash;
23.27 Nag unnantamwog wanantamwáheonat nummissinninnúmog n8wesuonk, nashpe wuttinnukquomuwonganooash, neg ánoncheg nishno[h] pasuk weetatteamunguh, neane 8sh8uh wananatamohettit n8wesuonk wutche Baal.
23.28 Quoshodtumwaenin noh anukquonk, unn8w[á]j unnukquom8onk, kah noh ohtunk nuttinn8waonk, unn8waj nuttinn8waonk, pabuhtanumwe: teagwas wussadteamunash ut wheatut? wussin Jehovah.
23.29 Sunnummatta nuttinn8waonk tatuppéyeuunn8 n8taut? wussin Jehovah, kah onatuh hammer, ne sogquetahham8m8uk qussuk?
23.30 Newutche kusseh, nen nutáyeuuhkon quoshodtumwaenuog, wussin Jehovah, neg kôm8tukeg nuttinn8w[á]onk niṣh$noh pasuk wutch weetatteamunganit.
23.31 Kusseh, nen nutáyeuuhkon quoshodtumwaenuog, wussin Jehovah, neg m8sitteunkeg weenannu8 kah an8wahettit, noh wussin.
23.32 Kusseh, nag nutáyeuuhkonoog quoshae missohhogig pann8wae unnukquom8ongash wussin Lord, kah wussinneau, kah panne usseáheáog nummissinninnúmog nashpe uppann8waongan8oash, kah nashpe wunnonkan8ongan8, qut matta nutann8noog, asuh nuttinann8nóuneau: newaj piṣh mat wunáyeuheahetteg yeuh missinninnúh wussin Jehovah.
23.33 Kah yeug missinninnúog, asuh quoshodtumwaen, asuh sephausuwaen, nat8tamungquean, n8wahettit, teagwas 8weéanun Lord? neit nag piṣh kuttinòog, teagwe weanun? nen kutohquanumunumw8 wussin Jehovah,
23.34 Kah quoshodtumwaen, kah sephausuwaen, kah missinninnumog neg an8wacheg, 8wéanun Jehovah, nussasamatuh noh wosketomp, kah wek.
23.35 Yeu piṣh kuttinnoneau niṣhnoh pasuk weetatteamungoh, kah nishnoh pasuk wematoh, toh unnunnamp8ham Jehovah, kah toh n8wau Jehovah?
23.36 Kah 8weanun Jehovah matta piṣh wonk kummiṣhamm8uneau: newutche niṣh$noh howan ukkutt8wonk ne piṣh 8weanun, newutche k8woonkitteamw8 ukkutt8wongash pomantamwae God; Jehovah ayeuteaunit num$Manitt8mun.
23.37 Yeu pish kuttinnon quoshodtumwaenin, toh kuttin namp8hamunk Jehovah, kah Jehovah toh n8wau?
23.38 Qut newutche kussimw8, 8weanun Jehovah, newaj yeu n8wadt Jehovah, newutche yeu kussinneau kutt8onk, 8weanun Jehovah, kah nunnegont8wop en kuhhogkaout, nussip, matta pish kussimw8 8weanun Jehovah.
23.39 Newutche kusseh, nen papaquánne k8wananumunumw8, kah kutohquanumunumw8, kah keitotan aninnumauunog, kah k8sh8woog, kah kuppogkenunnumw8 wutch anaquabeh.
23.40 Kah kuppaudtauunumw8 machemoht[a]g spu[n]adtuonk, kah machemohtag akodchuonk matta pish wanatam8muk.
24.1 LOrd nukkuhk8tomunkqunuh, kah kusseh, neesunnútogkodtash figsash ponamunash anaquohtag wut-Templum Jehovah, Nebuchadnezar Babilone ketass8t mahche missinohkonittue monchanont Jeconiah wunnaumonuh Jehojakim Judae ketass8t, kah Judae sontimoog, kah weekitteaenuog kah Smithsog wutch Jerusalem, kah uppas8uh Babilon.
24.2 Pasuk Man8t ohteau wunnegenash figsash, ogqueneunkquodtash figsash nish negonne kesa[n]8tagish: kah onkatog Man8t matchetaṣh figsash, niṣh woh mo meech8mukiṣh newutche mamatchittaṣh.
24.3 Neit Jehovah nuttinuk, teagwas kenaum Jeremiah? kah nussip, figsaṣh: wunnegenash figsash, ahche wunnegenaṣh, kah machukiṣh ahche matchitaṣh, niṣh woh mo meech8mukiṣh newutche mamatchitaṣh.
24.4 Neit wonk wuttinn8waonk Jehovah nuppeyaonuk n8wau,
24.5 Yeu wussin Jehovah um-Manitt8moh Israel, ogqueneunkquotaṣh yeuṣh wanegukiṣh figs[a]ṣh, ne nuttinne waheoneau, neg masinohteamukeg wutch Judah, neg ann8t[è]amwéoneg yeu wutch ayeuonganit en wutohtuóut Caldeansoh wutche wanegik.
24.6 Newutche nag nummonunneauóog wutch wanegik, kah nag wonk nupp8oog yeu ut ohkeit, kah nag n8weekikkonóog, kah matta nunn8kinóog, kah nag nutohteuhkonunk, kah matta nukkodadchabukinóog.
24.7 Kah nag nuttinnumauáog metah n8wahikquna[ó]ut, nen noh Jehovah, kah nag piṣh nummissinninnúmog, kah nag nen um-Manitt8m8uh: newutche nag piṣh quinnuppeog ut nuhhogkat nashpe mamusse wuttahhou.
24.8 Kah onatuh matche figsaṣh, niṣh woh mo meech8mukiṣh newutche mamatchitash (wunnamuhkut yeu wussin Jehovah) ne nuttinne aninnumauón Zedechiah Judae ketass8t, kah wussontimom8uh, kah ashqshoncheg ut Jerusalem, [á]shqshoncheg yeu ut ohkeit, kah neg wadohkitche Egypte ohkeit.
24.9 Kah nag nuttinnumauóog ontahtauunat wame ass8tam8ongaṣh ohkeit, wutche woskeheaongan8, kehkomónat ushpunnamonat momontauonat, kah matchenánumáe unnonat ut wame ayeuonganehtu toh an8hkauog.
24.10 Kah nutann8tam togkodteg, kah mahshagquodt, kah unninneaonk kenugke nagoh, nô pajeh mahchimwunneaóont wutch ohkeit, ne anumauogkup, kah 8sh8oh.
25.1 WUttinn8waonk ne pauhônukqut Jeremiah papaume wame Judae missinninnúog, weyaue kodtum8m Jehojakim wunnaumonuh Josiah Judae ketass8t, ne 8skekodtum8g Nebuchad[r]ezzar Babylone ketass8t.
25.2 Ne Jeremiah quoshodtumwaen kôn8nompuh wame Judae missinninnúh, kah en wame wadohkitcheg Jerusalem, n8wau,
25.3 Wutch nabo wunnishwe kodtum8mut Josiah wunnaumonuh Ammon Judae ketass8t, pajeh yeu kesukok (ne neesneechage nishwe kodtum8) wuttinn8waonk Jehovah nuppeyaonuk, kah kuttinnonunnáop, nompoáe omohkeon kah kodt8hkôon, qut matta kukkeihketam8uneau.
25.4 Kah Jehovah nutann8nuk en wame kuhhogkaôut quoshodtumwaenûh wuttinninnúmoh, nompoáe omohkeon, kah ann8teamwean, qut matta ken8tam8m8, kah matta kenaúohtauogaemw8 n8tamunat.
25.5 Nag n8waog, qushkek wonk yeuyeu nishnoh pasuk wutch ummatche mayut, kah wutche kummatche usseonganit, kah ayekq ut ohkeit ne Jehovah aninnumunkqueog, kah k8sh8out micheme kah micheme.
25.6 Kah asuhkauúhteogk onkatogig manitt8og wuttinneumuhkauónat kah wowussumónat, kah ahque m8m8sqhegk en musquantam8onganit, nashpe kenutchegane anakausuongan8oash, kah matta piṣh k8woskhennomw8.
25.7 Qut matta kukkeiketiomw8 wussin Lord, onk woh kumm8hm8sqhinneaóut musquanitamunat nashpe kenutchegane anakausuonganóoaṣh, en k8woskhitteaongan8.
25.8 Newutche yeu wussin Jehovah ayeuteaunit, newutche matta ken8tam8mw8 nuttinn8waongaṣh.
25.9 Kusseh, nutann8n kah nunneemun wame nannummiyeue teateashiyeuongash, wussin Jehovah, kah Nebuchadrezzar Babylone ketass8t nuttinninneum, k[a]h nag nutayeuuhkonittue pas8oog yeu ohkeit, kah ayeuuhkonittue neg na wadohkitcheg, kah ayeuuhkonittue yeush wutohtim[ó]ineaṣh waeenu, kah nag nuppapaquane pagwanóog, kah nutch[é]pshaheoog, kah nummishannánumweheaog, kah machemohtag touwushin.
25.10 Nano, nag nutamaunumauóog póanittam8e wadatauatonkqussuonk kah weekontamóe wadtauatonkqussuonk, 8wadtauatonkqussuonk, wesseentamwaenin, kah 8wadtauatonkqussuonk weetauadteaenin, wadtauatonkque togguhwhonganompskosh kah 8wequai8m wequananteg.
25.11 Kah yeu mamusse ohke piṣh touwushin, kah chepshaonganú8, kah yeush wutohtimóinneaṣh piṣh wuttinneumuhkauáog Babylone ketass8tamwoh nesausuk tahshinchage kodtumwae.
25.12 Kah piṣh n$nih nesausuk tahshinchag kodtum8aṣh mahtshunk, nussasamatoh Babylone ketass8t, kah ne wutohtim[ó]in, wussin Lord, wutch ummatcheseongan8, kah wutohtu Caldeansog, kah ne nummicheme touwushitteauwáhtauun.
25.13 K[á]h nunnuhkinumau ne ohke wame nukkutt8wongaṣh ne áne ken8tam, wame ne ánsukwhosik yeu b8k, ne Jeremiah ayeuu[k]konittue quoshodtumwohtunk wame wutohtimóneaṣh.
25.14 Newutche monatash wutohtimóneash, kah mogass8tamwog piṣh na 8chiinneauh wonk; kah nag piṣh nuttinunkquottauóog neaunak wutusseongan8aṣh, kah neaunak nehenwonche wunnutchegane anakausuonganooaṣh.
25.15 Newutche yeu nuttugqun Lord um-Manitt8m8uh Israel, neemunush musquanittamwe wine wuttattamwaitch wutch nunnutcheganit, kah wame wutohtimóneash uttoh anann8nun wuttattamwáh.
25.16 Kah nag piṣh wuttattamwog, kah wogkouéog, kah kogkéyeuwaog, newutche togkodteg ne an8tam nag en kenugke.
25.17 Neit neemununup cup wutch Jehovah wunnutcheganit, kah wame wutohtimóneash n8tattamwaheoneáu, n$noh Jehovah ánunn8nukqueh.
25.18 Jerusalem, kah Judae keitotanaṣh, kah ukkeitass8tamóm8oh, kah wussontimóm8oh, n[á]g ayeuónaóut touwussinóonk, chepshaonk, mishanánittuonk, kah matchenanittuonk (neane yeu kesukok.)
25.19 Pharaoh Egypte ketass8t, kah wuttinneumoh, kah wussontimomoh, kah wame ummissinninnúmoh.
25.20 Kah wame kenukshae missinninnuog, kah wame ketass8tamwog ohkeit Uz, kah wame ketass8tamwog ohkeit Philistiansog, kah Ashkelon, kah Azzah, kah Ekron, kah sekqshoncheg ut Ashdod.
25.21 Edom, kah Moab, kah wunnaumonuh Ammon.
25.22 Kah wame Tyre ketass8tamwog, kah wame Zidon[é]e ketass8tamwog, kah munnáhhannu ketass8tamwog ut aongkoue ketahhanit.
25.23 Dedan, kah tema, kah Buz, kah wame neg apitcheg aonkgoue adt nashik.
25.24 Kah wame Arabie ketass8tamwog, kah wame ukketass8tamómoh kenukshae missinninnúog apitcheg touohkomukqut.
25.25 Wame Zimrie ketass8tamwog, kah wame Elame ketass8tamwog, kah wame Medse ketass8tamwog.
25.26 Kah wame nannummiyeue ketass8tamwog, nô apitcheg, kah páswoppitcheg, môeu, kah wame ass8tam8ongaṣh muttaohkeit, niṣh woskeche ut ohkeit, kah Sheshache ketass8t piṣh wutahtôe wuttattam8moh
25.27 Newaj pish nag unnádt, yeu wussin Jehovah ayeuteaunit um-Manitt8moh Israel, wuttattum8k, kah kogkeiussippam8k, kah menadtam8k, kah kepshunk, kah omohkéhteók, newutche togkodteg ne ân8tam en kenugke kuhhogkaou.
25.28 Kah piṣh n$nih, sekenamohettit nemunumunat wuttattamwaitch wutch kenutcheganit wuttattamunat, neit nag piṣh kuttinóog, yeu wussin Jehovah ayeuteaunit, wunnamuhkut piṣh k8tattamw8.
25.29 Newutche kusseh, nunn8che nuhkinnum machuk ut keitotanat, ne as8wésik wutche n8wesuonk, kah sun woh kuppapaquanne matta sasamatáhwhutteomw8? matta piṣh mat sasamatáhwhutteomw8: newutche n8wehquttum togkodteg ut wame wadohkitcheg ohkeit, wussin Jehovah ayeuteaunit.
25.30 Newutche ayeuuhkonittue quoshódtumau wame yeush kutt8wongash, kah nag us, Jehovah piṣh mishont8wau wutch wohqut, kah kussont8wau wutch 8neetupanatamwe appuonganit, piṣh menuhke mishont8wau ut wutappuonganit, piṣh ogque mishont8wau neg tahtahshkuhkogig weenomineash, ayeuuhkonittue wame wadohkitcheg ohkeit.
25.31 Mishont8waonk piṣh peyaum8 wehqshik ohke: newutche Jehovah penuantam wutohtimoneash: piṣh kéketehtam wame weyaus, neh machetinutcheh ummagunuh en togkodteganit wussin Jehovah.
25.32 Yeu wussin Jehovah ayeuteaunit, kusseh, machuk piṣh sohham8m8 wutch wutohtimoinneat en wutohtimoinneat, kah mishe pemsquoh piṣh waabu wutch weehqshik ohke.
25.33 Kah nashoncheh Jehovah, ne kesukok, piṣh wutch wee[h]qshik muttaok onk yaan weehqshik: nag matta piṣh maumuttam8[on]óog, asuh mukkinóog, asuh posekinóog, nag piṣh anohkeyeu8og ut ohkeit.
25.34 Mishont8wak kenaau nanaushepsaénuog, kah mau8k, kah ôiyômegk pukquee, kenaau negonneweógish ut flokut: newutch kenushitteae kesukodtoash, kah naswaiyeue pakodjteausuash, kah piṣh kutogque penushomw8 wunne wishquadt.
25.35 Kah nanaushepsaenuog matta piṣh ohtoog toh woh ashphow[á]hettit: asuh negonnewutcheg ut flokut pohquohhamunat.
25.36 OOwadtauatonkqussue mauongan8 nanaushepsaenuog, kah wutt8noongan8 negoneyeuutcheg ut flockut, newutche Jehovah matchehteou wuttittanadtupp8ongan8.
25.37 Kah wunohteáe áyeuongaṣh tuméhthamun[a]ṣh, newutche ummishe musquanitteaonk Lord.
25.38 Ahquontam ukkuppiyeum onatuh qunnónou, newutche nag wutohkou touwushin, newutche wutchekee usseonk sunukkutchóhh8waénin, kah newutche wutunkque musquanitteaonk.
26.1 NOOche nanawuñuadt Jehojakim wunnaumonuh Josiah Judae ketass8t, wuttinn8waonk 8m88 Jehovah$ut, n8wau,
26.2 Yeu wussin Jehovah, neepaush chippinneutunkanit ut Jehovah wekit, kah ken8s wame Judae keitotanash, neg paoncheg waussumónat ut wekit Jehovah, wame kutt8wongash nish an8nonish nag unnónaóut: ass[a]nukon pasuk kutt8onk.
26.3 N8tamwehettit, kah nishnoh pasuk qushkeit wutch ummatche mayut, onk woh nutaiuskoiantam ne machuk kodnéhheog, newutche ummatche usseongan8oaṣh.
26.4 Kah piṣh nag kuttinóog yeu wussin Jehovah, matta kukkehtiéog, pomusháonónat naumatuonk noh|pónog anaquabeog.
26.5 N8tamunat ukkutt8wongan8oaṣh quoshodtumwaénue nuttinneumog, neg ann8nogig en kuhhogkaóut, naneeswe nompoáe omohkeon, kah ann8nog (qut matta ken8tamomw8.)
26.6 Neit yeu wetu nutogquehteauun Shiloh, kah yeu keitotan nummatanatamwe hettamwátauun ut wame ohkee wutohtimoneaṣh.
26.7 Neit sephausuenuog kah quoshodtumwaenuog, kah wame missinninnuog n8tauáog Jeremiahoh wussinneat yeush kutt8wongash ut wekit Jehovah.
26.8 Kah n$niyeup mahche Jeremiah unn8wadt wame Jehovah neanunn8nont, ken8nónat wame missinninnuog: sephausuenuog kah quoshodtumwaenuog, kah wame missinninnuog wuttohqunoush, n8waog, wunnamuhkut pish kenup.
26.9 Tohwutch quoshódtuman ut 8wesuonganit Jehovah, unn8waan, yeu wetu piṣh tatuppeyeu8 Shiloh, kah yeu keitotan piṣh touwushin, amtta ayéyinat: kah wame missinninnuog ayeuuhkonittue miyaéhtauwaog Jeremiahoh, ut wekit Jehovah.
26.10 Judae sontimòog yeush n8tamwéhettit, neit nag kuhkuhqueog wutch ketass8t wekit en wekit Jehovah, kah nag appuog ut ahhut petutteamuk wuskesquont ut wekit Jehovah.
26.11 Neit sephausuenuog kah quoshodtumwaenuog ken8naog sontimoh, kah wame missinninnúh n8waog: yeuoh wosketomp tumuhhouau nupp8onk, newutch yeuoh ayeuuhkonittue quoshaeu missohham yeu keitotan, neane n8tamóg ut kuhtauogk8w[ô]ut.
26.12 Neit Jeremiah ken8nau wame sontimoh, kah wame missinninnúh, n8wau, Jehovah nutann8nuk ayeuuhkonittue quoshóe missohhamunat yeu wetu, kah ayeuuhkonittue yeu keitotan, wame kutt8wongash niṣh n8tamógish.
26.13 Newutche yeuyeu sampweteau8k kummay8woash kah kutusseonganóoash, kah n8swehtam8k 8wadtauatonkqussuonk Jehovah kum-Manitt8mw8, kah Jehovah piṣh aiuskoiantam ne machuk ayeuuhkonittue pogkóduttumunkqueóg.
26.14 Qut nen, kusseh, nutap kenutchegan8wout: unnéhhek uttoh an tápeneámók.
26.15 Qut wahteau8k wunnamuhkut, nushéóg, wunnamuhkut piṣh kenuhkenumauómw8 mat woskehuwae musqueheonk ut kuhhogkaóut, kah yeuut otanat, & neg na wadohkitcheg: newutche wunnamuhkut Jehovah nutann8nuk en kuhhogkaout, unn8wonat wame yeush ut kuttauogk8wout.
26.16 Neit sontimoog kah wame missinninnúog, unnaog sephausuenuh, kah quoshodtumwaénúh, yeuoh matta tumuhhouóou nuppun: newutche kukken8nukqun ut 8wesuonganit Lord kum$Manitt8mun.
26.17 Neit nawhutch eldersog ne ohkeit, neepoog kah ken8naog wame mukkinnée missinninnúh, n8waog,
26.18 Micah wut-Moràshit, quoshodtumup pomontog Hezechiah Judae ketass8t, kah ken8nau wame Judae missinninnuh, n8wau, yeu wussin Jehovah ayeuteaunit, Zion piṣh ogque anaskhamun ohteuhkonit, kah Jerusalem piṣh nanómukqueau; kah weetuome wadchu, touohkomukque qunuhqui ayeuongash.
26.19 Hezechiah kah wame Judah wunnushóóussohhoh? sunnummatta wabesuonauous Lord, kah wehquetumauop Lord kah Lord aiuskoiantamup ne machuk, nean pogkodtittumauomp? ne woh nashpe kuppaudtauónan kukketeahogkôununónog mahshe matchuk.
26.20 Wonk na mo wosketomp noh quoshoe missohhogkup ut 8wesuonganit Jehovah, Urijah wunnaumonuh Shemajah, wutche[i] Kirajth$jearim: noh quoshae mussohhogkup ayeuuhkonittue yeu keitotan, kah ayeuuhkonittue yeu ohke, neaunak wame ukkutt8wongash Jeremiah.
26.21 Kah Jehojakim ketass8t, kah wame ummenuhkesuenumoh, kah wame sontimóog n8tamwehettit ukkutt8wongash, ketass8t ukkod-nushoh: qut Urijah n8tog, wabesúp, kah wussemop, kah auop Egypt.
26.22 Kah Jehojakim ketass8t ann8nau wosketompuh en Egypt, Elnathan wunnaumonuh Achbor, kah wosketompoh weechok en Egypt.
26.23 Kah sohh8unaog Urijah wutch Egypt, kah uppas8ouh Jehojakimit ketass8t, kah wunnushoh nashpe togkodteg, kahwuttinnohkonoh nupp8e wuhhogkuh en 8weenohkeout missinninnuog.
26.24 Qut wunnutcheg Ahikam wunnaumonuh Shaphan weetomau Jeremiahoh, matta woh umag8unat en wunnutchegan8óut missinninnúog, wunnushonaout.
27.1 NOOche nanauwunnuadt Jehovjakim wunnaumonuh Josiah Judae ketass8t, yeu kutt8wonk peyaonukqun Jeremiah wutch Lordut, n8wau,
27.2 Yeu Jehovah nuttugqun, ayimau kuhhog kishpissuongash kah yoakash, kah ponsh kussittuppukanit,
27.3 Kah niṣh negonshhuash en Edome ketass8tamwut, kah en Moabe ketass8tamwut, kah en Amonitse ketass8tamwut, kah Tyruse ketass8tamwut, kah Zidone ketass8tamwut, ut wunnutchegan8out onn8naenuog neg paoncheg Jerusalem, en Zedechiahut Judae ketass8t.
27.4 Kah nag us wuttinnon[a]oont wussontimóm8oh: yeu wussin Jehovah ayeuteaunit um-Manitt8moh Israel, yeu piṣh kuttinnoneau wussontimóm8og,
27.5 Nutayim ohke, wosketomp kah puppinashim neg apitcheg wosketohkeit, nashpe ummishe menuhkesuonk, kah nashpe summagunumwe nuhput, kah nuttinnumauón uttoh woh kod aninnumaúog.
27.6 Kah yeuyeu wame yeush wutohtimoneash nummagunash en wunnutcheganit Nebuchadnezzar Babilone ketass8t, nuttinneum, kah ohteuhkone puppinashimwog wonk nuttinninnumau, 8tinninneumuhkongqunat.
27.7 Kah wame wutohtimoneash pish 8tinninneumuhkauouh, kah wunnaumonuh, kah wunnaumonuh wunnaumonuh, nô pajeh wutohkeé ahquompiyeum peyaum8uk: kah neit monateash wutohtimoneash kah mogke ketass8tamwog pish 8chiyeuounouh.
27.8 Kah pish n$nih, ne wutohtimoin, kah ass8tamoonk ne matta wadtinninneumuhkauog nenan Nebucadnezzar Babilone ketass8t, kah matta agwe ponamog wussittuppuk 8weyokum Babilone ketass8t, ne wutohtimoin pish nussásamatahhamun, wussin Lord, nashpe togkodteg, kah nashpe mahshagquodt, kah nashpe enninneaonk, nô pajeh nummohtupanonaoont nashpe wunnutcheg.
27.9 Newutche ahque n8tau, kukquoshodtumwaenumog, asuh quoshae missohhamwaenuog, asuh kuttinnukquomweneum8woog, asuh kuppauwom8oog, asuh kummoneteum8oog, neg ànukqueogig, n8waog, matta pish k8tinninneumuhkauomw8 Babilone ketass8t.
27.10 Newutche nag kuppann8wae quoshodtumunk8oog, nòadtit kuttin ontashikq[a]nnaoont wutch kutohtuout, ônk woh kussohh8kauununnaoont, onk woh kenuppunaoont.
27.11 Qut wutohtimoneash neg paudtunkeg wussittipukan8 ut agwe weyokumut Babilone ketass8t, kah wadtinneumuhkauoncheg yeug nutappeheoog nehenwonche wutohtkeyeuout, wussin Lord, kah nag pish wutohteuhkoneau, kah pish na 8tohkinneau.
27.12 Kah wonk nuttin Zedéchiah Judae ketass8t neaunak wame yeush kutt8wongash nussip, paudto8k kussittippukanash ut agwe weyokum Babilone ketass8t, kah noh wuttinneumuhkok, kah ummissinninnumoh kah pomantam8k.
27.13 Tohwaj nuppog, ken kah kummissinninnumog nashpe togkodteg, nashpe mahshagquodt, kah nashpe enninneaonk neane ayeuuhkonittue ken8tog Jehovah wutohtimoin noh matta wadtinninnumuhkauonk Babilone ketass8t?
27.14 Newutche kuhkeitam8hteok wuttinn8waongan8oash quoshodtumwaeenuog, neg kon8nukqueogig, n8wahettit, matta pish k8tinninneumuhkauomw8 Babilone ketass8t: newutch kuppann8wae quoshodtumunk8oog.
27.15 Newutche mag nag nutann8noog, wussin Jehovah, qut onch pann8wae quoshodtumwog ut n8wesuonganit, onk woh kussohh8kauunumw8, onk woh kuppagwanyimw8 kenaau kah quoshodtumwaenuog ne quoshae missohhamunkqueogig.
27.16 Kah wonk nukken8nomp sephausuenuog, kah wame missinninnuog, nussip, yeu wussin Jehovah, n8tam8hteok ukkutt8wongan8oash kukquoshodtumwaeneum8oog neg quoshae missohhamunkqueogig, n8waog, kusseh, wishquash ut Jehovah wekit, pish teanuk nompe paudtauunash wutch Babilon, Newutche nag kuppann8wae quoshodtumunk8oog.
27.17 Nag ahque n8tau: wuttinneumuhkok Babilone ketass8t, kah pomantam8k: tohwutch woh yeu keitotan mahchumwushik?
27.18 Qut tohneit nag quoshodtumwaenuhettit, kah wuttinn8waonk Jehovah toh$neit nah weetomont, peantamauwahettich yeuyeu Jehovah ayeuteaunit, nish wishquash sequshunkish ut wekit Jehovah, kah weekit Judae ketass8t, kah ut Jerusalem, onk woh mo 8mun8ash Babilon.
27.19 Newutche yeu n8wau Jehovah ayeuteaunit, papaume pillarsash, kah papaume keitoh, kah papaume agweyeu8gish, kah papaume ashqshunkish wishquash, nish|ohtagish yeu otanat.
27.20 Nish Nebuchadnezar Babilone ketass8t mat neemunum8gkupash, masinohtead Jeconiah wunnaumonuh Jehojachin Judae ketass8t, wutch Jerusaleme en Babilon kah wame Judae kah Jerusalem sontimoog.
27.21 Nux yeu wussin Jehovah ayeuteaunit um-Manitt8moh Israel papaume wishquash nish ashqshunkish ut Jehovah wekit, k[á]h ut wekit Judae ketass8t kah Jerusalém.
27.22 Nash pish uss8tauunash Babylon, kah na pish ohteau nô pajeh ne kesukok nag natauwaheog wussin Lord, neit pish wonk nukkuhkuhk8uttauunash, kah nompatauunash yeu ut ayeuonganit.
28.1 KAh n$niyeup ne nan kodtumuk n8che nánawunnuadt Zedechiah Judae ketass8t, yaue kodtum8g, kah napanna adtahs8it nepauz, Hananiah wunnaumonuh Azur quoshodtumwaen, noh wadchiit Gibeon, nukk[e]n8nuk ut Jehovah wekit, ut anaquabhettit sephausuenuog, kah wame missinninnúog, n8wau,
28.2 Yeu wussin Lord ayeuteaunit um-Manitt8moh Israel n8wau, nuppohqshan weyoakumoh Babilone ketass8t.
28.3 Wuttuhshit yeu neeneese kodtum8, piṣh wonk nuppaudto yeuut ayeuonganit wame wishquash wadchikiish Jehovah wekit, niṣh Nebucad-nezzer Babilone ketass8t amaunukupash yeu wutch ayeuonganit, kah as8tunkupash Babilon.
28.4 Kah wonk nuppasou yeuut ayeuonganit Jeconiah wunnaumonuh Jehoiachim Judae ketass8t, weeche wame missinóog neg aumpanneg Babilon wussin Jehovah, newutche nuppokshadtoh weyokum Babilone ketass8t
28.5 Neit Jeremiah quoshodtumwaén unnau quoshodtumwaenúh Hananiah ut anaquabhettit sephausuenuog, kah ut anaquabhettit wame missinninnúog, neg neepauutcheg wekit Lord.
28.6 Quoshodtumwaen Jeremiah n8wau, Amen, Jehovah ne usseiteh, Lord usseitch wuttinn8waongash niṣh quoshae missohhogish, paudtauunat wonk wishquash wadchiigish wekit Jehovah kah neg wame másinóhteamukuppanneg, wutch Babilon, yeuut ayeuonganit.
28.7 Qut yeuyeu n8tash yeu kutt8wonk an8wi ut kehtauogkut, kah ut wuhtauogkut wame missinninnúh.
28.8 Quoshodtumwaenuog neg negonuhkiitcheg, & neg negonuhkunkqueaneg n8adt, nag ayeuuhkonittue quoshoe missohhamwontamwog monaash wutohtimoneash, kah kehche ass8tam8ongash, papaume mattompagq, kah papaume machuk, kah papaume enninneaonl.
28.9 Quoshodtumwaen noh quoshae missohhog wunohteaonk, wuttinn8waonk quoshodtumwaen nnák, neit quoshodtumwaen piṣh waheau, wunnamuhkut Jehovah wutañ8nuh.
28.10 Neit Hannaniah quoshodtumwaen, nemunau yoakoh wutch Jeremiah quoshodtumwaen wussittuppukanit, kah uppohqenumun.
28.11 Kah Hannaniah kutt8, ut wame anaquabhettit missinninnúog n8wau, yeu wussin Lord, ne nuttinne pohquenon weyokumoh Nebuchadnezzar Babilone ketass8t, wutch wussittippukan8wóut wame wutohtimóneunk, ash naneese kodtumun8kup, kah Jeremiah quoshodtumwaen monchu.
28.12 Neit wuttinn8waonk Jehovah peyaónuk Jeremiah quoshodtumwaen (mahche Hananiah quoshodtumwaen pohquenont yoakoh wutch wussittippukanit Jeremiah quoshodtumwaen) n8wau,
28.13 Monch, us Hannaniah n8wash, yeu wussin Jehovah, ken kuppohquenum mehtugque yokash, qut nag piṣ[k] kenompe ayimauoog mussehchuogque yoakoh.
28.14 Newutche yeu wussin Jehovah ayeuteaunit um-Manitt8moh Israel nupponam misséhchuogque yoak wussittippukan8óut wame wutohtimóinneunk, onk woh nag wuttinneumuhkauaog Nebucchad-nezzar Babilone ketass8t, kah nag piṣh 8tinninneumuhkauouh kah wonk nuttinninnumau wonk ohteuhkone puppinashimwoh.
28.15 Neit Jeremiah quoshodtumwaen unnau Hananiahoh quoshodtumwaen: yeuyeu n8tash Hananiah, Jehovah matta kut[á]nn8nuk8h, qut yeug missinninnúog kuppabahtantamwaheóog pann8waonk.
28.16 Newutche yeu wussin Jehovah, kusseh, kuppogkenush wutch wosket-ohkit: yeu kodtumuk piṣh kenup newutche kukkuhk8tomwehteam cheketauónat Lord.
28.17 Neit Hannaniah quoshodumwaen nup ne nan kodtumuk, nabo nesausuk adtahs8it nepauz.
29.1 YEuyeu yeush wussukwhosue kutt8wongash, nish Jeremiah quoshodtumwaen negonshhuadche wutch Jerusalem, en ashqshoncheg eldersog, neg masinóhteámukeg, kah en sephausuénuut, kah en quoshodtumwaenuut, kahen wame missinninnuut, neh Nebuchhádnezzar másinohteacheh wutch Jerusalem en Babilon.
29.2 (Ne mahche Jeconiah ketass8t, kah sonksq, kah eunuchsog, kah Judae kah Jerusaleme sontimoog, kah weekitteaenuog, kah smithsog mahche amaeog wutch Jerusalem)
29.3 Nashpe wunnutcheganit Elasah wunnaumonuh Shaphan, kah Gemariah wunnaumonuh Hilkiah, neh Zedechiah Judae ketass8t ánan8noncheh Babilon, en Nebucchadnezzar Babilone ketass8t n8wau,
29.4 Yeu wuttinnon Jehovah ayeuhteaunit um$Manitt8moh Israel, wame neh másinóhteamukeh, neg masináhhuwáheogig wutch Jerusalem en Babilon.
29.5 Wekikunk kah ne ayék, kah ohteuhkontam8k tanohketeaongash, kah meech8k ne nóh adtanegik.
29.6 Ummittamwussek, kah wunnaumonaek kah wuttaunek, kah ummittamwussuhkók kenaumona[o]og, kah 8wessukkauhkok kuttaun8oog, onk woh nag wunnaumoniyeuog kah wuttaunuog, onk woh na kuttit monôneau, kah matta kutogguhs8mw8.
29.7 Kah nattinneham8k 8nohteaonk ne keitotan uttoh an missinóhkonittuáhinóg, kah peantamwanshúk Jehovahut, newutche ne piṣh k8nohteamw8 wunohteom8uk.
29.8 Newutche yeu wussin Jehovah ayeuteaunit um-Manitt8moh Israel, kukquosh[ó]dtumwaenúmog, kah quoshoe missohhogig, neg apitcheg kenashom8óut as8kekodteamuk8teok, kah kuhkeihtam8hteok kuttinukquom8ongan8oash, nish anukquo[m]ogish.
29.9 Newutche nag pann8waeu kukquoshoe missohhamunk8oog ut n8wesuonganit: matta nag nutann8noog wussin Lord.
29.10 Newutche yeu wussin Jehovah, mahche nesausuk tahshinchage kodtum8ash mahtshunk ut Babilon, pish kenatauwahunumw8, kah pish nutussem n8ne kutt8onk en kuhhogkaoont, kukquinnuppekompauwah[eo]un naoont yeu en ayeuonganit.
29.11 Newutche n8wahteoh unnanetam8ongash, nish ananatamonish en kuhhogkaout, wussin Jehovah, wunohteae unnantam8ongash, kah matta machuk, kuttinnumauununaoont pahtussuwontamoe wohkukquoshin.
29.12 Neit pish kuppeantamaiimw8, kah pish kummonchem8, kah pish kuppeantamiimw8, kah pish ken8tauunumw8.
29.13 Kah pish kenatinneahimw8, kah pish kummishkiimw8, natinneahwheog nashpe mamusse kuttahhou.
29.14 Kah pish kenamhimw8 8wau Jehovah, kah pish nukquinnuppinum kummissinnoongan8, kah kummukkinunumw8 wutch wame wutohtimoinneat, kah wutch wame ayeuonganehtu uttoh ann8hkauunog, wussin Jehovah kah wonk pish kuppas8unumw8, ut ayeuonganit ne$waj missinohkonuwahinogkup.
29.15 Newutche kussimwop, Jehovah kuttahshinumunkq[un] quoshodtumwaenuh ut Babylon,
29.16 Yeu wussin Jehováh papaume ketass8t noh quenapit wutappuonganit David, kah papaume wame missinninnuog neg apitcheg ne otanat, kah papaume kematt8oog neg matta weeche sohham8muk8ogig en missinnainneut.
29.17 Yeu wussin Jehovah ayeuteaunit, kusseh, nunnuhkinnumauoog togkodteg, mahshagquodt kah enninneaonk kah nutogqheoog nishkeneunkque figsut, nish woh mo meech8mukish newutche matchitash.
29.18 Kah nag nunn8sittahwhoog, nashpe togkodteg, kah nashpe máhshagquodt, kah nashpe enninneaonk, kah nag nupponoog ontsappinneat en wame ass8tam8ongash ut muttaohkit: mattanumwae unnonaoont, kah chepshónaóont & mishonánumónaoont, kah kekomonaoont ut kenugke wame wutohtimoneat uttoh ann8hkauog.
29.19 Newutche matta kukkeitamoog nukkutt8wongash wussin Jehovah, nish negons[h]huwaánish nashpe quoshodtumwae nuttinnumog, nompoae omohkeon, kah ann8nog qut matta ken8tam8mw8 wussin Jehovah.
29.20 Newutche n8tam8k wuttinn8waonk Jehovah, wame kenaau missinoog neg ann8nogeg wutch Jerusalem en Babylon.
29.21 Yeu wussin Jehovah ayeuteaunit um-Manitt8moh Israel, papaume Ahab wunnaumonuh Kolajah, kah papaume Zedechiah wunnaumonuh Maasejah, nag quoshae missohhogig pann8waonk ut n8wesuonganit, kuss[é]h, nag nupponôog ut wunnutcheganit Nebuchad-nezzar Babilone ketass8t, kah noh piṣh wunnushoh ut anaquabeóg.
29.22 Kah nag papaume matanumwe uttuonk piṣh neemunnuma[u]óog wame Judae masin[á]itcheg, apitcheg Babilon, n8waog, Jehovah ogquehikqush Zedechiahut, kah Ahabut, neh Babilone ketass8t app8sipuh ut n8taut.
29.23 Newutche usseog nishkeneunkqussuonk ut Israel, kah mamussuog weetatteamunganóuh ummittamwuss8oh, kah n8waog pann8wae kutt8wongash ut n8wesuonganit, niṣh matta ann8nóogish nen n8wahteauunnash kah n8wauwaénuh, wussin Jehovah.
29.24 Yeu wonk piṣh kuttinnon Shemajah wut-Nehelamit, n8wash,
29.25 Yeu wussin Jehovah ayeuteaunit um-Manitt8moh Israel n8wau, newutche negonshhuau lettersash ut k8wesuonganit en wame missinninnuut neg apitcheg Jerusalem, kah en Shephaniahut wunnaumonuh Maasejah sephausuwaen, en wame sephausuwaénuut, kussip,
29.26 Jehovah kenompe sephausuwaenuwahik Jehojada sephausuwaen, onk woh kenaau aninnohsuenuog ut wekit Lord, wutch niṣh$noh pasuk noh kâgkéadt, kah quoshodtumwaenuwáheont wuhhogkuh, onk woh kukkupshagkin, kah ut stoksut.
29.27 Newutche yeuyeu, tohwutch mat auskomóad Jeremiah, wut-Anathoth, noh quoshodtumwaenuwáheont wuhhogkuh en kuhhogkaóut?
29.28 Newutche newaj negonshhuau en kuhhogkanónut ut Babilon, n8wau, yeu missinno8onk sepeyeu8, wekekunk & ne ayék, ohkehteagk tanohketeaongash, kah meech8k ne adtannegik.
29.29 Kah Zephaniah sephausuaen yeu wutogketamun wussukwheg, ut wuhtauogkit Jeremiah quoshodtumwaen.
29.30 Neit wuttinn8waonk Jehovah peyaonuk Jeremiah n8wau,
29.31 Aunchem8kae negonshhuash wame missinóog n8wash, yeu wussin Jehovah, papaume Shemajah wut-Nehelamit, newutche Shemajah kukquoshoe missohhamwa[n]shikkou, kah matta nutann8nuh, kah kuppabuhtanumwahikou pann8waonk;
29.32 Newutche yeu wussin Jehovah, kusseh, nussasametah Shemajah wut-Nehelamit, kah 8skanneumuneoh: matta piṣh 8wosketomp8moh ayeoh kenugke yeug missinninnúog, kah matta piṣh naum8 wanegik, ne piṣh aseaunshau nummissinninnúmog wussin Jehovah, newutche kuhk8tomwehteau cheketauónat Jehovah.
30.1 WUttinn8waonk ne pauhônukqut Jeremiah wutch Jehovah$ut, n8wau,
30.2 Yeu wussin Jehovah um-Manitt8moh Israel, n8wau, wame kutt8wongash nish ánunonish, wussukhumush ut b8kut.
30.3 Newutche kusseh, kesukodtash peyaum8, wussin Jehovah, wonk nuppaudto ummissinnoongan8 Israelle kah Judae nummissinninnumog, wussin Jehovah, kah wonk nukqushkeáheaog en ohkeit ne anumauogkup 8sh8uh, kah nag pish wutoht[à]uuneau.
30.4 Kah yeush kutt8ongash nish Jehovah an8wopash papaume Israelloh kah papaume Judahoh.
30.5 Newutche yeu wussin Jehovah nunn8támumun nunnukshae kah wabesue wuttauatonkqussuonk, kah matta wunohteae.
30.6 Nat8tamwehte8k yeuyeu, kah naum8k sun wosketomp onkquommom8e neechau? tohwaj naum niṣh$noh wosketomp wunnutchegash ogque ut wusseganit mittamwoṣsis neechadt, kah wame muskesukquaṣh quinnuppem8aṣh en wompekuṣhonat.
30.7 Woi, newutche ne kesukok miṣsi, newaj wanne tatuppein8g: ne ahquompi ne adt Jakob wuttamehpunadt, qut piṣh na wutch wadchanon.
30.8 Newutch piṣh n$nih ne kesukok, wuṣsin Jehovah ayeuteaunit, nuppohqun weyokumoh wutch kuṣsittippukanit, kah nuppashkukkom kukkenepissuongash, kah pen8wohteaog matta piṣh wonk 8chiéináuh naṣhpe nahoh.
30.9 Qut nag piṣh wuttinneumuhkauáog Jehovah um-Manitt8m8oh, kah Davidoh ukketass8tamomoh neh piṣh tahshinnumauogeh.
30.10 Newutche wabesehkon woi nuttinninneum Jakob, wuṣsin Jehovah, asuh chepshuhteogk woi Israel: newutche kusseh, piṣh k8wadchanṣh wutch noadtit, kah k8skannemuneog wutch ummiṣinae ohkeyeout, kah Jakob piṣh qushku kah piṣh anwohsin, & pish chequnappu, kah matta piṣh howan 8wabesuwaheuh.
30.11 Newutche k8weetomsh wussin Jehovah k8wadchanunat tôkonogque n8wohkukquoshitteauun wame wutohtimoneash uttoh an seahwhun: qut onk matta k8wohkukquosumun8: qut quttuhham8e kussásamatohwhush, kah matta mamusse mat kussasamatahwhun8 kenukkonun8.
30.12 Newutche yeu wussin Jehovah, ken8chumweteahwhutteaonk matta woh neetskehteauouun, kah k8wosketeawhutteaonk unkqueneunkquot.
30.13 Matta howan kukkeket8konshik8, onk woh kutasseepsu: wanne kutahtoou ne neetskehuwom8uk.
30.14 Wame womonacheg k8wananumuk, matta nag kenatinneahik8og, newutché ken8chumwehtoush nashpe matwae n8chumwetahwhuttuonk, nashpe wussasamatuhh8waonk unkqueneunkqussit, wutch mataanukish kummatcheseongash, newutche kummatcheseongash nano monat[a]sh.
30.15 Tohwutch wuttuhpôsean kutunkquanumoonk? kutunkquanumoonk matta woh neetskehteauouun, newutche mataanukish kummatcheseongash, newutche kummatcheseongash nano monatash waj yeu unnehen.
30.16 Newaj wame neg mahchipp8wonukqueaneg, nag pish mahchipwutuog, kah wame ayeuuhkonuhqueaneg nag pish missinno8og, nish$noh pasuk, kah nag magk8kinukqueaneg, pish mukk8kinittuog, & wame neg chechekqunukqueaneg, pish chechequnaog.
30.17 Newutche kenompenumoush neetskehettuonk, kah keneetskehteoush ken8chumwetahwhutteaongash, wussin Lord, newutche nag kutuss8wenukquog pagkenit: n8wahettit, yeuoh Zion, matta howan natinneawhonkeh.
30.18 Yeu wussin Jehovah, kusseh, wonk nuppaudtoh Jakob ummissinnae komukquash, kah nummonaneteam wutáyeuonganooash, kah keitotan pish ayimun ut nehenwonche 8wadchumut; kah mishikkomuk pish sepohteau neaunak wuttinniyeuonk.
30.19 Kah nag wutch pish sohham8m8 tabuttantamoonk, kah 8wadtauatonkqussuongan8 neg pôacheg, kah nag nummuttaanheoog, kah nag matta pish ogguhs88og; nag wonk nussohsumwaheoog, kah n[a]g matta pish ogguhs8og.
30.20 wunneechan8oh wonk pish tatuppeyeu8oh n8adt, ummukkinneongan8 pish menehketeauun ut anaquabeh: kah nussasamatoh wame neg sanakutchohwhoncheg.
30.21 Kah ukkencheiyeum8uh pish nehenwoncheyeu8og kah wunnanawunnuaeneum8oh pish wutch sohhamog wutch wunnasha[u]m8o[ut]: nkah nuppas8tshah, kah noh pish nuppas8su[k]unk: newutche howan yeuoh quoshauom8uk wuttah nuppas8sukunkqunat wussin Jehovah.
30.22 Kah kenaau pish nummiṣsinninnuog, kah nen kum-Manitt8mw8.
30.23 Kusseh uppemsquohhumoh Jehovah chekee sohham, sepohtae pemsquoh, onkquomom8e pish appu uppuhkukqut matcheetou
30.24 Ummishe musquanitteaonk Jehovah matta pish qushkemun8 nô pajeh mahche usseit, kah nó pajeh mahche ussenat wuttahh8wae unnantam8ongash: ut maumachish késukodtut pish kenatwontamumw8.
31.1 NEnan ahquompag wuṣsin Jehovah nen um-Manitt8m8oh wame wutteateashiyeuongan8 Israel, kah nag pish num[-]miṣsinninnumog.
31.2 Yeu wussin Jehovah, missinninnuog neg ashquttahwhoncheh togkodteg namehteoog kitteamonteanittuonk ut touohkomukqut, Israel, nonche anwohsinw[a]heog.
31.3 Jehovah n8adt nunnaehtunk, n8wau, nux, kenashpe womonsh machemohtag womonittuonk: newaj nashpe womonittuonk kuppas8tshahesh.
31.4 Wonk, k8weekekonsh, kah pish k8weekekonit woi Israelle penomp, pish wonk kenashpe wunn8whos kuttabretsash, kah pish kussohhom ut uppumukkaongan8oont neg weekontogeg.
31.5 Pish wonk kutohketeam weenomwussippogwosh ut Samaria wadchutu, ohkehteaenuog pish wutohteakonaoash, kah nish pish nutogque meechinaoash nanweguk.
31.6 Newutche pish kesukodu8, askuhwheteaenuog ut 8wadchumut Ephraim pish mishont8waog, neepok, kah kuhkuhquetuh en Zion en Jehovah num-Mánitt8mut.
31.7 Newutche yeu wussin Jehovah, weekontamwe ket8hamwanshuk Jákob, kah mishont8agk ut kenugke kehche wutohtimoinneat n8tamwahuwagk, tabuttántam8k, kah n8wak, woi Jehovah wadchán kummissinninnumog, sekqshoncheg ut Israel.
31.8 Kusseh, nag n8s8woog nanumohkeit, kah nag nummukkinoog wutch wekqshik óhke, kah nag kenugke pogkenukeg kah quanukquesitcheg, kah wompequae mittamwossis, kah noh neechadt moeu, m8chequshaog pish na wuttin quinnuppenau.
31.9 Nag pish maue peyaog, kah nashpe peantam8ongash nussagkompa[n]oog: nuppannupwushaheáog sepupagwut, en sampwe mayut uttoh matta pish togkuṣsittassunehettég: newutche nen 8sh8oh Israel kah Ephraim noh mohtammegheog.
31.10 N8tam8k wuttinn8waonk Jehovah woi kenáau wutohtimoinneunk, kah wahteauwahuagk en n8adte m[u]nahhannehtu, kah n8wak, noh seahwhont Israelloh pish ummoúnuh, kah pish wutogque nanawéheuh nanaushepsuenuut ufflokumut.
31.11 Newutche Jehovah man8hwhau Jakoboh, kah wuttáphumauónuh neh anúe menuhkesumukqutcheh.
31.12 Newaj piṣh peyahettit kah ket8hamóog ut kodtuhkóag Zion, kah nag piṣh moe kussitchuwanúog ut 8nétuwonganit Jehovah, wutch wheatash, kah wutche wine, kah wutche pummee, kah wutch floke kah hearde wuskoshimwesit: kah ukketeáhogkon8oh piṣh tatuppeyeu8oh sokenippontamwe tanohketeaonganit, kah matta piṣh wonk unkquanumoog.
31.13 Neit penomp piṣh pumukáeu muskauantam, naneeswe kehchiog kah wuskenuog moeu: newutche nukquinnuppinnum ummauongan8 en weekontam8onganit, kah nuttapheóog, kah nummuskauantamwaheoog mahche onkquanumwéhettit.
31.14 Kah nuttapehteau ukketeahogkôunoh seph[á]usuwaen nashpe wees, kah nummissinninnúmog piṣh tapheóog wanegik, wussin Jehovah.
31.15 Yeu wussin Jehovah, wuttauatonkqussuonk n8tonkquod ut Ramah, maumuttam8onk, kah weesogohp[ó]suonk, Rachel mauémont wunneechanoh sekeneam taphettinneat wutch wunneechanoh, newutche nag matta ayeu8og.
31.16 Yeu wussin Jehovah, quehtittaush kummauongane wadtauatonqussuonk, kah kuskesukque missippegwash, newutche kutanakausuonk piṣh onkquodtantamun, wussin Jehovah, kah nag piṣh wonk 8mwog wutohtuóut matwaug.
31.17 Kah ne annoósuonganú8 ut k8wóhkukquosininat, wussin Jehovah, onk woh keneechanog wonk peyaog ut nehenwonche wutohkeit.
31.18 Wunnamuhkut nunn8tamup Ephraim maumuttamwaheont wuhhogkuh, kussasamatahheh, kah nussasamatahwhutteap; onatuh ox asquam yokhôsegk: quinnuppineh, kah piṣh nukquinnuppinit, newutche ken Jehovah num-Manitt8m.
31.19 Wunnamuhkut mahche quinnuppinitteap, nutaiuskoiantamup: kah mahche kuhk8tomonteaon nupponketahhamup neehquau: nutakodchip, nux nutchepshomp, newutche nunnayeutamup n8skenue kehkomitteaonk.
31.20 Sun Ephraim womonog nunnaumon? sun noh nuttapeneaue mukkies? newutche nadteah ayeuuhkonittue ken8nog, nummenuhke ash pumme mehquanum; newaj nunnogkis na[b] wutt[à]mánumont, wunnamuhkut piṣh nummonanum, wussin Jehovah.
31.21 Wunohtoush, maye kuhkinneasuongash: mishe numwonkquodtush: ponsh kuttah nogque toumáogquehtu, may ne ayôop: qushkish wonk woi Israelle penomp, qushkish wonk en kukkeitotanahtu.
31.22 Toh kuttitt8che papaumṣham, woi ken as8ep8sue wuttaunin? newutch Lord kesteauun wuske ne teag ut ohkeit: mittamwossis piṣh quinuppekauau wosketompoh.
31.23 Yeu wussin Jehovah ayeuteaunit um-Manitt8moh Israel, aṣhpumme yeu piṣh auwohteaog kutt8onk ut ohkit Judah, kah ut ukkeitotanahtu, wonk paudtauon ummissinnoongan8, wunánumukquṣh Jehovah, woi sampweusseae ayeuonk, kah wunneetupanatamwe wadchu.
31.24 Kah ohketeaenuog piṣh ayeuog Judah, kah ut wame ukkeitotanehtu moeu; kah nag sohwhuttunkeg flocksaṣh.
31.25 Newutche nuttapeh sauunumwe keteahogkou, kah numwaméchumeh niṣh$noh neuantamwe keteahogkou.
31.26 Yeu ânag, nutt8hkep, nunnatauwompip, kah nukouéonk wunnegen ut nuhhogkat.
31.27 Kusseh, kesukodtaṣh peyaum8 wussin Jehovah, nutohketeam wek Israel kah wek Judah nashpe wosketompae wuskannem, kah nashpe puppinaṣhimwe wuskannem.
31.28 Kah piṣh n$nih, neane nag askuhwhekonog, nukkôdtinónat, kah pohqunónat, kah nukkepuhkonat, kah pagwanonat, kah onkapunuhkonat, ne nuttinne askuhwhekonóneáu weekekonat, ohteuhkonat, wussin Lord.
31.29 Ut yeuṣh kesukodtaṣh matta piṣh wonk n8wa8og, wut8shinneunk meechwog seáne weenominneaṣh, kah mukkiog wusketompeteáog.
31.30 Qut niṣh$noh pasuk piṣh nupp8wontam nehenwonche ummatcheseonk, niṣh$noh pasuk noh meechik seáne wenominneaṣh, piṣh wuskeompeteau.
31.31 Kusseh, kesukodtaṣh peyaum8aṣh wussin Jehovah, piṣh nutáyimau wuske wunn8waonk wek Israel, kah wek Judah.
31.32 Matta neaunak wunn8waonk ne ayimauogkup 8sh8uh, ne kesukok ânunog wunnutchegan8out, sohh8wunónat wutch ohkeit Egypt, ne n8n8waonk pohquenumhettit, tôkonogque nen nag wásukó8uh wussin Jehovah.
31.33 Qut ne wunn8waonk ne áyimauog wek Israel, mahche yeuṣh kesukodtaṣh, wussin Jehovah, nuppon nuttinnaumatuonk wuttinnomiyeum8óut, kah n8sukkuhhumun ut wuttahh8wout, kah neen um-Manitt8moh, kah nag piṣh nummissinninnúmog.
31.34 Kah matta piṣh wonk kuhk8tomauó8 niṣh$noh pasuk weetatteamung, kah niṣh$noh pasuk wematoh, n8wonat wahúk Jehovah: newutche nag piṣh wame n8wahikquóg, wutch p[e]ississit pajeh másukkenuk wussin Jehovah, newutche nutahquontamauóog ummatcheseongan8, kah matta wonk nummequontam8 ummatcheseongan8.
31.35 Yeu wussin Lord, noh maguk nepauzsoh wutch kesukque wequai, kah nanepauh[s]hadt, & anogqse kuhquttum8ongash wutch nuhkonáe wequai; noh chachapenuk keitoh, tukk8og mahshont8wahetticheh, Jehóvah ayeuuhteanit ussowesu.
31.36 Yeush kuhk8wwaongash amaem8uk wutch anaquabeh wussin Jehovah, neit 8skannemuneoh Israel piṣh wohkukquoshinin wutohtimo88ut anaquabeh micheme.
31.37 Yeu wussin Jehovah tohneit kesuk wohqut woh quttuhhumuk, kah quenohtag ohke mishkomuk ut agque, nen piṣh wonk nuppogketam wame 8skannem Israel, wutch wame ne matche ussehettit, wussin Jehovah.
31.38 Kusseh kesukkodtash peyaum8ash wussin Jehovah, keitotan piṣh ayimauau Jehovah, wutch qunnikommuk Hananeel, wehque [hâssá]nue squontamut.
31.39 Kah quttuhhumoe pemuneat piṣh na en piuhsuke summagunumun, ut wadchuut Gareb, kah piṣh weenisheáu wehque Gath.
31.40 Kah mamusse 8nôuhkoiyeu nupp8e muhhogkunk, kah pukque, kah ohteuhkonash wehque sepuissit Kidron, wehque adt nahshik horsese wutchepwoiyeue squont, piṣh wunneetupanatamweyeu8 en Lordut, matta piṣh pohqunnum8un, asuh wonk kepuhteaun micheme.
32.1 KUtt8onk ne p[á]uh[ô]nukqut Jeremiah wutch Jehovahut, ut uppiukque kodtum8mut Zedechiah Judae ketass8t, ne nabo shwosuk wutteáshe kodtum8m Nebuchad-nezar.
32.2 Newutche neit ukkenauwameonk Babilone ketass8t weenuhkom Jerusalem: kah Jeremih quoshodtumwaen kuppuhhôsu ut chippinnutongane kuppishagkinittuonganit, ne ut wekit Judae ketass8t.
32.3 Newutche Zedechiah Judae ketass8t ukkuppuhwhoh, n8wau, tohwaj quoshodtuman, n8w[a]an, yeu wussin Lord, kusseh, nummag ne keitotan ut wunnutcheganit Babilone ketass8t, kah noh piṣh wussohkomun?
32.4 Kah Zedechiah Judae ketass8t matta piṣh pohquohham8 wutch wunnutchegan8óut Caledansog, qut wunnamuhkut noh piṣh ponau wunnutcheganit Babilone ketass8t, kah mutt8n8e piṣh keket8koadtuog, kah piṣh wuskesuk88ash moninneadtum8ash.
32.5 Kah noh piṣh uss8wunau Zedechiahhoh en Babilon, kah na piṣh wutappin nô pajeh nunnátauahónat, wussin Jehovah, tôkonogque kutáyeuuhkonon Caldeansog, matta piṣh kussohkôsu.
32.6 Kah Jeremiah n8wau, wuttinn8waonk Jehovah nuppeyaonuk n8wau,
32.7 Kusseh, Hanameel wunnaumonuh Shallum, kussusses, noh piṣh kuppeyaónuk, n8wau, adtôash nutohteuk ne ut Anathoth: ne wutche kussampwe adtôon.
32.8 Neit Hanameel n8susses wunnaumonuh nuppeyaonuk ut kuppishagkinnittue chippinneutunganit, neaunak wuttinn8waonk Lord, kah nuttinuk, [á]dtôash nutohteuk, k8wehquetumoush, ne ut An[a]thoth, ne ut wutohkit Benjamin; newutche sampwe ohto[ó]nk ne kuttaihe, kah adtoâonk kuttaihe, adt[ô]ash ken. Neit n8wahteóh ne wuttinn8waonk Jehovah.
32.9 Kah nuttaphumauop wutohteuk Hanameel nussusses wunnaumonuh, ut Aanathoth, kah nukquthamau teaugwash, nabo nesausuk tahshinash silvere shekelsash.
32.10 Kah n8sukkuhhumup wussukwhosuongash, kah nukkehkinneas[ú]hkonah, kah n8wauwaeneúteáp, kah nukquthum[á]uop teagwash ut quttompagh8teganit.
32.11 Neit nunneemunomp adtô[á]e wussukwhosuongash, naneeswe ne kahkinne[a]sukósik neaunak naumatuonk, kah uṣhuwaonk, kah ne wôshwohtag.
32.12 Kah adtô[á]e wussukwhosuongash nuttinnumauomp Baruch wunnaumonuh Neriah, wunnaumonuh Maasejah, ut anaquabit Hanameel nussusses wunnaumonuh, kah ut anaquabhettit wauwacheg, neg wásukkuhhukeg adtoáe wussukwhosuonk, ut anaquabhettit wame Jewsog, neg apitcheg kuppishagkinittue chippinnutunkanit.
32.13 Kah nummeechumuhkonomp Baruch, ut anaquabhettit, nussip,
32.14 Yeu wussin Jehovah ayeuteaunit um-Manitt8moh Israel, yeush neemunush wussukwhosuongash, adtoae wussukwhosuongash, naneeswe ne sealhausik, kah ne woshwohtag wussukwhosuonk, kah ponsh ohkee wishqut, onk woh nish m8cheke kesukquohtaash.
32.15 Newutche yeu wussin Jehovah ayeuteaunit umManitt8moh Israel, weetuomash, kah ohtéuhkonash, kah wenominneohtekonash piṣh wonk ohtauunash yeuut ohkeit.
32.16 Kah mag8on adtoáe wussukwhosuongash en Barachut wunnaumonuh Neriah, nuppeantamauomp Jehovah, nussip,
32.17 Woi Lord Manit, kusseh, kukkezteoh kesuk kah ohke nashpe kummishe menuhkesuonk kah kussummagunnum8e kuhpit, kah monteag kussiogkéhik8.
32.18 Kenáhtin womoausuonk muttannonganogkussuog, kah ummatcheseongan8oash 8sh8oh, kutonkquatantam ut upp8chenauóun8óut nahohtôeu wunneechan8oh, Masugkenuk, kah M[a]nuhkesit Manit, Jehovah ayeuteaunit ne 8wesuonk.
32.19 Noh missugken ut kogohqutteamwunneat, kah menuhkesu ut anakausuonganit, (newutche kuskesukquash woshwohtaash ut wame ummayeu[ou]t wunnaumonuh wosktompaog, aninnumauonat nishnoh pasuk neaunak ummayash, kah neanummeechumuk wutusseongash)
32.20 Noh ponuk kuhkinneasuongash kah monchanatam8ongash ut ohkit Egypt, pajeh yeu késukok, kah ut Israel kah kenugke onkatogig wosketompaog, kah k8wesuonganuhkau ku[h]hog, onatuh ne kesukok.
32.21 Kah kussohh8wun Israelle kummissinninnumog wutch Egypte ohkeit, nashpe kuhkinneasuongash, kah nonchanatam8ongash, kah nashpe menuhkiyeue menutcheg kah nashpe summagunnum8e muhpit, kah nashpe mishe wabesuonk.
32.22 Kah neg kittinnumau8og yeu ohke, ne chadchekeimop 8sh8oh kittinnumauónat, ohke ne tomogok sogkodtunk, kah hony.
32.23 Kah nag petutteaog, kah wutahtauunneau, qut nag matta n8swehtam8og k8wadtauatonkqussuonk, asuh pomushontam8og kuttinnaumatuonk, nag monteag usséog nean ann8nadt wutussenaout, newaj wame ne machuk nuhkunumauadt.
32.24 Kusseh, wadchukontamwog, nag peyaog keihtotanat sohkomunnaoont, kah keitotan magun wunnutchegan8out Coldeansog, neg ayeuuhkontogig, wutche togkodteg, kah mahshagquodt kah unninneaonk, kah uttoh an8waon n$nih, kah kusseh kenaumun.
32.25 Kah kutussip, woi Lord Jehovah, adtoash ohteuk wutch teagwash, kah wauwaenuog neemun: newutche keitotan magun en wunnutchegan8out Caldeansog.
32.26 Neit peyaonuk Jeremiah wuttinn8waonk Jehovah, n8wau,
32.27 Kusseh nen Jehovah um-Manitt8moh wame weyaus: sun ne teag nussioggehik?
32.28 Newutche yeu wussin Jehovah kusseh, yeu nummagun keitotan en wunnutchegan8wout Caldeansog, kah en wunnutcheganit Nebuchadnezzár Babilone ketass8t, kah noh pish wussohkomun.
32.29 Kah Caldeansog neg ayeuuhkontogig yeu keitotan, nag pish peyaog, kah pish chikohsumwog ne keitotan, kah chikohsumwog weetuomash nish ut woskeche sephamauwahetteup weetemungquok Baal, kah sokanumauw[á]hetteup wuttattamwe sephausuongash onkatogeh manittoh, m8m8sqhikqunnaoont.
32.30 Newutche wunnaumonuh Israel, kah wunnaumonuh Judah webe matcheseog ut anaquabeh wutch 8kenuunneaoont: newutche wunnaumonuh Israel webe numm8m8sqhikquog, nashpe wunnutchegane anakausuongan8, wussin Lord.
32.31 Newutche yeu keitotan nummusquantamwahikqun, kah nuppehchhikqun, wutch ne kesukok kezteauhettit, pajeh yeu kesukok, onk woh nutontahtauun wutch anaquabeh.
32.32 Wutche wame ummatchitt8m8 wunnaumonuh Israel, kah wunnaumonuh Judah, ne asehettit numm8m8sqhikqunnaout, nag, ukkehtass8tamóm8uh, wussontimom8uh, wussephausueneum8uh, kah ukquoshodtumwaeneum8uh, kah Judae wosketompaog kah wadohkitcheg Jerusalem.
32.33 Kah quinnuppinnumwog uppisquan8 en nuhhogkat, qut matta wuskesuk8, tôhkônogque nukkuhk8tomauóneau nompoáeu omohkéonish, kah kuhk8tomauog, qut o[n]ch matta n8tam8og attumunumunat kuhk8tomóadtuonk.
32.34 Qut nag ponamwog wunnishkeneunkquodt8m8, ne ahhettammuk nashpe n8wesuonk, nishketeauunat.
32.35 Kah nag ayimauáog qunúhqui ayeuongaṣh Baaloh, niṣh ut wut8nouhkôiyeumut wunnaumonuh Hinnom: wunnaumonáuh kah wuttaunoh pannupwusháheaog n8taut en Molechut, ne matta a[n]ann8náog, asuh matta paómun8g nuttenantam8onganit, nag woh yeu wutussenáout unkquanumukquok, matcheseáheónat Judah.
32.36 Kah yeu$yeu yeu$waj n8wadt Jehovah um-Manitt8moh Israel, papaume yeu keitotan, uttoh adt n8wáog, ne piṣh magun en wunnutcheganit Babylone ketass8t nashpe togkodteg, nashpe mohshagquodt kah nashpe enninneaonk.
32.37 Kusseh, nag nummukkinóog wutch wame wutohtimoneat, uttoh ann8hkauog musquanumog kah chenauosánumog, kah mishe musquantamon, kah wonk nuppas8óog yeu ayeuonganit, kah n8niyeuhéoog:
32.38 Kah nag piṣh nummissinninnúmog, kah nen um-Manitt8m8uh.
32.39 Kah nag nuttinnumauóog pasuk metah, kah pasuk may, onk woh nag nukqushhukquog micheme, wutche 8niyeuongan8, kah wunneechan8oh nahohtôeu.
32.40 Kah nutayimauoog machemohtag wunn8waonk, onk woh matta nukqushkehtauóog, n8neunneheonáóont, qut nupponum wuttahh8wout n8wabesuwónitteaonk onk woh nag mat nunnukkonuk8og.
32.41 Nux, nummuskouantamounóog n8neunneheonaóont, kah nag piṣh wunnamuhkut nutohteuhkonunk ut ohkeit, nashpe mamusse nuttah, kah mamusse nukketeahogkou.
32.42 Newutche yeu wussin Jehovah, neane nuhkunumauog yeug missinninnúog wame yeu mishe machuk, ne nuttinne paudtauóneau wame wanegik ne quoshómogkup.
32.43 Kah ohteuhkonash pish taphumunash yeu ohkeit, uttoh ad n8waog, tne touwushin, wanne wosketompaun8, asuh puppinashimun8, ne magun ut wunnutchegan8out Caldeansog.
32.44 Wosketómpaog pish adtoaog ohteuhkonash wutche teagwash, kah wussukhumwog wauwaongash, kah kuhkinneasukóntam8ongash, kah pish wauwaenuhteaog ut ohkeit Benjamin, kah ut ayeuonganehtu quinnuppe Jerusalem, kah ut Judae keitotanehtu, kah ut wadchae keitotanehtu, kah ut 8nouhkoiyeue keitotanehtu, kah ut sowanie keitotanehtu, newutche nukqushkeah missinoog wussin Jehovah.
33.1 NAno wuttinn8waonk Jehovah peyaonuk Jeremiah, nahohtoeu (ashpamu kuppuhhausit kuppishagkinittue chippinneutunkanit) n8wau,
33.2 Yeu wussin Jehovah noh kesteunk, Jehovah noh kahkenauwehteunk, ummenuhkehtinat, Jehovah ne 8wesuonk.
33.3 Wehkomeh, kah kenamp8hamoush, kah kukkuhk8tomoush mogagish kah mamenuhkagish, nish mo wahteau8anish.
33.4 Newutche yeu wussin Jehovah um-Manitt8moh Israel, papaume weetuomash yeu ut keitotanat, kah papaume week8oash Judae ketass8tamwog nish kepuhteamukish nashpe wadchuuhkontam8ongash, kah nashpe togkodteg.
33.5 Nag peyaog ayeuuhkononat Caldeansog, qut ne nashpe numwohtauóneau nupp8e muhhogkuh, neg nohshogeg nashpe nummusquanitteaonk, kah nashpe nutchenauausuonk, kah wutche wame yeuṣh matcheseongaṣh nupputtogguhhum nuskesuk wutch yeu keitotanat.
33.6 Kusseh, nuppaudtauwontamun pomantamóonk, kah neetskehuwaonk, kah nag nunneetskeheaog, kah n8wahteauwahéoog monat wunoht[é]aonk kah wanamuhkutéyeuuk.
33.7 Kah ummissinoóonk Judah ah ummissinoóonk Israel nukqushkeaheoog, kah nutogque wekitteahéoog weskeu.
33.8 Kah nuppahkhéoog wutch wame ummatcheseongan8óut, uttiyeu nashpe matchenéhehetteup, kah nutahquontamauóog wame ummatcheseongan8óaṣh, nish nashpe matchenehetticheh kah pannesehtiehetticheh.
33.9 Kah piṣh ut nuhhogkat wekonatmwe wesuonk, waeenomáonk kah quttiánittuonk ut wame anaquabhettit wutohtimoneunk ut ohkeit, neg n8togiṣh wame wanegik ne ánheog: kah nag piṣh wabesuog kah nunnuksháog wutche wame wanegik, kah wutche wame wunáyeuonk, ne ánteau.
33.10 Yeu wussin Jehovah, wonk piṣh n8tamun yeu$ut ayeuonganit (ne an8waog ne touwushin matta wosketompaun8, kah matta puppinashimun8, ut Judae keitotan[e]htu, kah Jerusalemme toumaogquehtu, nish touushikiṣh wanne wosketom[a]un8, wanne wutohkeit, wanne puppinashimun8.)
33.11 Muskouanatamwe wadtauatonkqussuonk, kah weekontamwe wadtauatonkqussuonk, 8wadtauatonkqussuonk weetauadteaénin, 8wadtauatonkqussuongan8 nag piṣh an8wacheg, tabuttantamok Jehôvah ayeuuhteaunit, newutche Jehov[a]h wunneetou, newutche ummonanitteaonk michemohteau, kah neg piṣh paudtunkeg tabuttantamoe sephausuonk ut wekit Jehovah: newutche nukqushkeáh ohkee missinoonk, neane wesku wussin Jehovah.
33.12 Yeu wussin Jehovah ayeuteaunit, wonk yeu$ut ayeuonganit, ne touushik matta wosketompaun8ut, kah mat puppinashimun8, kah ut wame niṣh keitotanehtu piṣh wutáyeuongan8 nanaushepsaenuog, sepsinn8waheog ut flocksum8uh.
33.13 Ut wadchu[é] keitotanahtu, ut 8nouhkoiyeue otanahtu, kah sowaniyeue otanahtu, kah ut wutohkit Benjamin, kah ut ayeuonganéhtu quinnuppe Jerusalem, kah ut Judae otanahtu flocksog piṣh wonk pámwushaog ut agwe wunnutcheganit noh agkemont, wussin Jehovah.
33.14 Kusseh, kesukodtaṣh peyom8aṣh, wussin Jehovah, nutussen ne wanegik ne quoshoái ut wekit Israel, kah ut wekit Judah.
33.15 Ut yeush kesukodtaṣh, kah na ahquompag, nunneetuwáht[ó]h ut wekit David sampweusseae Wuttuhk, kah noh piṣh usseu wussittumóonk kah sampweusseonk ut ohkeit.
33.16 Yeush ut kesukodtash Judah pish wadchanau, kah Jerusalem pish wadchanae wutayin, kah yeu pish ussowetamun, Jehovah nussampweusseonganun.
33.17 Newutche yeu wussin Jehovah, David matta pish quena[u]ahik8 wosketompuh quenapinutche Israelle weke appuonganit.
33.18 Kah sephausuenuog kah Levitsog matta pish quenauehikk8og wosketompuh ut anaquabeh, magunat chikohtae sephausuongash, kah nashqussumunat metsue sephausuongash kah nagwutteáe sephausinneat.
33.19 Kah wuttinn8waonk Jehovah peyaonuk Jeremiah n8wau,
33.20 Yeu wussin Jehovah pohquenumóg nukkesukodte wunn8waonk, kah nunnukkonae wunn8waonk, onk woh mo kesukodtino, kah nuhkonunn8, ut utt8cheyeu8ut.
33.21 Neit wonk woh n8n8waonganun David nuttinneum pohqunnumun, matta 8naumoniyeinat nanawunnuonat ut wuttappuonganit: kah n8n8waonganun Levitsog kah sephausuenuog nunohtompeantogomog.
33.22 Neane kesukque kenauwameonk woh mo wáogketamomuk, kah kehtahhunomuk matta woh waeu quttuhhum8un, ne nuttinne mishehteauun 8skannem David nuttinneum, káh Levitsog neg wowussumukqueaneg.
33.23 Nano wuttinn8waonk Jehovah peyaonuk Jeremiah, n8wau,
33.24 Sun matta kenatwontam8 yeug missinninnuog toh an8wahettit, n8wahettit, neesit teashiyeu8onk neh Jehovah pepenog, uppogkenuh? yeu wuttinne jishanumoneau nummissinninnumog onk woh matta wonk wutohtimoeinn8 ut anaquabhettit.
33.25 Yeu wussin Jehovah, tohneit kesukodae kah nukkonae n8n8waonk matta ohtan8g, kah mátta kuhquttum8on kesukque kah ohkee kuhquttum8ongash.
33.26 Neit nuppogketam 8skannem Jakob kah David nuttinneum, newaj matta noh wuttinnum8 8skannem, wunnanauwunnumunnaoont 8skannemuneoh Abraham Isaak, kah Jakob: newutche nukqushkeahto ummissinn8ongan8, kah nag nummonanumoog.
34.1 WUttinn8waonk ne pauonukqut Jeremiah wutch Jehovah$ut (Nebuchadnezzer Babilone ketass8t, kah wame ukkenauwameumoh kah wame ass8tam8ongash ut ohkeit, ut wunnanauúnnum8onganit, & wame missinninnuog ayeuuhkontamwog Jerusalem, & ayeuuhkonittue wame keitotanash na ohtagish) n8wau.
34.2 Yeu wussin Jehovah um-Manitt8moh Israel, monchish ken8s Zedechiah Judae ketass8t, kah us, yeu wussin Jehovah, kusseh; yeu nummagun keitotan en wunnutcheganit Babilone ketass8t, kah noh pish wutchikkossumun ut n8taut.
34.3 Kah ken matta pish kuppogquohham8 wutch wunnutcheganit: qut pish wunnamuhkut kuttohqunit, kah kuskesukquash pish naum wuskesukquash Babilone ketass8t, kah noh mutt8n8e kukken8nuk, kah pish kuttom Babilon.
34.4 Qut onch n8tash wuttinn8waonk Jehovah, woi Zedechiah Judae ketass8t: yeu wussin Lord papaume ken, matta pish kenupp8h, nashpe togkodteg.
34.5 Qut pish k8nohteae nup, kah nashpe wutchikkossum8ongan8oash k8sh8oog, negonne ketass8tamwog, neg negonnekunkqueaneg, ne pish kitt[t]nne chikkohsumunkquneau, kah nag pish kummauwemukquog n8wahettit woi Lord: newutche nukkutt8kontam kutt8onk wussin Jehovah.
34.6 Neit Jeremiah quoshodtumwaen, wuttinnonash wame yeush kutt8ongash Zedechiahoh Judae ketass8t ut Jerusalem.
34.7 Ukkenauwameonk Babilone ketass8t ayeuuhkontamunit Jerusalem, kah wame Judae keitotanash nish sequttahhamukish, Lachish kah Azekah: newutche yeush pummenutausue keitotanash ashpumohtáash wutch Judae keitotanat.
34.8 Yeu kutt8onk ne pauhonukup Jeremiah wutch Jehovah$ut, mahche Zedechiah wunn8wahettit wame missinninnuh neg, apitcheg Jerusalem, nag wahteauwahuonat chippinnu8onk.
34.9 Nish$noh wosketmp woh chippinnuwaheau wosketompae wuttinninneumoh Hebrewyeu8it kah nish$noh wosketomp mittamwussisse wuttinninneumoh Hebrewyeu8it, wanne howan 8chieinneat Jewsue wematoh.
34.10 Kah wame sontimoog, kah wame missinninnuog neg wán8wacheg n8tamwehettit, nish$noh wosketomp woh chippinnewah[é]au wosketompae wuttinninnumoh, kah nishnoh mittumwossisse wuttinninneumoh, matta woh wonk 8chienaoont, neit n8swehtámwog kah ummoncheaheuh.
34.11 Qut ompetak nag quinnuppeog kah ukqushkeaheóuh wuttinneum8ut kah ummaidum8uh neh chapinninnuwaheahetteupoh, kah wutagwapehheouh 8tinninneumunaóut.
34.12 Newaj wuttinn8waonk Jehovah peyaonukqut Jeremiah wutch Jehovah n8wau,
34.13 Yeu wussin Lord um$Manitt8moh Israel, n8n8waheomp k8sh8óog ne kesukok sohh8wunog wutch Egypte ohkeit, wutch missinnae-kommukqut nussip,
34.14 Wehqhshik nesausuk tahshe kodtumm8, nishnoh wosketomp moncheáheonch wemátoh Hebrewoh, noh kodtauwompámunuukkus: kah noh wuttinneumuhkonukquean nequtta tahshe kodtumwaeu, neit piṣh kutchippinninnuáh wutch kuhhogkat, qut k8sh8óog matta nukkeihketónk8, asuh nutáhchuwussittuonk8og.
34.15 Kuhquinnuppinitteamw8 yeuyeu, kah kutussemwop ne sampwag ut anaquabeh, wahteauwáhuwáóg chippinnú8onk nishnoh pasuk en weetatteamonganit, & k8n8wamwop ut anaquabeh, ut wetuomut ne áhettamuk nashpe n8wesuonk.
34.16 Qut kukquinnuppemw8, kah kenishketeomw8 n8wesuonk, kah kukqushkeáheomw8 nishnoh wosketomp wuttinneumoh, kah nishnoh wosketomp ummaidumoh, neg chappinninnuwáheógkuppanneg, uttoh án kodtantamwéhettit, kah kutagwapéhe[ó]óog, k8tinninneumunneaóut kah k8maidumunneaóont.
34.17 Newaj yeu n8wadt Lord, matta nukkehketi8mw8, wahteauwáhuónat chippinnú8onk, niṣhnoh pasuk weematoh, nishnoh pasuk wetatteamungoh: kusseh n8wahteauwáhuwam kutchippinninnu8ongan8 wussin Jehovah, en togkodteganit, en enneaonganit, kah en mahshogquodtut: kah kutontashinnumw8 en wame ass8tam8ongash ut ohkeit.
34.18 Kah wosketompaog neg panneusséhtunkeg n8n8waonk neg matta asegek wunn8wae kutt8wongash niṣh áyimukish ut anaquabeh, póhshiswáhettit calfoh, kah pannupwusháhettit ut nôeu chippaiyeuut.
34.19 Judae seontimoog, kah Jerusalemme sontimoog eunuchsog, kah sephausuenuog, kah wame missinninnúog ohkeit, neg pannupwushacheg nashaue calfe chippaiyeuut.
34.20 Neg nummagununk en wunnutchegan8out ummatwomoh, kah ut wunnutchegan8óut neg kodnushoncheg, kah nupp8e wuhhogkauh ne piṣh ummeetsuongan8 kesukque puppinshasog, kah ohkee puppinashimw[o]g.
34.21 Kah Zedechiah Judae ketass8t kah wussontimomoh, neg nummagununk ut wunnutchegan8out ummatwom8uh, kah ut wunnutchegan8óut neg kod nushoncheg, kah ut wunnutchegan8out ukkenauwameongan8 Babilone ketass8t, neg kuhkuhquecheg wutch kuhhogkaóut.
34.22 Kusseh, nag nutann8nóog, wussin Lord, kah nukqushkeaheóog yeu in otanat, kah nag piṣh wutayeuuhkontamuneau, kah piṣh wussohkomuneau, kah piṣh chikkossumuneau ut n8taut: kah Judae keitotanash nuttauwushitteauunash, matta wutohkeinneat.
35.1 WUttinn8waonk ne pauhónukqut Jeremiah wutch Jehovah, ut ukkesukodtumut Jehojakim wunnaumonuh Josiah Judae ketass8t n8wau,
35.2 Aush wekuout Rechabitsog, kah nag ken8s, kah nag petukos wekit Jehovah, ut pasuk chamberut, kah aninnumau wine wuttatumunat.
35.3 Neit nunnemunomp Jaazaniah wunnaumonuh Jeremiah, wunnaumonuh Habaziniah, kah weematoh, kah wame wunnaumonuh, kah mamusse wek8 Rechabitsog.
35.4 Kah nuppetukonóog wekit Jehovah, ut wutchamberum8out wunnaumonuh Hanan wunnaumonuh Igdaliah Manittowomp, ne ohtag kishke wutchamberum8out sontimóog, ne waabe wutchamberumut Maasejah wunnaumonuh Shallum nanasquontamaenin,
35.5 Kah nupponum anaquabhettit wunnaumonuh Rechabitse wetu, wishquahtu nanumwohteau wine, kah wuttattamwaitchuaṣh, kah nag nuttinnópanneg wuttattam8k wine.
35.6 Kah nag n8waog, matta n8tattam8mun wine: newutche Jonadab wunnaumonuh Rechab, nutann8nukqunnónup, n8wop, wuttattam8hteok wine kenaau asuh kenaumonáog micheme.
35.7 Weekitteáhteogk, kah ohketeáhteogk, kah weenominneohketeahteogk, kah ahque ohtau8k: qut [n]isohke|pomantamog ayék weetuomut, onk woh kussepepomantamumw8 ut ohkeit ne adt penuwohteayeóg.
35.8 Yeu nuttinne n8swetamunan 8wadtauatonkqussuonk Jonadab wunnaumonuh Rechab n8shun, wame neáne meechumuhkonukquéog, matta wuttattam8unat wine nisohke pomantamog, nenawun, nummittamwussinnonog, nunnaumonánonog, kah nuttaununónog.
35.9 Matta n8wékekongk8unnanónut, ayinneat, kah matta n8weenominneohtekoneumun, matta n8tohteuhkoneumun, asuh n8skennémunneumun.
35.10 Qut nut[á]yimun wetuómut, kah nunn8swehtamumun, kah n8wame ussénan ne Jonadab n8shun ánann8nukqueog.
35.11 Qut n$niyeup Nebuchadnezzar Babylone ketass8t kó[h]ku[h]quit yeu in ohkeit, nussi[m]unnonup, kah, ontuh Jerusalem, newutche n8wabesuóntamumun Syrianse kenauwameonk, kah Babylone kenauwameonk, ne$waj ayéog Jerusalem.
35.12 Neit wuttinn8waonk Jehovah peyaonuk Jeremiah, kah n8wau,
35.13 Yeu wussin Jehovah ayeuteaunit um-Manitt8moh Israel, monchish, us Judae wosketompaog, kah wadohkitcheg Jerusalem, sunnummatta kuttattumunumomw8 kuhk8tomwehteaonk n8tamunat nukkutt8wongaṣh, wussin Jehovah.
35.14 Wuttinn8waongash Jonadab wunnaumonuh Rechab, neanann8nomp wunnaumonuh matta wuttattam8unat wine, wutusseneau, newutche pajeh yeu kesukok matta wuttattam8og, qut n8wehtamwog 8sh8oh wutann8team8onk: qut kukken8numw8, nompoáeu omohkeon kah kodt8hkôon, qut matta kukkehketiyeúmw8.
35.15 Nutann8nop wonk en kuhhogkaóut wame nuttinninnumwog quoshodtumwaenuog, nompoáe omohkeon, kah nag ann8nog, nussip, yeuyeu qushkek nishnoh pasuk wutch ummatche mayut kah oncheteau8k kutusseongan8oaṣh, kah asuhkauúhteok onkatogig manitt8og nag wuttinneumuhkauónat, kah piṣh kutayimw8 ohkeit, ne anumauunóg, kah k8sh8wóog, qut matta kutahchuwussittam8mw8, asuh kukkeihketai8mw8.
35.16 Newutche wunnaumonuh Jonadab, wunnaumonuh Rechab, usseog wutann8team8onk 8sh8uh, ne ánann8nomp nahoh, qut yeug missinninnuog matta nukkehketunk8og.
35.17 Newaj yeu n8wadt Jehovah ayeuhteaunit um-Manitt8moh Israel, kusseh, nunnuhkinnumauôog Judah kah wame wadohkitcheg Jerusalem, wame machuk ne ayeuuhkone áne ken8nog: newutche nag nukken8nóog, qut nag matta n8tam8og, kah nag n8wehkomóog, qut namp8hamunk8og.
35.18 Kah Jeremiah unnop wek8 Rechabitsog, yeu wussin Jehovah ayeuteaunit um-Manitt8moh Israel, newutche ken8swehtamumw8 wutann8team8onk Jonadab k8shw8, kah kenanawehteomw8 wame ukkuhk8waongaṣh, kah kutussemw8 wame neánan8nukqueóg.
35.19 Newajeh yeu n8wadt Jehovah ayeuteaunit um-Manitt8moh Israel, Jonadab wunnaumonuh Rechab matta piṣh quenanéhik8 wosketompuh nepauinneat anaquabeh micheme.
36.1 KAh nniyeup ut weyaue kodtum8mut Jehojakim wunnaumonuh Josiah Judae ketass8t, yeu kutt8onk uppeyaónukqun Jeremiah wutch Jehovahut, n8wau,
36.2 Nemunumush tuttuppequia[n]ôsuwu b8k, kah ne ut wawawussukwhuṣh, kutt8wongash nish ayeuuhkonittue ânogish Israel, kah Judah, kah wame wutohtimoneaṣh, wutch ne kesukok kôn8nunon, wutch ukkesukkodtumut Josiah pajeh yeu kesukok.
36.3 Pagwodche wek Judah woh n8tam wame machuk ne kod néhheog, onk woh nag qushkeog nishnoh pasuk wutch ummatche mayut onk woh nutahquontam ummatcheseongan8, kah uppanneseongan8.
36.4 Neit Jeremiah wehkomau Baruchoh wunnaumonuh Neriah, kah Baruch wussuhkhum wutch wutt8nut Jeremiah, wame ukkutt8wongaṣh Jehovah, nish ánompaṣh, ut tuttuppequanausue b8kut.
36.5 Kah Jeremiah ann8nau Baruchoh, n8wau, nukkuphaus, matta woh nutóh weekit Jehovah.
36.6 Newutche monchish, kah ogketash ut tuttuppequanausuut ne wásuhkuhhuman wutch nutt8nut, ukkutt8wongash Jehovah ut wu[h]tauogk8out missinninnuog, ut wekit Jehovah, ut matta meetsue kesukkodtut: kah niṣh piṣh wonk kutogketmunash, ut wame wuhtauogk8óut Judah neg sohhogeg wutch wutotanaóut.
36.7 Pâguodcheh piṣh ponamwog uppeantam8ongan8 ut anaquabit Jehovah, kah piṣh qushkeog nishnoh pasuk wutch ummatche mayut, newutche missi ummusquanittam8onk kah wutchenauausuonk ne Jehov[a]h kôn8tog ayeuuhkonittue yeuh missinninnúh.
36.8 Kah Baruch wunnaumonuh Neriah wutussen neane wame ne Jeremiah quoshodtumwaen ánann8nont, ogketamup ut b8kut wuttinn8waongash Jehovah, ut Jehovah wekit.
36.9 Kah nniyeup napanna wutteashe kodtum8mut Jehoiakim wunnaumonuh Josiah Judae ketass8t, ut pasuk8gun adtas8it nepauz, nag wahteauwáhuwaog mat meetsuonk ut anaquabit Jehovah wutch wame missinninnúog ut Jerusalem, kah wutch wame missinninnúog neg wagig Judae keitotanahtu en Jerusalem.
36.10 Neit Baruch ogketamup b8k, ukkutt8wongash Jeremiah ut wekit Jehovah, ut wutchambarumut Gemariah wunnaumonuh Shaphan noh scribe, ut qunnunkquohtag chippinnutunkanit, ahhut petutteamuk wuske squontamut wekit Jehvoah, ut wuhtauogk8óut wame missinninnúog.
36.11 Michajah wunnaumonuh Gemariah, wunnaumonuh Shaphan, n8tog wutch b8kut [vv]ame [vv]uttinn8[vv]aongash Jehovah.
36.12 Neit w8msu en ketass8t weekit, ut wut-chamberumut Scribe, kah kusseh wame sontimóog na wutappinneau, Elishama noh Scribe, kah Del[a]jah wunnaumonuh Shemajah, kah Elnathan wunnaumonuh Achbor, kah Gemariah wunnaumonuh Shaphan, kah Zedekiah wunnaumonuh Hananiah, kah wame sontimóog.
36.13 Neit Michajah na 8wahteauwâhuun wame kutt8wongaṣh nish n8togish: Baruch ágkeetog b8k ut wuhtauogk8óut missinninnúog.
36.14 Newaj wame sontimóog negont8waog Jehudi wunnaumonuh Nethaniah, wunnaumonuh Shelemiah, wunnaumonuh Cushi en Baruch$ut n8waog, nemunuṣh ut kenutcheg[a]nit tuttuppéquianaúsik ne agketaman ut wuhtauogk8[ó]ut missinninnuog, kah peyauṣh; neit Baruch wunnaumonuh Neriah nemunum wuttuppequianaúsik ut wunnutcheganit, kah nah uppeyaonuh.
36.15 Kah nah wuttinóuh nummatappish, kah ogketaṣh ut nehtauogkinnónut.
36.16 Kah n$nih n8tamwehettit wame kutt8wongaṣh wabesuog nishnoh pasuk, kah nag unnaog Baruchoh, wunnamuhkut nuttinnonnánonaṣh ketass8t wame yeush kutt8wongaṣh.
