36.17 Kah nag nat8tomauáog Baruchoh, n8waog, ussunan yeuyeu, uttoh kuttin wussukhumunas wame yeush kutt8wongaṣh ut wutt8nut?
36.18 Neit Baruch wunnamp8hamauoh, yeush wame kutt8wongaṣh nuttugqunaṣh nashpe wutt8n, kah niṣh n8sukkuhhumunaṣh nashpe ink ut b8kut.
36.19 Neit sontimóog unnáog Baruchoh, puttogquesh, ken kah Jeremiah, kah howan wahteau8hkitch ut$toh apeóg.
36.20 Kah petutteaunaog ketass8toh, ut mishe-komukqut, qut ponamwog tuttuppequayânôsik ut wut[-]chamberumut Elishama noh Scribe, kah wussinnaoaṣh wame kutt8wongaṣh ut wuhtauogkut ketass8t.
36.21 Neit ketass8t ann8nau Jehudi neemskomunat tuttuppequianaúsik; kah wunnemunnumun wutch wut-chamberumut Elishama noh Scribe, kah Jehudi wutogketamun ut wehtauogut ketass8t, kah wame wehtauogk8óut sontimóog neg kéhchekompauwéhtauoncheg ketass8toh.
36.22 Kah ketass8t appu popone-komukqut, ut pasuk8gun adtahs8it nepauz, kah na n8tau ut ahohtag n8tau chikohteau, ut anaquabit.
36.23 Kah n$nih Jehudi agketog shuoh asuh yauoh wunnepagwoh, w[u]ttummussumun nashpe méqunéhquog, kah wuttinnúhkon n8taut, ne ut ahohtag n8teau, nô pajeh mamusse tuttuppéquianuk mahchikuttaut, ut n8taut ne ahhohtag n8teau.
36.24 Qut matta wabesuog asuh nehnekikkom8og wutohtk8un8aṣh, matta ketass8t asuh howae wuttinneumoh n8taminnit wame yeush kutt8wongaṣh.
36.25 Qut onch Elnathan, kah Delajah, kah Gemariah wehquetumauópanneg ketass8toh matta wutchikkossum8unat tuttuppequiánunk, qut nah mat wunn8tauoh.
36.26 Qut ketass8t ann8team8 Jerahmeel wunnaumonuh Hammelech, kah Serajah wunnaumonuh Azriel, kah Shelemiah wunnaumonuh Abdiel, tohqunnónat Baruch noh Scribe, kah Jeremiah quoshodtumwaen: qut Jehovah wutadtahshuh.
36.27 Neit wuttinn8waonk Jehovah peyaonuk Jermiah, (mahche ketass8t chikkohsuk tuttuppéquianaúsik kah kutt8wongaṣh nish Baruch wasukk8hukupaṣh ut wutt8nut Jeremiah) n8wau,
36.28 Nemunush wonk onkatuk tuttuppéquianausik, kah tanúhsukkuhwhush wame negonne kutt8wongaṣh nish ohtagkupaṣh negonne tuttuppéquianausik, ne Jehojakim Judae ketass8t châgkossik.
36.29 Kah piṣh kuttin Jehojakim Judae ketass8t, yeu wussin Jehovah yeu kutchikkossumunáh tuttuppèquianaúsik kussip, tohwhutch na$ut wussukhuman, Babylone ketass8t pish wunnamuhkut peyau, kah piṣh yeu pagwadtauun ohke, kah piṣh wohkukquôsumau na wutch wosketompoh kah puppinashimwoh?
36.30 Newutche yeu wussin Jehovah papaume Jehojakim Judae ketass8t, matta pish wadchanóon howane appinneat wutappuonganit David, kah nupp8e wuhhogkuh piṣh sohwhôkauónuh ut kussittae kesukodtut, kah ut t8hpue nuhkonut.
36.31 Kah noh piṣh nussasamatoh kah 8skannemunneoh, kah wuttinneumoh, wutch ummatcheseongan8, kah nunnuhkinnumauóog, kah ut wadohkitcheg Jerusalem, kah ut Judae wosketompaut, wame machuk ne ayeuuhkonittue únnog: qut matta kukkeihtam8og.
36.32 Neit Jehovah onkatog nemunum tuttuppéquianaúsik, kah wuttinnumauoh Baruchoh noh Scribe wunnaumonuh Neriah, kah na wuttit wussukhumun wutch wutt8nut Jeremiah, wame b8ke kutt8wongaṣh niṣh Jehojakim Judae ketass8t châgossukupash ut n8taut, kah naut k8tnéhteauunash onkatogaṣh monaash kutt8wongaṣh neyaneyeu8gish.
37.1 KAh ketass8t Zedekiah wunnaumonuh Josiah nompinau Coniahoh wunnaumonuh Jehojakim, neh Nebuchadnezzar Babylone ketass8t kóhtahs8tamwéhteóhpoh ut Judae ohkeit.
37.2 Qut matta nagum asuh wuttinneumoh, asuh ne ohkee missinninnuog kuhkeitamóog wuttinn8waongash Jehovah, nish án8wopash nashpe Jeremiah quoshodtumwaen.
37.3 Kah Zedekiah ketass8t an8team8 Jehucal wunnaumonuh Shelemiah, kah Zephaniah wunnaumonuh Maasejah sephausuaen, en Jeremiahut quoshodtumwaen, n8wop, yeuyeu peantamwanshinnean en Lord num-Manitt8munónut.
37.4 Kah Jeremiah petutteau, kah sohham ut kenugke missinninnútu: newutche nag matta ukkupshagkinóuh.
37.5 Neit Pharaoh ukkenauwameumoh sohhamwop wutch Egypt: kah Caldeansog neg weenuhkogig Jerusalem n8tamwehettit unaunchem8k[o]naongan8, nag nukkodtumwog Jerusalem.
37.6 Neit wuttinnw8aonk Jehovah peyaónuk Jeremiah quoshodtumwaen, n8wau,
37.7 Yeu wussin Jehovah um-Manitt8m8oh Israel, yeu piṣh kuttinnoneau Judae ketass8t noh an8nukquéog en nuhhogkat, nat8tamonteanat, kusseh, ukkenauwameonk Pharaoh ne sohham8m8uk kutann8munkqunnaóut, piṣh qushkeog en Egypt nehenwonche wutohtuóut.
37.8 Kah Caldeansog piṣh wonk peyaog, kah piṣh ayeuuhkontámwog yeu keitotan, kah piṣh wussohkomuneau, kah piṣh wutchikkossumuneau.
37.9 Yeu wussin Jehovah, as8kekomuhteógk kuhhogkaóog, n8wáog, Caldeansog piṣh wunnamuhkut nunnukkonukqunnónog: newutche nag matta piṣh moncheog.
37.10 Tôhkônogque kuttogkomonáoh mamusse Caldeanse kenauwameonk, ne ayeuuhkonukqueógig, kah webe squsháhettis n8chumwehtahwhutcheg missinninnúog ut kenugke nagoh, qut onch nag woh neepóog nishnoh pasuk ut wekit, kah piṣh chikohsumwog yeu keitotan nashpe n8tau.
37.11 Kah n$nihyeup ukkenauwameongan8 Caldeansog neepauwehettit wutch anaquohtag Jerusalem, quhtamunat ukkenauwameonk Pharaoh.
37.12 Neit Jeremiah sohham wutch Jerusalem, ônat wutohkeit Benjamin, na$wutch chippeinat ut nashaue missinninnútu.
37.13 Kah apit 8squontamut Benjamin, askuhwheteae mugquomp na wutappináh, noh ussoweu Irijah wunnaumonuh Shelemiah, wunnaumonuh Hananiah, kah tohqunau Jeremiahoh quoshodtumwaénuh, n8wau, kutontsehtau Caldeansog.
37.14 Neit Jeremiah n8wau, ne pann8waonk, matta nutontsehtauoh, Caldeansog, qut matta ukkehketauoh: neit Irijah tohqunau Jeremiah kah uppas8uh sontimmouhtu.
37.15 Newaj sontimoog musquanumaog Jeremiahoh, kah wuttogkomouh, kah ukkupshagkinau, ut wekit Jonathan noh Scribe, newutche ne ukkupshagkinegonuhkoneau.
37.16 Jeremiah petuttead[t] pohkenaekomukqut, kah wonogquehtu, & Jeremiah na m8chetikqunohteadt,
37.17 Neit Zedechiah ketass8t ann8team8 & uppohquohshagkunuh; & ketass8t ukkeme nat8tomauoh ut wékit, kah n8wop, sun ne teagwe kutt8onk wutch Jehovahut? kah Jeremiah n8wau, ohtau, newutche n8wau, ken pish kupponit ut wunnutcheganit Babylone ketass8t.
37.18 Nano Jeremiah unnau ketass8toh Zedechiahhoh, toh kittinne matchenehesh, asuh kittinneumog, asuh yeug missinninnuog, waj kuppishagkinneog?
37.19 Uttiyeug kukquoshodtumwaeneumog, neg quoshodtumunkqueaneg, n8wahettit, Babylone ketass8t matta pish kutayeuuhkonuk8 asuh yeu ohke.
37.20 Newutch yeuyeu n8tash k8wehquetumoush, woi nul$Lordum ketass8t, nunnanumpanwaonk tapeneaumunach ut anaquabean k8wehquetumoush, onk woh mo kukqushkeahheu en wekit Jonathan noh Scribe, ishkont ná nuttit nuppun.
37.21 Neit Zedechiah ketass8t ann8team8 woh pononat Jeremiah kuppishagkinnittue chippinneutunganit, kah asekesukokish woh wutassamonaoont kodchuhki petukqunnunk wutch wuttaumaogkumut petukqununganehteaenuog, nô pajeh wame petukquneg keitotanat mahtshunk yeu wuttinne Jeremiah appin kuppishagkinnittue chippinneutunganit.
38.1 NEit Shephatiah wunnaumonuh Mattan kah Gedaliah wunnaumonuh Pashur kah J[u]cal wunnaumonuh Shelemiah kah Pashur wunnaumonuh Malchiah, nag n8tamw[ô]g kutt8wongash nish Jeremiah an8wajish en wame missinninnuut, n8wau,
38.2 Yeu wussin Jehovah, noh yeu apit keitotanat, pish nup nashpe togkodteg, nashpe mahshagquodt, kah nashpe enninneaonk, qut noh sohhog en Caldeansut pish pomantam: newutche noh pish ohto uppomantamoonk wutch toh an tohqunuk, kah pish pomantam.
38.3 Yeu wussin Jehovah, yeu keitotan pish wunnamuhkut magun en wunnutchegan8out Babylone ketass8t ukkenauwameonk, neg pish sohhogig
38.4 Newaj sontimoog unnahettit ketass8toh, k8wehquetumauunumun yeuoh wosketomp nushunach: newutche yeu wuttiñe n8chumwehteauun wunnutchegan8oash ayeuhteaenuog neg apitcheg yeu otanat, kah wunnutcheganooash wame missinninnuog, nish anont kutt8wongash newutche yeuoh wosketomp matta natinneham8 8niyeuongan8 yeug missinninnuog, qut woskehuonat.
38.5 Neit Zedechiah kétass8t n8wau, kusseh noh appu kenutchegan8out, newutche ketass8t matta woh toh kuttin wuttamhik8.
38.6 Neit nag nemunaog Jeremiahoh, kah wuttinuhkonauh ut uppohkononogk8mut Malchiah wunnaumonuh Hammelech, ne [ó]htag kuppishagkinnittue chippinnutonganit, kah n8kompanaog Jeremiahoh nashpe pemuneahtonash: kah ut pohkenonogque matta nippen8, qut pisseogquanu8: neit Jeremiah quttaueu ut pisseogqu[a]nit.
38.7 Neit Ebedmelech wut-Ethiopian, pasuk euneuch ut ketass8t wekit, n8tog nag ponaog Jeremiahoh pohkinnaonogqut (ketass8t neit apit ut Benjamine squontamut.)
38.8 Ebedmelech sohham wutch wekit ketass8t kah ken8nau ketass8toh n8wau,
38.9 Nul$Lordum ketass8t yeug wosketompaog matche usseog wame ne anheahettit Jeremiahhoh quoshodtumwaenuh neh pánonteahetticheh en pohkinonogqut, kah noh nahen paskanontam ut ayeuonganit ne ayit, newutche matta wonk petukqununganun8 ut keitotanat.
38.10 Neit ketass8t ann8nau Ebedmelech wut-Ethiopian, n8wau, neemun yeu wutch nishwinchahkodtog wosketompaog, kah kuhkuhquin, Jeremiah quoshodtumwaenin wutch pohkenónog[p]ut, ash na nupp8kup.
38.11 Neit Ebedmelech neemunau wosketompuh, kah petutteau wekit ketass8t ut agwe nompak8unnekomukqut, kah na 8tinnumun nukkononákinaṣh, kah nukkonéwhiash, kah niṣh uppinnompánumaú[o]náoaṣh nashpe pemunneahtonaṣh en pohkinónogqut en Jeremiahut.
38.12 Kah Ebedmelech wut-Ethiopian unnau Jeremiahoh, ponsh yeuyeu yeush nukkononakinash, kah nukkonéhwhiaṣh agwe kenukqueit agwe pemuneohtonit, kah Jeremiah ne wutussen.
38.13 Neit kuhkuhqu[n]aoh Jeremiah nashpe pemuneohtanash, kah nag wunneemun[o]uh wutch pohkinónogqut, kah Jeremiah appu kuppishagkinnittue chippinnutunkanit.
38.14 Neit Zedekiah ketass8t ann8team8, kah nemunumau, Jeremiahoh quoshodtumwanúh, ut nashwunnú8k ahhut petutteamuk Jehovah wekit, kah ketass8t unnau Jeremiahoh, kenat8tomouṣh ne teag adtahtiéhkon ne teag.
38.15 Neit Jeremiah unnau Zedekiahoh, wahteauwahunon sunnummatta woh wunnamuhkut kenusheu? kah kogkuhtimunon, sunnummatta woh kukkehketiyeu?
38.16 Neit ketass8t kemu chadchekéimoh Jeremiahoh, n8wau, pomantog Jehovah noh ayimukquean yeuh keteahogkôunoh, matta kenushin8h, asuh matta nummag8 kuhhog en wunnutchegan8wóut yeug woskeompaog kod nushhukqueaneg.
38.17 Neit Jeremiah unnau Zedekiahoh, yeu wussin Jehovah um-Manitt8m8oh ayeuteaog, um-Manitt8m8oh Isr[à]el, tohneit wunnamuhkut sohhaman en wussontim[ô]mut Babylone ketass8t, neit kukketeahogkou piṣh pomantam, kah yeu keitotan matta piṣh chikohtano n8taut, kah piṣh ken kuppomantam, kah kek.
38.18 Qut matta sohham8an en wussontimómut Babylone ketass8t, neit piṣh yeu keitotan magun en wunnutchegan8óut Caldeansog, kah nag piṣh wutchi[k]kossùmuneau ut n8taut, kah matta piṣh kuppohquohham8 wutch wunnutchegan8out.
38.19 Kah Zedekiah ketass8t unnau Jeremiahoh, n8wabesuon Jewsog neg anogquehcheg Caldeansog, ishkont nag nupponukquog wunnutchegan8óut Caldeansog, kah nuttôontohkônukquog.
38.20 Qut Jeremiah n8wau, nag matta piṣh magwog kuhhog, n8swetaṣh k8wehquetumoush 8wadtauatonkqussuonk Lord, ne ânun: neit piṣh k8nihukqun, kah kukketeahogkou piṣh pomantam.
38.21 Qut sekeneaman sohhamun, yeu kutt8onk ne Jehovah nahtussit.
38.22 Kah kusseh, wame mittamwussissog sekqshoncheg ut Judae ketass8t wekit piṣh sohh8wunóog ut wussontimóm8ut Bablyone ketass8t, kah yeug piṣh n8waog, keetompaog kukkitchittôusháhikquog, kah kussohkunkquog, kusseetash quttauushauṣh ut pissagquanit, kah nag qushkeog.
38.23 Neit nag piṣh sohh8wunaog wame kummittamwussoh kah kummukkiésumoh en Caldeansut, kah matta piṣh kuppohquohham8 wutch wunnutchegan8out, qut piṣh ken kuttohqunit nashpe wunnutcheg Babylone ketass8t: kah yeu piṣh kutchikkossumwáhtauun keitotan ut n8taut.
38.24 Neit Zedekiah unnau Jeremiahoh, howan wohteau8hkitch yeush kutt8wongaṣh kah matta piṣh kenupp8.
38.25 Qut sontimóog n8tamwehettit kukkeket8hkouṣh, kah nag peyaonukquean, kah unnukquean, wahteauwáhenan uttoh âun adt ketass8t: ahque adtohtaiinnean, kah matta kenushin8mun, kah wonk toh ánukquean ketass8t.
38.26 Neit nag piṣh kuttinnóog, nupponamup n8wehquetum8onk anaquabit ketass8t, woh mo nukqushkeáhik8unat en [J]onathan wekit naut nuppunat.
38.27 Neit wame sontimóog peyaonóog Jeremiahoh, kah nag wunat8tomauóuh, kah wuttinónash wame niṣh neaunak ketass8t ánann8nont: neit wutahque keket8hkauóuh, newutche matta wahsham8 ne teag.
38.28 Neit Jeremiah appu kuppishagkinittue chippinnutunkanit pajeh nâ kesukok Jerusalem sohkomuk, kah na wutappineah Jerusalem sohkomuk.
39.1 PAsuk8gun wutteashe kodtum8muk Zedekiah Judae ketass8t, ut piogqussit nepauz, Nebuchádrezzar Babylone ketass8t, kah wame ukkenauwameónk ayeuuhkonittue peyaontamwog Jerusalem, kah nag 8wéenuhkomuneau.
39.2 Nabowunnukqutte kodtum8mit Zedekiah, ut yaue nepauzsaut, kah pasuk8gun adtashikqunohhog, keitotan pokqsheau.
39.3 Kah wame wussontimom[ô]h Babylone ketass8t petutteaog, kah appuog nasha[ú]e usquontamut, Nergal-Sharezer, Samger-Nebo, Sarsechim, Rabsaris, Nergal-Sharezer, Rabmag, kah wame onkatogig Babylone ketass8t wussontimómoh.
39.4 Kah n$nih[,] Zedekiah Judae ketass8t noh nauont, kah wame ayeuhteénúh, neit nag wussem8og, kah sohhamwog wutch [ó]tanat nukkonáeu, en may$ut ne kishke ketass8t tanohketeaonganit, en squontamut ut nashaue neese qussukquaneuntunkanit, kah en sohham mukoshquttae may$ut.
39.5 Qut Caldeansog ukkenauwameongan8 nah wunn8swuttahwhóuh, kah mattanáog Zedekiahoh ut Jerichoe mukoshquttaut, k[á]h tohqunáhettit, nag uppas8óuh Nebuchadnezzarut Babylone ketass8t ut Riblah ut ohkeit Hamath, uttoh adt wussumomp.
39.6 Neit Babylone ketass8t nushau wunnaumonuh Zedekiah ut anaquabit, ut Riblah, kah wonk Babylone ketass8t nushau wame Judae sontimuh.
39.7 Nano, skojkesukquánau Zedekiahoh, kah wutáhtogkuppanuh chainsaṣh wutuss8unónat Babylon.
39.8 Kah Caldeansog chikkossumwog ketass8t wek, kah wek8oash missinninnuwog ut n8taut, kah n8konteaog Jerusaleme pummeneutunk.
39.9 Neit Nebuzaradan askuhwheteáe mugquomp missinóhteau ashqshoncheg missinninnuog, neg apitcheg keitotanat, kah yeug amaéhcheg, ummosogquéhtunkquoh, kah onkatogig missinninnuog neg ashqshoncheg.
39.10 Qut Nebuzaradan askuhwheteáe mugquomp nukkonau matchekue missinninnúh neg monteag ohtau8gig ut ohkeit Judah, kah nah wuttinnumauoh weenominneohtekonaṣh kah ohteukonash ne nan ahquompág.
39.11 Kah Nebuchanezzar ketass8t ann8nau papaume Jeremiah, Nebuzaradan askuhwhetae mugquomp, n8wau,
39.12 Nemun kah wunádchan, kah woskeheúhkon, qut unneh ne woh ánukquean.
39.13 Neit Nebuzaradan askuhwhetae mugquomp, ann8team8, kah Nebushazban, Rabsaris, kah Nergal-Sh[a]rezer, Rabmag, kah wame wussontimómuh Babylone ketass8t.
39.14 Nag ann8team8og kah neemunoog Jeremiahoh wutch kuppishagkinnittue chippinnutunkanit, kah wutáhtashónuh ut Gedaliah wunnaumonuh Ahikam, wunnaumonuh Shaphan, woh nummonchanónat en weekit, neit weechayeumau missinninnúh.
39.15 Neit wuttinn8waonk Jehovah peyaónuk Jeremiah ash kophâusit kuppishagkinnittue chippinnútunkanit, n8wau,
39.16 Monchish ken8s Ebedmelech wut-Ethiopian, n8wash, yeu wussin Jehovah ayeuhteaunit, um-Manitt8moh Israel, kusseh, nunnuhkinnumau nuttinn8waongaṣh yeuoh keitotan, wutche machuk kah matta wanegik, kah nish pish pakodche n$niyeuash ut anaquabean.
39.17 Qut kupppohquohwhunush ne kesukok wussin Jehovah, kah matta pish kupponitteoh wunnutchegan8óut yeug wosketompaog quoshadcheg.
39.18 Newutche wunnamuhkut kuppohquohwhunush, kah matta piṣh kuppenushoh n[a]shpe togkodteg, qut pish kuppomantam 8w[o]ntam kuttohqunnum8onk, newutche kuppabuhtanumeh wussin Jehovah.
40.1 WUttinn8wank ne pauhónukqut Jeremiah wutch Jehovahut, mahche Nebuzaradan askuhwhetae mugquomp moncheáheont wutch Ramath, noh nemunont tohtogkuppissit chainsaṣh, ut kenugke wame neg masinohteamukeg wutch Jerusalem kah Judah, nag masinohteamukeg en Babylon.
40.2 Kah askuhwheteae mugquomp nemunau Jeremiahoh, kah wuttinuh, Lord kum-Manitt8m matche ken8tam ne machuk yeu ut ayeuonganit.
40.3 Yeuyeu Jehovah uppaudtauun, kah wutussen ne an8wop: newutche kummatcheneheomw8 Jehovah, kah matta ken8swehtam8mw8 8wadtauatonkqussuonk, newaj yeu nuhkuhkongqueóg.
40.4 Kah yeuyeu kusseh, kutompenush yeu kesukok wutch chainsash ohtagish kenutcheganit; wekontaman k8weechaiinneat Babylon, peyaush, kah k8ne nanauwuhhesh; qut matta wekontam8an k8weechaiinneat en Babylon, ne nohtaj: kusseh wame ohke anaquabean; uttoh wekontaman ónat ne âush.
40.5 Kah asquam quashkeit, n8wop, qushkish wonk en Gedaliahut wunnaumonuh Ahikam, wunnaumonuh Shaphan, neh Babylone ketass8t nanawunumwaheumpoh wame Judae keitotanash, kah noh weetom ut kenugke missinninnuog: asuh aush uttoh an tapeneaman ônat neit askuhwheteae mugquomp wuttinnumauoh m[é]echum, kah onkquatunk, kah ummoncheaheuh.
40.6 Neit Jeremiah âonau Gedaliahoh wunnaumonuh Ahikam en Mizpah, & 8weetomuh ut kenugke missininnuh neg asqunutcheg ut ohkeit.
40.7 Neit wame kenauwamee mukquompaog ut ohteuhkontu, nag kah 8wosketomp8m8uh, n8tamohettit Babylone ketass8t nanawunnumwaheau Gedaliahoh wunnaumonuh Ahikam, ut ohkeit: & wutahtohshuh wosketompoh, kah mittamwussissoh kah mukkiesoh, madchekitcheg ut óhkeit, neg sequnutcheg wutche ma[u]nohteamukeg ut Bablyon;
40.8 Neit nag peyaonaog Gedaliahoh ut Mizpah, Ishmael wunnaumonuh Nethaniah, & Johanan kah Jonathan wunnaumonuh Kareah, & Serajah wunnaumonuh Tanhumeth; & wunnaumonuh Ephai, wut-Netophathite[,] kah Jezaniah wunnaumonuh wut-Maachathite, nag kah 8wosketompom8uh,
40.9 Kah Gedaliah wunnaumonuh Ahikam, wunnaumonuh Shaphan, nah wutchadchekeimuh, kah wuttinninneum8uh, n8wau, wabesehteok k8tinninneumuhkauonaoont Caldeansog: wutohkek yeu ohkeit, kah wuttinninneumuhkok Babylone ketass8t, & pish k8niyeuwontamuneau.
40.10 Kah nen, kusseh, nuttai Mizpah wuttinninneumuhkauonat Caldeansog, neg pish páuh[ó]nukqueagig: qut kenaau mauinne[á]k wine, kah neepunné meechummuongash kah pummee, kah nish ponam8k k8wishquaout kah ayek kukkeitotanahtu, nish attumunumogish.
40.11 Nano wame Jewsog ut Moab, kah kenugke Ammonitsog, kah ut Edom, & neg ayitcheg wame ohkeit, nag n8tamwehettit Babylone ketass8t, sequnau Judae sequnutcheg, kah nanawunnumwaheau Gedaliahoh wunnaumonuh Ahikam wunnaumonuh Shaphan.
40.12 Wame Jewsog qushkeog wutch wame ayeuonganehtu uttoh an8kauuttus, kah nag peyaog Judae ohkeit, en Gedaliahut, en Mizpah, kah nag mukkinnumwog wine, kah neepunne meechummuongash m8naash.
40.13 Nano, Johanan wunnaumonuh Kareah, kah wame kenauwamee mugquompaog ut ohteuhkontu, nag peyaonaog Gedaliahoh ut Mizpah.
40.14 Kah wuttinuh, sun kuppahke wahteoh, Baal Ammonitse ketass8t, ann8nau Ishmaeloh wunnaumonuh Nethaniah kenushikqunat qut Geadliah wúnnaumonuh Ahika matta wunnamptauoh.
40.15 Neit Johanan wunnaumonuh Kareah, keme ken8nau Gedaliahoh ut Mizpah, n8wau, k8wehquetumoush moncheti, kah nunnush Ishmael wunnaumonuh Nethaniah, kah matta howan pish 8wahteau8un, tohwutch woh noh nushikquean, neg wame Jewsog miaehtunkquéaneg, woh noswaiyeuog, kah yeug sequnutcheg ut Judah woh pagwanoog.
40.16 Qut Gedaliah wunnaumonuh Ahikam, unnau Johananoh wunnaumonuh Kareah, matta yeu pish kutussein, newutche kuppann8wáh Ishmael.
41.1 KAh n$nih, ut nesausuk adtahs8it nepauz, Ishmael, wunnaumonuh Nethaniah wunnaumonuh Elishamah, ketass8tamwe wuskannem, kah wussontimausoh ketass8t piogqussuoh woskeotmpuh weechog, peyaonog Gedaliahoh wunnaumonuh Ahikam ut Mizpah, kah na meechwog petukqunneg ut Mizpah.
41.2 Neit Ishmael wunnaumonuh Nethaniah kah piogqussuh wosketompuh weechogqutcheh neepoog, kah togkomaog Gedaliahoh wunnaumonuh Ahikam wunnaumonuh Shaphan nashpe togkodteg, kah wunnushouh, neh Babylone ketass8t nanawunnumwaheompoh ut ohkeit.
41.3 Ishmael wonk nushau wame Jewsoh, neh weechayeumumpoh, weeche Gedaliah ut Mizpah, kah Caldeansog neg na apitcheg, kah ayeuhteaenuog.
41.4 Kah n$niyeup, nahohtôeu kesukok mahche nushit Gedaliah, k[á]h matta howan 8wahteauouun.
41.5 Na 8muneau nawhutche wutch Shechem, wutch Shiloh, kah wutch Samaria, shwosuk tahshinchagkodtog, m8sôsik 8weeshitt8un8òash, wuthogk8un8ash nehneekuhkôsuash, kah neekussôsik wuhhogkauh, mag8ongash kah weetemungquok ohtag wunnutchegan8óut, nish paudtauunat wekit Jehovah.
41.6 Kah Ishmael wunnaumonuh Nethaniah, sohham wutch Mizpah nah wunnogskauonat, nauwadtohpausu ne ayont, kah n$nih nah nogskauo[n]t, nah wuttinuh, peyaón8k Gedaliah wunnaumonuh Ahikam.
41.7 Kah n$nih paahettit nô|8tâni, Ishmael wunnaumonuh Nethaniah nah wuñushoh, kah wuttinuhkonuh ut nanashaue pasáhtheganit, nagum, kah wosketompuh neh weechógqutcheh.
41.8 Qut piukqussuog ut kenugke wuhhogkaout neg anoncheg Ishmaeloh, ahque nushinnean, nutohtomun nompak8unash ut ohteuhkontu, wheatash, kah barlyhash, kah pummee kah hony, neit kehchithau, kah matta wunnushoh ut kenugke wematut.
41.9 Kah ne passohtheg ne Ishmael petuhteadt wame nupp8e wuhhogkauh (neh nashoncheh newutche Gedaliah) né Asa ketass8t ayikup wutche u[k]qushaonk Baashahoh Israelle ketass8toh, kah Ishmael wunnaumonuh Nethaniah wunnumwamechumuhkon neh nashómukeh.
41.10 Neit Ishmael missinohteau wame sekqshonutcheh missinninúh ut Mizpéh, ketass8t wuttaunoh, kah wame missinninúog, neg sekqshoncheg ut Mizpah: neh Nebuzaradan askuhwhete[a]e mugquomp ohtúhshau Gedaliahoh wunnaumonuh Ahikam; kah Ishmael wunnaumonuh Nethaniah ummissinóhkonu[h] kah monchu qushkogkonat en Ammonitsut.
41.11 Qut Johanan wunnaumonuh Kareah, kah wame kenawamee mugquompaog, n8tamwehettit wame ne machuk Ishmael wunnaumonuh Nethaniah ne asit,
41.12 Neit nemunaog wame wosketompuh, kah ayeuuhkonaog Ishmaeloh wunnaumonuh Neth[a]niah, kah nag wunnamheouh ut kishke mishe nippeut ne ut Gibeon.
41.13 Kah n$nihyeup, wame missinninnuog neg weechayeumoncheg Ishmaeloh, n[a]uahettit Johananoh wunnaumonuh Kareah, kah wame kenauwamee mugquompaog, neh weetómukqutcheh, neit weekontamwog.
41.14 Neit wame missinninnúog neh Ishmael masinohteacheh wutch Mizpah, quinnuppeog, kah qushkeog, kah auog Johananut wunnaumonuh Kareah.
41.15 Qut Ishmael wunnaumonuh Nethaniah pohquohham wutch Johananut, kah weeche shwosuk tahsuog, kah auog Ammonitsut.
41.16 Neit Johanan wunnaumonuh Kareah, kah wame kenauwamee mugquompaog, nag neemunáog wame ashqshonutcheh missinninnúh, neh pohquohwhunoncheh wutch Ishmaelut wunnaumonuh Nethaniah, wutch Mizpah, (mahche nushont Gedaliah wunnaumonuh Ahikam) menuhkesue ayeuhteaenúog, kah mittamwussissog, kah mukki[é]sog, kah Eunuchsog neh wôs8oncheh Gibeon.
41.17 Kah nag monch[é]og, kah appuog wutappuonganit Chimham, ne kishke Bethlehem, woh wutch petutteamuk en Egypt.
41.18 Wutch Caldeansog: newutche nag ukqushóuh, newutche Ishmael wunnaumonuh Nethaniah nushop Gedaliahoh wunnaumonuh Ahikam, neh Babylone ketass8t nanawunnumwáheumpoh ut ohkeit.
42.1 NEit wame kenauwamee mugquompaog, kah Johanan wunnaumonuh Kareah, Jeremiah wunnaumonuh Hoshajah, kah wame missinninnuog wutch peississit pajeh masugkenuk, nag pas8tshaog.
42.2 Kah unnaog J[e]remiahoh quoshodtumwaénuh, k8wehquetumunumun, n8wehquetum8onganun tapeneunkqutch ut anaquabean, kah peantamwanshinnean en Jehovah kum-Manitt8mut, wutche wame yeug ashqshoncheg (newutche nutogguhse sekqshomun wutch mattaanukuppanneg, neh kuskesukquash yeuyeu nauoncheh)
42.3 Onk woh Jehovah kum-Manitt8m nunnáhtinukqun may uttoh woh aôog, kah ne woh aséog.
42.4 Neit Jeremiah quoshodtumwaen nah wuttinuh, ken8tauunumw8, kusseh, nuppeantamau Jehovah kum-Manitt8mw8 neaunak kukkutt8wonganooash, kah pish nnih, uttoh áne Jehovah namp8hamunkqueóg, pish k8wahteauwáhenuneau: wanne teag kukkogkôununumauun8mw8.
42.5 Neit nag unnáog Jeremiahoh, Lord noh wunnamuhkutee, kah pabuhtánumwe wauwaeni[e]ch nashauwe ut nenawun, matta usseog neaunak wame nish Jehovah kum-Manitt8m, ann8nukqueániṣh en nuhhogkanónut.
42.6 Wanegik asuh machuk n8swehtamumun 8wadtauatonkqussuonk Jehovah num-Manitt8mun, noh ánunn8nunog, onk woh n8niyeuhhikqunan n8swehtomog 8wadtauatonkqussuonk Jehovah num-Manitt8mun.
42.7 Kah n$nihyeup mahche piogkukquinogok, wuttinn8waonk Jehovah peyaónuk Jeremiah.
42.8 Neit wehkomau Johananoh wunnaumonuh Kareah, kah kenauwamee mugquompaog, neh weechayeumukqutcheh, kah wame missinninnuog wutch peississit pajeh masugkenuk.
42.9 Kah nah wuttinuh, yeu wussin Lord um-Manitt8moh Israel, noh ánano8seógkup, kupponamunat k8wehquetumo8ongan8 [ú]t anaquabit.
42.10 Ash yeu pumappeóg ohkeit, neit k8wekikónunumw8, kah matta ken8kinin8mw8, kah kutohteuhkonunumw8, kah matta kuppohqunun8mw8, newutche nutáuskoiantam wutche machuk ne anhén[n]óg.
42.11 Wabesuonúhteok Babylone ketass8t, noh quoshog, noh wabesuonúhteogk wussin Jehovah, newutche k8weetómunumw8 k8wadchanunaóont, kah kuppohquohwhununnaóont wutch wunnutcheganit.
42.12 Kah kummonanumunumw8, onk woh kummonánumukou, onk woh kukqushkeáhik8 en nehenwonche kutohtkeout,
42.13 Qut unn8waog matta n8tohtéumun yeu ohkeit, kah matta n8swehtam8mun 8wadtauatonkqussuonk Jehovah kum-Manitt8mw8.
42.14 N8waog, matchaog, qut nutômun ohkeit Egypt, uttoh mo adt naum8og mattompog, kah matta nunn8tam8mun mishont8wae trumpet, kah matta pish nukkodtitteam8mun petukquneg, kah na nutáyinnean.
42.15 Kah yeuyeu newutche n8tam8k wuttinn8waonk Jehovah, kenaau askqshéogish Judah, yeu wussin Jehovah ayeuteaunit um-Manitt8moh Israel, tohneit mamusse ponamok kuskesukooaṣh petukonat en Egypt na$ut keohteainneat.
42.16 Neit pish n$nih, togkodteg ne quohtamóg, ne pish kummattan[ú]kqunneau ut ohkeit Egypt, kah mahshagquodt ne quohtamóg, pish môsogque asuhkongquneau ut Egypt, kah na pish kuttit nuppuneau.
42.17 Ne pish wuttinniinneau wame nag anaquohtunkeg wuskesuk88aṣh ônat Egypt, na ut kéohteáinneat, nag pish nupwog nashpe togkodteg, nashpe mahshagquodt, kah nashpe enninneaonk, kah matta howan nag pish wusseksqshoh, asuh pohquohhamóh machuk ne nóhkenumauog.
42.18 Newutche yeu wussin Jehovah ayeuteaunit, um-Manitt8moh Israel, neane nummusquantamóonk kah nunnisquétuonk sókenumauoneau wadohkitcheg Jerusalem; ne ne nunnisquétuonk pish kussókenumonteaneau petutteaóg Egypt; kah kenaau pish kummattanumitteae utteamw8, kah kutchepshónitteamw8, kah kummatchenànumitteamw8 kah kutushpinanitteamw8, kah matta pish wonk yeu ayeuonk kenaum8uneau.
42.19 Jehovah n8wau papaume kenaau, woi kenaau sekqshaógish Judah, onteógk Egypt, pahke wahteau8k, kukquosháe amaumunnumw8 yeu kesukok.
42.20 Newutche kuteiantoge ussemw8 kuttahh8wout án8néóg en Lord kum-Manitt8m8wóut, an8waog, peantamwanshinnean en Lordut núm-Manitt8munónut, kah neaunak wame ne Jehovah an8wadt, ne ne w[e]ahteauwáhinan, kah mos nutussenan.
42.21 Kah yeuyeu yeu kesukok k8wahteauwáhenuneau, qut matta ken8swehtamomw8 8wadtauatonkqussuonk Jehovah kum-Manitt8mw8, asuh ne teag ne ann8sit en kuhhogkaóut.
42.22 Newutche yeuyeu pahke wahteau8k, pish kenup[m]w8 nashpe togkodteg, nashpe mahashagquodt, kah nashpe enninneaonk, ut ne ayeuonganit ne an kodtantamóg penuwohteainneat.
43.1 KAh n$nih, Jeremiah mahche ken8nont wame missinninnùh, wame ukkutt8wongaṣh Jehovah um-Manitt8m8uh, wutche nish Jehovah um-Manitt8m8uh an8teamwutcheh nah en, wame yeush kutt8wongaṣh
43.2 Neit Azariah wunnaumonuh Hoshajah, kah Johanan wunnaumonuh Kareah, kah wame pahtuánumwutcheg, nag keket8kaog unnáog Jeremiahoh, kuppann8wayim: Jehovah num$Manitt8mun, matta kutann8nuk8h n8wonat, onteógk Egypt na$ut kéohteaineat.
43.3 Qut Baruch wunnaumonuh Neriah kenushquáh en kutáyeuuhkónukqunnanónut, ummagunat kuhhogkaunonash en wunnutchegan8óut Caldeansog, onk woh nag kenushikqunnónog kah kummissinóhkonukqunnanonut en Babylon.
43.4 Neit Johanan wunnaumonuh Kareah kah wame kenauwamee mugquompaog, kah wame missinninnúog matta n8swehtamóog 8wadtauatonkqussuonk Jehovah, wutohkinneat Judae ohkeit.
43.5 Qut Johanan wunnaumonuh Kareah, kah wame kenauwamee mugquompaog, nag neemunáog wame askqushóncheg ut Judah, kah neg quashkécheg wutch wame wutohtimóinneat uttoh ann8kauut, ayinneat Judae ohkeit.
43.6 Wosketompaog, kah mittamwussissog, kah peississog, kah ketass8t wuttaunoh, kah nishnoh howan, neg Nebuzaradan askuhwheteáe mugquomp sequnnumauoncheh Gedaliahoh wunnaumonuh Ahikam, wunnaumonuh Shaphan, kah Jeremiah quoshodtumwaen, kah Baruch wunnaumonuh Neriah.
43.7 Neit peyaog ohkeit Egypt, newutche matta n8swehtam8og 8wadtauatonkqussuonk Jehovah: neit peyaog Taphnes.
43.8 Neit wuttinn8waonk Jehovah peyaonuk Jeremiah ut Taphnes, n8wau,
43.9 Nemunush mogke qussukquanash ut kenutcheganit, kah niṣh adtahtaaṣh ut man8skut ut ahhutchikkoswut bricksog, ne ahhut petutteamuk Pharaoh wek ut Taphnes, ut anaquabhettit Judae wosketompaog:
43.10 Kah nag us, yeu wussin Jehovah ayeuteaunit um$Manitt8moh Israel, kusseh, nutann8team, kah nunneemun Nebuchadnezzar Babylone ketass8t, nuttinneum, kah nukquenahtóh wutappuonk ut woskeche yeush qussukquanaṣh nish adtahtauoniṣh, kah ne woskeche piṣh wuttit sepágenumun wussontimóe kommuk.
43.11 Kah peyont piṣh togkodtam Egypte ohke: neg woh napukeg en nuppunnat, neg woh masinácheg en missinnáinneat, neg woh wutch togkodteg en togkodteganit.
43.12 Kah nunn[a]shqunánum n8teau en wekuóut Egypte manitt8og, kah niṣh piṣh wutchikkossumunaṣh, kah piṣh ummissinóhkonuh, kah pish hogk8 Egypte ohke, onatuh nanaushepsaen ágqut wuthogk8onk, kah na 8ch piṣh wunohteáe sohhamun.
43.13 Kah piṣh wonk pokshanáog Bethshemeshe unneukontunkanog, ne ohtag Egypte ohkeit, kah wek8óash um-manitt8m8uh Egyptiansog pish wutchikkossumunaṣh n8taut.
44.1 WUttinn8waonk ne pauhonukqut Jeremiah papaume wame Jewsog neg wadohkitcheg Egypte ohke, neg wadohkitcheg Migdol, kah Tahpanhes, kah Noph, kah ut wutohkeit Pathros, n8wau,
44.2 Yeu wussin Jehovah ayeuteaunit um-Manitt8moh Israel, kenaumw8 wame machuk ne án nuhkinnumauog Jerusalem, kah wame Judae keitotanéhtu: kah kusseh yeu kesukok touushin, kah matta howan na 8tohkéin.
44.3 Newutche ummatcheseonganooash niṣh asehettichish, numm8m8sqhikqunnaóut, newutche chikossumauópanneg weetemungquok wuttinneumuhkauónat onkatogig manitt8og, neh matta waheáhettegeh matta nag, asuh kenaau, asuh k8sh8woog.
44.4 Qut nutann8nomp en kuhho[g]kaóut wame quoshodtumwae nuttinneumog, nompoae omohkeon, kah ann8nog, nussip, ussehteogk ne nishkeneunkquok ne sekeneam.
44.5 Qut nag matta n8tamoog, kah matta ahchusittam8og, quinnuppenat wutch ummatcheseongan8óut, matta chikohsumauónat weetemungquok onkatogig manittoog.
44.6 Newaj nunnishquetuonk kah nummusquantamoonk sohkenumomp kah nasqunop ut Judae keitotanáhtu, kah Jerusalem[e] toumáogquehtu, kah niṣh mohchim8ash kah touishineash neane yeu kesukok.
44.7 Newutche yeuyeu yeu wussin Jehovah um-Manitt8m8oh ayeuteáog, um-Manitt8m8oh Israel, tohwaj yeu unayeúhkone matchenéheog kukketeahogkôn8, tummehtahwhonat wutche kuhhogkaout wosketomp kah mittamwossis, mukkies kah n8nuk wutch Judah, matta kussequnitteaunnaóut.
44.8 Newutche kumm8m8sqhimw8, nashpe kenutchegane anakausuwonganooash, châgossumauog weetemungkquok onkatogig manitt8og, ut ohkeit Egypt, uttoh a[ó]og kutayeinneaóut, onk woh kuttummetahwhomw8 kuhhogkaoog, onk woh kummattanumitteamw8, kah kukkehkômitteamw8 ut kenugke wame ohkee wutohtimóneáhtu.
44.9 Sun k8wananittamw8 ummatchetowongan8 k8sh8[ô]og, kah ummatchetowongan8 Judae ketass8tamwog kah ummittamwuss8uh ummatchetowongan8, kah nehenwonche kummatchetowongan8, kah kummittamwuss8oog ummatchetowongan8, niṣh aséhetticheh ut Judae ohkit, kah ut Jerusaleme toumáogquehtu.
44.10 Nag matta pohqueteahá8og pajeh yeu kesukok, kah matta wabeséog, kah matta pomushaóntam8og nuttinnaumatuonk, kah nukkuhk8waongash niṣh ponamónish anaquabeóg kah anaqu[a]hettit k8sh8óog.
44.11 Newutche yeu wussin Jehovah ayeuhteaunit um-Manitt8moh Israel, kusseh, kutayeuuhkonittue ponamauonumw8 nuskesuk wutche machuk, kah tummetahwhonat wame Judah.
44.12 Kah nunneemun ashqshoncheg ut Judah, neg anaquoushácheg Egypt na$ut penuwohteáinneat, kah nag piṣh wame mohtuppaéog, kah penushaog ut ohkit Egypt: nag piṣh mahchim8og nashpe togkodteg, kah nashpe mahshagquodt, kah nag piṣh nupwog wutch peississut pajeh masugkenut, nashpe togkodteg kah nashpe mahshagquodt kah nag piṣh mattanittuonk, chepshaonk, kah matánum8[utt]uonk, kah ushpunadtuonk.
44.13 Newutche nag nussasamatahwhóog wadohkiitcheg Egypte ohkeit, neane sasamatahwhogkup Jerusalem nashpe togkodteg, nashpe mahshagquodt kah nashpe enninneaonk.
44.14 Newaj matta howan ashqshoncheg ut Judah neg aóncheg Egypte ohkeit, na$ut n8sausinneat, piṣh pohquohhamm8 asuh sekqshó[o]u, woh nag qushkenóont en Judae ohkeit, ne kodtantamw[é]hettit, en qushkénat, na ayinneat newutch matta piṣh howan qushkeu, qut neg pohquohhogig.
44.15 Neit wame wosketompaog neg wáheoncheg ummittamwuss8oh chikossumau[á]og weetemungquok onkatogeh manitt8h, kah wame mittamwussissog neg na kishke neepauticheg, mattaánukeg, wame missinninnúog neg wadohkitcheg Egypt, ut Pathros, nag namp8hamauâog Jeremiahoh, n8wau,
44.16 Kutt8onk ne áseog ut 8wesuonganit Jehovah, matta kukkuhkeitauunómun.
44.17 Qut wunnamuhkut pish nutussenan uttoh án sohham8m8uk wutch nutt8nunónut chikkohsumauónat weetemungquok kesukque kehchissonkusq, kah sókenumauónat wuttattamoe sephausuongaṣh, ne mahche usséog, nenawun kah n8shunónog: nukketass8timómunónog kah nussontimomunonog ut Judae keitotanahtu, kah Jerusaleme toumaogquehtu: newutche neit nummishe meechumumunónup kah n8niimunónup, kah matta naum8mun machuk.
44.18 Qut nádteuh ahque chikossumauogkut weetemungquok kesukque kehchissonkusq, kah sókenumauonat wuttattamwe mag8ongaṣh, nukquenauhikkumun wame teanteaquassinish, kah nummahche mohchimumun nashpe togkodteg, kah nashpe mahshagquodt.
44.19 Kah chôgossumauógut weetemungquok kesukque kuhchi[s]sonkusq, kah sokenumauogkut wuttattamoe mag8ongash, sun nuttáyimauóunónus petukqunegaṣh wowussumónat, kah sun nussokanumauóunónus wuttattamoe mag8ongash ne toh ut matta násukôunonog?
44.20 Neit Jeremiah unnau wame missinninnúh, wosketompuh, kah mittamwossissoh, kah wame missinnúh neh namp8hamunutcheh, n8wau,
44.21 Weetemungquok ne chôgossumogkup, ut Judae keitotanahtu, kah ut Jerusaleme toumaogquehtu kenaau, kah kussontim8m8oog, kah ohkee missinninnúog, sunnummatta Jehovah ummequanumuh, kah sunnummatta peyomunóus ut wuttenantam8onganit?
44.22 Newaj Jehovah matta sepe kehchithog, wutche machuk kutusseongan8, kah wutche ne unkquánumukquok ne aséog: newaj touushik kutohtu, kah chepshaonganu8, kah matanittuonganu8, matta wutohkéin, neane yeu kesukok.
44.23 Newutche kutchikkossumw8 weetemungquok, newutche kummatcheneheomw8 Jehovah, kah matta ken8swetamomw8 8wadtauatonkqussuonk Jehovah, kah matta kuppomushomw8 wuttinna[u]matuonganit, kah matta ukkuhk8waonganit, asuh 8wauwaonganit, newaj yeu machuk peyaonukqueóg, neane yeu kesukok.
44.24 Nano Jeremiah unnau wame missinninnúh, kah wame mittamwussissoh: n8tam8k wuttinn8waonk Jehovah, wame Judah neg apitcheg ohkeit Egypt.
44.25 Yeu wussin Jehovah ayeuhteaunit um-Manitt8moh Israel, n8wau, kenaau kah kummittamwuss8oog, naneeswe kussimw8 nashpe kutton8wout, kah kummahche usseneau nashpe kenutchegan8, kussimw8: wunnamuhkut nutussenan nukquoshomuwaonganunonaṣh, niṣh quoshoáogiṣh, chikohsumauonat wetemungquok kesukque kehchissonkusq, kah sokanumauónat wuttattamoe mag8ongaṣh: wunnamuhkut piṣh kuppahkodchehteomw8 kukquoshomuwaongan8oaṣh, kah wunnamuhkut piṣh kutussemw8 kukquoshomuonganooaṣh.
44.26 Newutche n8tam8k wuttinn8waonk Jehovah, wame Judah neg wadohkitcheg Egypt ohkeit, kusseh, nutchadchekéyeuop nashpe nummishe wesuonk, wussin Lord, n8wesuonk matta piṣh wonk missohham8un ut wutt8nut, howae Judae wosketomp ut wame Egypte ohkeit, unn8wadt Jehovah Manit pomantam.
44.27 Kusseh, nag nutaskwhonóog wutche machuk, qut matta wanegik, kah wame Judae wosketompaog ut ohkeit Egypt, nag piṣh mahchim8og nashpe togkodteg, kah nashpe mahshagquodt, nô pajeh 8wohkukquossinunaóont[.]
44.28 Qut ogguhsikeg neg pohquohhogig togkodteg, nag pish qushkeog wut-Egypte ohkeit en Judae ohkeit: kah wame ashqshoncheg Judah neg aoncheg Egypt na$ut n8sausinneat, nag pish wa[h]teauog howan ukkutt8onk manuhkohtag, nukkutt8onk asuh nagumau.
44.29 Kah yeu pish kukkehkinneasuongan8, wussin Jehovah, kussasamatahwhush yeu$ut ayeuonganit, onk woh k8wahteomw8, wunnamuhkut pish nuttinn8waonk, kummenuhtikkompauwehtunkquneau wutche machuk
44.30 Yeu wussin Jehovah kusseh, Pharoh-Hophra Egypte ketass8t nuppon wunnutchegan8wout ummatwomoh, kah en wunnutchegan8out neg kodnushoncheg, neane mag8omp Zedechiah Judae ketass8t en wunnutcheganit Nebuchadnezzer Babylone ketass8t ummatwomoh noh kodnushomp.
45.1 WUttinn8waonk ne JEremiah quoshodtumwaen anont Baruchoh wunnaumonuh Neriah, mahche wâsukkuhh8k ut B8kut yeush wuttinn8waongash, wutch wutt8nut Jeremiah, ut weyaue kodtum8mut Jehojakim wunnaumonuh Josiah Judae ketass8t, n8wau,
45.2 Jehovah um-Manitt8muh Israel yeu kuttugqun, woi Baruch.
45.3 Kussip, yeuyeu missi nutonkapunaonk, newutche Lord k8tnehtau neuantam8onk en nutonkquanum8onganit, nussauunumup mahshanomweon, kah matta nunnampteo8 anwôsin8onk.
45.4 Yeu woh kuttinnon, yeu wussin Lord, kusseh, ne ayimomp nuppohquenumun, kah ne ahketeaomp nuppohqunumun, yeu mamusse ohke.
45.5 Kah kenatinneaham magogish? wutch kuhhog natiñeham8hkon: newutche kusseh, nunnuhkenumau machuk wame weyaus wussin J[é]hovah, qut kuppomantamoonk kuttinnumauunun wutch kuttohqunnumoonk ut wame ayeuonganéhtu uttoh aoan.
46.1 WUttinn8waonk Jehovah, ne peyaonuk Jeremiah quoshodtumwaen ayeuuhkonittue penuwohteaog.
46.2 Ayeuuhkonittue Egypt ayeuuhkone ukkenauwameonk Pharoh$Necho Egypte ketass8t, noh ayeup kishke Euphratese sepuut, ut Carcemish, ne Nebuchadnezzar Babylone ketass8t togkodtogkup ut weyaue kodtum8mut Jehojakim wunnaumonuh Josiah Judae ketass8t.
46.3 Wunohto8k bukler kah ogqunneg, kah pas8tshagk ayeuwuttinneat.
46.4 Wunneheuk horsesog, kuhkuhquegk naiyeumutteaogish, kah neepauwehtam8k nashpe kuppuhkukk8out ahohtagish, wunnehteogk qunuhtugquash, kah hogk8k brigandinsash.
46.5 Tohwutch nag nauog wutchepshonaoont, kah qushkeog? kah ummissugken8m8uh n8ketahwhoninneuh, kah kenuppe puhh8waog, kah matta ompamuhquaeog, newutche wabesuonk quinuppohtop, wussin Jehovah.
46.6 Neg kakenupshoncheg, wusseemohettekitch, kah mas[ú]gkenuk, pohquohhogitch, nag pish togkussittassunwog, kah penushaog nogque nanummiyeu, kishke Euphrates.
46.7 Howan yeuoh ogque kuhkuhquit tomogkonit noh wunnuppeash agque mamonchem88g sepuut?
46.8 Egypt ohque waapem8 tommogkonit, kah wunnuppemash ogque mamonchem8ash sepuut, kah n8wau, nukkuhkuhquem, nunnuhkuhkom ohke, nuppagwatoh keitotan kah wame neg na wadohkitcheg.
46.9 Kuhkuhquegk kenaau horsesog, kah mishont8wag kenaau chariotsash, kah manuhkesitcheg sohhamwehettich, Ethiopiansog kah Lybiansog, neg nohtonukeg ogqunneg, kah Lydiansog neg nahtuhtunkig, kah p8tunkanoncheg ohtompeh.
46.10 Newutche yeu ukkesukkodtum Lord Jehovah ayeuhteaunit, ann8tôadtue kesukod onk woh ann8tauau ayeuuhkonukqutcheh: kah togkodteg pish mahchipp8m8, kah pish wamep8h[,] kah kogkeissippam8 nag 8sqheongan8: newutche Lord JEhovah ayeuteaunit sephausuonk ohtoou ut nanum ohkeit, ut kishke Euphratise sepuut.
46.11 Kuhkuhquegk en Gilead, kah neemunuṣh balme woi penomp Egypte wuttaunin: tahn8che piṣh kutauwóhteam iyánaskéhtuaṣh: newutche matta piṣh keneetskesu.
46.12 Wutohtimóneunk n8tamwog kutakodchuonk, kah kummauonk numwohtau ohkeit: newutche menuhkesuen ayeuuhkonittue togkussittassum8óneau masugkenutcheh, kah nag neeswe moeu kepshaog.
46.13 Wuttinn8waonk ne Jehovah ánont Jeremiahoh quoshodtumwaenúh, uttoh an piṣh Nebuchadnezzar Babylone ketass8t peyont, kah togkodteg Egypte ohke.
46.14 Wahteauwáhuwagk ut Egypt, kah n8tamwahuw[a]gk ut Migdol, kah n8tamwahuwag ut Noph, kah ut Taphnes, n8wagk, menehtikkompauṣh, kah nanashwiṣh, newutche tokkodteg piṣh mahchipp8 ut k8wohkôiyeumut.
46.15 Tohwaj kummenuhkesuenúmog chékuhwhut? matta neepau8og, newutche wutáma8hkauópuh Jehovah.
46.16 Monaoh penusháheau, nux, papenush[a]ónittuog, kah n8waog, omohkek, kah wonk óntuh nehenwonche kummissinninnumunónut, kah ut keneetue ohkéunnonut wutch sunukkutchoh8wae togkodteganit.
46.17 Nag na wuttit mauunáop, Pharaoh Egypte ketass8t noh webe wuttauatonkqussuonk, noh paumuhkom kuhquttum8e ahquompi.
46.18 Pomantamon, wussin ketass8t noh ás8wesit Jehovah ayeuteaunit, wunnamuhkut neane Tabor ut kenugke wadchuuhkontu, kah neane Carmel kishke ketahhannit, ne piṣh wuttinne peyon.
46.19 Woi ken wuttaunin áyean Egypt, tâpauwamish en missinnainneat, newutche Noph piṣh mahchim8, kah touwushin, matta wutohkéinneat.
46.20 Egypt tatuppeyeu8og wunnetue heifer$ut, qut paguanuonk peyau: 8m88 nanummiyeu.
46.21 Kah wonk ann8nutcheg ut wunnashómut, nag tatuppeyeu8og wunnogque oxenat, newutche nag wonk qushkeog, kah m[ó]eu wussem8og, nag matta neepau8og, newutche uppaguanúe kesukkodtum8 nuhkuhkongquog, kah natauwahaongane ahquompi.
46.22 Ne wuttauatonkqussuonk piṣh ohque monchem8 ask8kut: newutche nag piṣh moncheog weeche kenauwameonk, kah piṣh wutayeuuhkonittue uppeyaun[ó]uh nashpe togungaṣh, kah pogkomshaenúog.
46.23 Nag piṣh tummehtamwog wuttouohkomuk8 wussin Jehovah, tohkônogque woh mo pannuppadtinneuhkóntam8un, newutche nag ánuánwog onk neg chantsampsog, kah ahantanwog.
46.24 Egypte wuttaunin piṣh chepshau, noh piṣh ponau ut wunnutchegan8out nanummiyeue missinninnuog.
46.25 Jehovah ayeuteaunit um-Manitt8moh Israel, n8wau, kusseh, nussasamatoh mataánukeg No, kah Pharaoh, kah Egypt, weeche um-manitt8m8uh, kah ukketass8tam8m8uh, Pharaoh kah wame neh pabuhtanumukqutche.
46.26 Kah nag nummagunununk ut wunnutchegan8out neg kodnushoncheg, kah ut wunnutcheganit Nebuchadnezzar Babylone ketass8t, kah ut wunnutchegan8out wuttinneumoh, kah ompetak piṣh wutohkim, neane nôadt wussin Jehovah.
46.27 Qut wabeséhkon, ken woi nuttinneum Jakob, kah chepshuhkon woi Israel, newutche kusseh, k8wadchāsh wutche n8adtit, kah k8skannem wutch ummissinnáe ohkéyeuóut, kah Jakob piṣh qushkeu, kah piṣh anwôsin, kah mánunniyeu, kah matta piṣh howan 8wabesuwaheuh.
46.28 Wabesehkon, woi Jakob nuttinneum wussin Jehovah, newutche k8weetomsh, newutche n8wohkukquossum wame wutohtimoneash uttoh ann8hkauun, qut matta ken kuppapaquanne wohkukquossumunn8, qut quttuh[h]am8e kussasamatoush onch matta kummamusse mat sasamatahwhun8.
47.1 WUttinn8waonk Jehovah ne pauhonukqut Jeremiah quoshodtumwaen, ayeuuhkonittue Philistiansog, asquam Pharaoh togkomunk Gaza.
47.2 Yeu wussin Lord, kusseh, nippeash waapém8aṣh wutch nanummiyeu, kah niṣh piṣh anúchuwáne tommogkon, kah piṣh anúchuan ohke, kah wame na na ohtag keitotan kah neg na wadohkitcheg: neit piṣh wosketompaog mauog, kah wadohkitcheg ohkeit pish 8n8og.
47.3 Wadtauatongqussinit wúhkass8oh menuhke wut-horsesumoh, kah kogunkshik wut-chariotsumash, kah téqunum8m8uk 8wheelumash, wut8shimau matta piṣh ompamuhquaéhtauau wunneechanuh wutche n8chumwiyeuut wunnutchegaṣh.
47.4 Newutche kesukod peyaum8 matcheheonaoont wame Philistiansog, kah tummehtahwhonat wutch Tyrus, kah Zidon, nish$noh anninnohsuen noh sekqshont: newutche Jehovah pish matcheheau Philistiansoh, wutusk[q]shaongan8 Caphtore wutohtimoin.
47.5 M8sontuppaonk nuhkuhkom Gaza: Ashkalon tummetahwhou, weeche 8nouhkoiyeue askqshonutcheh: toh utt8ch pish kuttummetah kuhhog?
47.6 Woi ken wuttogkodtegoh Jehovah, toh utt8che pish kutchonchequnap? pechish pechehquogkunganit, anwôsish kah chequnapsh.
47.7 Uttoh woh en chequnohteau, newutche Jehovah ummechumuhkontamun ayeuuhkone Ashkelon, kah ayeuuhkone ketahhanne unnunohkomuk? na wuttit kukquttumun.
48.1 AYeuuhkone Moab yeu wussin Jehovah ayeuteaunit, um-Manitt8moh Israel missi wutonkapunaonk Nebo newutche matchehteauun: Kirjathaim chepshaum8, kah sohkomun: Misgab chepshaum8 kah quequena[u]onum8m8.
48.2 Matta pish wonk waeenomoun Moab, ut Heshbon wutayeuuhkonittue natwontammontamunneau machuk: peyunk tummehthamuttuh, matta wutohtimoinneayeu8 ut ken wonk pish kuttummetahwhit, woi Madmen, togkoteg pish k8naumatuhkunk.
48.3 Maue wadtauatonkqussuonk wtuch Horonaim, mukk8kinnuwaonk, kah mishe pagwanuonk.
48.4 Moab pagwanau, uppeissesumoh n8tamwahuwon ummauongan8.
48.5 Newutche ahhut kuhkuhquemuk Luhith maue mauonk kuhkuhquem8: newutche ahhut w8mussimuk Horonaim, matwaog n8tamwog pagwunue mauonk.
48.6 Wusseem8k, pohquohwuttau8k kuppomantam8ongan8, ogqueneunkqussek poskissuwontugqut tou$ohkomukqut.
48.7 Newutche newaj pabuhtantaman kutanakausuongash, kah kenompak8unash, ken wonk pish kuttogquinit, Chemosh pish sohham en missinnainneat weeche wussephausueneumoh, kah wussontimomoh moeu.
48.8 Kah woskehuwaenin piṣh nuhkuhkom nishnoh keitotan, kah matta otan piṣh pohquohham8mun8; 8nóuhkôi wonk piṣh paguanum8, kah mukoshqut piṣh pagwatauun, ne an8wop Jehovah.
48.9 Wunnuppawhunuhkok Moab onk woh pt8wu, kah monchasseau, newutche ukkeitotanaṣh piṣh touishinneash, matta howan wutayeineat.
48.10 Matánumunach noh mehshane usseit wutanakausuonk Jehovah: kah matan[ú]munach noh kohkôunuk wuttogkodteg wutch wusqueheonganit.
48.11 Moab manunaiyeup wutch wuskenúuneat, áhtoteapáshitteau wul-leesum, kah matta wuttuhhòntsu sequnnum8un en wishquadt, kah matta missinoou, newaj wuttishpukqussuonk ash pumohtunk, kah wuttussumunkqussuonk matta ôs8wemun8.
48.12 Newutche kusseh, kesukodtash peyom8 wussin Lord, negonshhúam en wuhhogkat kogkeompoh, nag piṣh ukkogkéompohéouh, kah nag piṣh sequnnumwog 8wishquaṣh, kah piṣh soquttahhamwog 8wishquaṣh.
48.13 Kah Moab akodchuwonau Chemoṣh, neane Israelle wek akodchuwontogkup Bethel uppabahtantamoonk.
48.14 Tohwaj n8waog, nenawun nummissugkénimun kah nummenuhkesimun en ayeú[h]konat.
48.15 Moab matcheheau, kah kuhkuhqueu wutch ukkeitotanáhtu, kah uppepénamwe wuskeneumoh womsuog en pagwanittiñeat, n8wau ketass8t, noh [á]s8wesit, Jehovah ayeuhteaunit.
48.16 Wutunkquanumoonk Moab pas8cheyeu8, kah wutonkapunaonk kenupshaum8.
48.17 Wame kenaau weenuhkauógiṣh mauunitteaunshúk, kah wame kenaau wahteauógiṣh 8wesuonk, n8wak, uttoh en menuhke anwohhou poksheau, kah wunnegenne pogkommunk.
48.18 Ken wuttaunin áyean Dibon womsish wutch kussohsum8onganit, kah kunkutt8n8e appish: newutch noh matcheneheont Moaboh piṣh kenuhkuhkunk, kah noh piṣh pagwatau k8wonkon8sinaṣh.
48.19 Woi ken wadohkean Aroer, neepaush kishke mayut, kah askuhwheteaṣh, nat8tomau noh waseemuk, kah noh pohquohhuk, toh mahche n$nih?
48.20 Moab quequenauánum8 newutche pohquetahwhôu; 8n8k kah mau8k, unnok ut Arnon, Moab matcheheau.
48.21 Kah wussittumoonk nuhkuhkom mukoshqutáe wutohtimóin, ut Holon, kah ut Jahazah, kah ut Mephaath,
48.22 Kah ut Dibon, kah ut Nebo, kah ut Beth$diblithaim.
48.23 Kah ut Kirjathaim, kah ut Beth[-]gamul, kah ut Beth-meon,
48.24 Kah ut Kirjoth, kah ut Bozrah, kah ut wame Moabe keitotanahtu, noóhkish kah pás8giṣh
48.25 Wutaskonoh Moab tummetahwhôu, kah 8hpit pohquetahhamun wussin Jehovah.
48.26 Kogkeissippamwéheúk, newutche mishehheau wuhhogkuh ayeuhkonónat Jehovah; Moab wonk piṣh ôômeu ummenádtam8onk, kah noh wonk piṣh ahanehtauôu.
48.27 Newutche sunnummatta Israel kutáhanehtauómus? sun noh nameheous kenugke komm8towanúut? newutche nadteuh weadtimadt, kukquequeshomp wutche wekontam8onk.
48.28 Woi kenaau wadohkéogiṣh Moab, nukkodtum8k keitotanaṣh, kah ayégk qussukquannéhtu, kah ogqueneunkqussek wuskuhwhununáut, noh ádtanadsháteadt sussippôeu wônogquehtu.
48.29 Nunn8tamumun[ó]nup uppehtuanum[o]onk Moab (noh mishe pittuánum8) ukqunnunkquanumoonk ummish[á]numoonk, kah uppehtuánumoonk, kah ukqunuhqutteaháonk.
48.30 N8wahteoh ummusquanittam8onk wussin Lord, qut ne matta piṣh nano uppann8waongaṣh matta piṣh ussémun8.
48.31 Newaj 8n8wanshok Moab, kah nummishont8wam wutche wame Moab, nuttah mauunnitteauwánshau Kir-hereze wosketompaog.
48.32 Woi Sibmahhe weenomwussippog, kummauunitteauwanshish nashpe Jazere mauonk: niṣh adtannegikish kuhhogkat naish qushkodteam8aṣh kehtahhannit, nash weeksqhineash Jazere kehtahhannit, matchehuwaen penushadtam keneepunne meechummuongaṣh, kah ut k8wenominne kepenum8onganit.
48.33 Kah weekontam8onk kah muskouantam8onk amaunumun wutch missegunne ohteuhkonit, kah wutch Moabe ohkeit, kah wine monteagwunnuóhtauóuun wutch wine-pressut, matta howan mishont8wae wuttahtaskuhkom8un, ummishont8ongan8 matta piṣh mishont8womun8.
48.34 Wutch ummauonganit Heshbon wehque Elealeh, kah wehque Jahaz, mishont8waog wutch Zoar wehque Horonaim, ogque heifer nashwe kodtumwohkog: newutche wunnippem8aṣh Nimrim piṣh touishinneash.
48.35 Nano, n8wohkukquossum ut Moab, wussin Jehovah, noh sephausit ut qunuhqui ayeuongan[e]htu, kah noh chôgossumauont weetemungquok, ummanitt8moh.
48.36 Newaj piṣh nuttah ogque mishont8wag puhpekquónit, wutche Moab: kah nuttah piṣh ogque mishont8wau puhpequonit, wutche Kir-hereze wosketompahtu: newutch 8weenauwetuongash niṣh ohtunkish mahtshaaṣh.
48.37 Newutche nishnoh muhpuhkuk piṣh mukukki, kah nishnoh weeshitt8n m8sumun; ut wame menutcheganéhtu piṣh tannogkussim8onganú8, kah ut wame musseganit man8tionakinnú8.
48.38 Pish maumuttam8onganú8 mamusseu wame woskéche kommukquehtu Moab, kah ut toumaogquehtu: newutche nutogque pohquttoh Moab wishquadt, uttoh adt matta weekontam8onganin8k, wussin Jehovah.
48.39 Nag piṣh 8n8wog, uttoh en pohquetahhamun? uttoh en Moab uppisk ukquinnuppinnumun en akodchuonganit: nein pish Moab ahanéhtauon kah chepshaonou wame neg quánuppuhkauoncheg
48.40 Newutche yeu wussin Jehovah, kusseh, noh piṣh ogque pt8wu wompesikkuhquait, kah piṣh anue sephagkenau wunnuppewhunoh ut Moab.
48.41 Kirjoth sohkomun, kah wonkon8sinash sohkomunaṣh: kah wuttahhou Moabe menuhkesuenuog piṣh tatuppeyeu8 mittamwussis wuttahhut, ut wutonkquommom8onganit.
48.42 Kah Moab pish paguanau matta ummissinninnueneat, newutche noh ayeuuhkonittue misheheau wuhhogkuh Jehovah$ut.
48.43 Wabesuonk, kah passohtheg, kah ahpeh pish kenuhkuhkunk, woi wadohkean Moab wussin Jehovah.
48.44 Noh wasemwut wutche wabesuonk petshau pass[o]theganit, kah noh kájeit wutch passohtheganit, pish puttahwho[u] ut appehhannit, newutche nunnuhkinnuamau, Moab natauwahae ukkodtum8m8 wussin Jehovah.
48.45 Neg wasemwutcheg nepoog ut agwe Heshbonne onkauohtaut, newutche chekee usseonk, qut n8tau pish sohham8m8 wutch Heshbon, kah n8n8nau wutch nashaue Sihon, kah pish mahchipp8m8 wunnashinneum Moab, kah ukkodtantupp[ô]un8 wogkouitcheg.
48.46 Missi kutonkapunaonk woi Moab, ummissinninnumoh Chemosh pagwanuog: kah kenaumonuh missinohkonunk kah kuttaunog missinoowog.
48.47 Qut wonk nukquehchuwuttoh ummissinooonk Moab ut ogkomae kesuko[k]tut wussin Lord yeu sohke wussumon Moab.
49.1 PApaume Ammonitsog yeu wussin Jehovah, Israel sun mo wunnaumoniyeu? sun mo howane nompenukkou? tohwhuech neit ukketass8tamom8uh nompenumunit Gad, kah ummissinninnumoh ayeuoh wutotanahtu?
49.2 Newutche kusseh, kesukodtash peyaum8 wussin Jehovah n8tamwahuwam mattompagwe wadtauatonkqussuonk ut Rahab ut Ammonitsut, kah ne pish touushinne numwunkquau, kah wuttaunoh pish chikkossuoh ut n8taut: neit pish Israel nompenau neh nompinukqutcheh wussin Jehovah.
49.3 OOnsh woi Heshnon, newutche Ai matchitteauun, mau8k kenaau wuttaun8oh Rabbah, puttukquobpissuwontam8k man8tionak: maumuttam8k, kah ahahsukqueu ussishunk pum̃enutunkanehtu: newutche ukketass8tam8m8uh pish missino8oh, wussephausueneumoh kah wussontimomoh moeu.
49.4 Tohwutch waeenowaan ut 8nouhkôiyeutu, kuttommogkonne 8nouhkoiyeum, woi as8epósue wuttaunin: noh pabahta[n]tog wunnompak8unash, n8wau, howan woh pauhausit?
49.5 Kusseh, kenuhkenumoush wabesuonk wussin Lord Jehovah ayeuteaunit, wutch wame yeug weenuhkongqueaneg, kah pish kenaau kussohh8konteamw8, nish$noh pasuk, piuhsuke, kah matta howan pish ummuhkinuh neh naswaiyinitch[e]h.
49.6 Kah ompetagk pish wonk nukqushkinnum ummissin8onk wunnaumonuh Ammon, wussin Jehvoah.
49.7 Papaume Edom, yeu wusin Jehovah ayeuteaunit sun waantamoonk matta wonk ohtano ut Teman? ukkogahqutteam8onk sun mahchem8 wutch waantamwehtu, sun mahtshaau 8waantam8ongan8?
49.8 Wussem8k, qushken, ayek monaiyeuut wói wadohkeogish Dedan: neuwtche nunnuhkenumau wutonkquanum8onk Esau, ahquompi ne adt n8tauwaheog.
49.9 Mainneacheg weenominneash peogqueog, sunnummatta sequnnum8og mukkupashquaeu weenomineash komm8towaenuog nukkonaeu, nag mukk8kinnuwaog nô pajeh wamepwunneaoont.
49.10 Qut Esau nupp8skissuah, nupposkinum ukkôussuongash, kah noh matt apish tapenum8 upputtogquenat: 8skannem match[é]hteanun, kah weematoh, kah weetatteamungoh, kah noh matta appu.
49.11 Nukkodtumah kuttouiesumog, nuppomantamwahheoog: kah kussekous[q]omog pabahtanumehettich.
49.12 Newutche yeu wussin Jehovah kusseh, nag wásumitcheg matta wuttattam8unat wuttattamwaitch, wunnamuhkut wuttattamwog, kah sun ken woh matta sasamatahwhont, qut wunnamuhkut pish k8tattamun.
49.13 Newutche nashpe nen nehenwonche nutchadchekeyeuwam wussin Jehovah, Bozra pish touwushin, kekontuonk mahchumm8onk, matanittuonk, kah wame ukkeitotaneumash, pish michemohtae touishinneash.
49.14 Nunn8tamup wadtauatonkqussuonk wutch Lordut, kah ann8naenin ann8nau en pen8wohteaut, n8wau, miyaek, ayeuuhkon8k, kah waabpek en ayeuwuttinneat.
49.15 Newutche kusseh, kuppéhesh ut kenugke penuwohteaut, kah kutjishanumukqush ut kenugke wosketompaog.
49.16 Kutunkqueneunkqussuonk kuppûhch8unuk, kuppetuánumwutteaháonk woi ken wadohkean, passipskodtut,, ken wadchanumon koduhkôag, t[ó]konogque ogque qunuhqueu wadjishóhteáan wompsikukquaut, nâ k8ch n8kinunin, wussin Lord.
49.17 Edom wonk pish touwushin: nishnoh pasuk nâ kishke paumushadt piṣh chepshau, kah piṣh quequssumau wáme enninneaongash na$ut.
49.18 Neane képuhteamukup Sodom kah Gomorrah, kah weene keitotanash, wussin Jehovah: matta howan na piṣh wutappein, kah matta wosketompae wunnaumonain piṣh 8tohkein.
49.19 Kusse[h], piṣh ogque kuhkuhqueu qunnónouut, wutch ummogquesuonk Jordan, ayeuuhkonittue wutáyeuongan8 manuhkesitcheg: qut nukkenuppe wussémowah wutch nahoh, kah howan pepenaue wosketomp, onk woh nah nanawunnumwahéonuh? newutche howan yâninneunkqusseh? kah howan woh kohquttumiit ahquompi? howan noh nanaushepsaen woh neepauit anaquabeh?
49.20 Newutche n8tamok ukkogáhqutteám8onk Jehovah, ne ayeuuhkonittue nemunum Edom, kah uppogkodtantam8onk ne pagkodtantog ayeuuhkonittue wadohkinitcheh Teman: wunnamuhkut peississit ut flockut, piṣh nah ukkódtinuh: wunnamuhkut piṣh touwushitteau wutáyeuongan8 weeche nahoh.
49.21 Ohke ontohteau panusháhettit: mauuhhettit, ne wadtauatonkqussuonk wuttussittamun mishque ketahhanit.
49.22 Kusseh, noh piṣh kuhkuhqueu, kah pt8wu onatuh wompsikukquáut, kah piṣh woskeche sepagenau umméqunuh Bozrah: kah n[è] kesukok wuttahhou Edome menuhkesuenuog, piṣh ogqutteahaog mittumwossis onkquonomit.
49.23 Papaume Damaskus, Hamath chepshau kah Arpad: kah newutche nag n8tamwog matchissetonkquot, nag sohqutteaháog, onkquanumoonk ohteau ketahhannit, matta woh chequnohtan8.
49.24 Damaskus nano n8chumwesu, quinnuppinnum wuhhog wussémunneat, kah wabesuonk nuhkuhkunk; onkquanum8onk kah onkquommom8ongaṣh wutogque tohqunukqun[a]ṣh mittamwossis neechadt.
49.25 Uttoh en waeenomae keitotan matta nukkodtum8un, n8weekontam8e keitotan?
49.26 Newaj piṣh 8skeneumoh penushonit ut toumaogquehtu, kah wame ayeuteaenuog piṣh tummetahwhôog ne kesukok, wussin Lord ayeuhte[a]unit.
49.27 Kah nunnashqunánum n8teau, ut Damaskusse hassunnútunkanit; kah piṣh mahchikkussum8m8 ummishe kommuk8maṣh Benhadad.
49.28 Papaume Kedar, kah papaume Hazore ass8tam8ongaṣh, niṣh Nebuchadnezzar Babylone ketass8t piṣh tôkodtogiṣh, yeu wussin Jehovah: omohkek, kuhkuhquek en Kedar, kah mukk8kin8k wutcheksue wosketompaog.
49.29 Week8oaṣh kah uf-flocksum8oaṣ nag piṣh amaunáog, nag piṣh nemunumoog wutonkwhongan8, kah wame 8wishqua8ash, kah Camelsum8uh, kah nag ummishont8wánumauóuh, wabesuonk quinnuppeyeu8.
49.30 Wusseem8k, nôadtut onkq, m8nôiyeuut ayék, woi wadohkéógiṣh Hazor wussin Jehovah: newutche Nebuchadnezzar Babylone ketass8t ayeuuhkonittue k8weadtimuk8, kah missantam pogkodtantamoonk ayeuuhkonittue kenaau.
49.31 Neepok kuhkuhquek wenauwetue wutohtimoineat[,] neg matta nan[a]uw[ó]ntamwe ayitcheg, wussin Jehovah, neg matta ohto8gig squontamash asuh barsash, neg nâsiitcheg.
49.32 Kah uk-Camelsum8uh piṣh tohqunnum8onganú8oh kah mataánukeg uppuppinashim8m8uh piṣh mukk8kinittuonganu8, kah nag nusseahwhôog ut wame wabanéhtu, neg aongkoue adt nashik, kah nuppaudto, wutonkquanum8ongan8 wutch waeenu, wussin Lord.
49.33 Kah Hazor piṣh wutáyeuongan8 dragonsog, kah micheme touwushin, matta na piṣh howan wutappein, kah matta wosketompae wunnumoniin piṣh 8tohkéin.
49.34 Wuttinn8waonk Jehovah uppeyaonukqun Jeremiah quoshodtumwaen, ayeuuhkonittue Elam; n8che nanauwunnuadt Zedechiah Judae ketass8t, n8wau,
49.35 Yeu wussin Jehovah ayeuteaunit, kusseh, nuppohqun wutahtompeh Elam, kehche ummenuhkesueneúm8uh.
49.36 Kah nunnúhkinumau Elam yauoh wuttinoh, wutch yaue kesukque chippiyeuut, kah nag nusseahwhôog nogque wame yeuh wabanehtu, kah na piṣh mat wutohtimoinneaèn8, uttoh en pogkénitcheg wutch Elam matta piṣh peyôuneau.
49.37 Newutche nutchepsháheaog Elam ut anaquabenit ummatwom8oh, kah ut anaquabinit kodnushikqutcheh: kah nunnuhkinnumauóog machuk, nummishe musquantamoonk wussin Lord, kah nag n8suhqunóog togkodteg, nô pajeh nummohtupponónaóont.
49.38 Kah nupponam nutappuonk ut Elam, kah na n8ch paguanon ketass8t kah sontimóog, wussin Jehovah.
49.39 Qut piṣh n$nih, ut majish kesukodtásh, piṣh wonk nukquehchuwutto ummissinóonk Elam, wussin Jehovah.
50.1 KUtt8onk ne ayeuuhkonittue Babylonut unn8wadt Jehovah, kah ayeuuhkonittue wutohtuout Caldeansog, nashpe Jeremiah quoshodtumwaen.
50.2 Wahteauwahu8k ut kenugke wutohtimôineat, kah n8tamwahuwagk, kah nepatto8k muttaagk, n8tamwahuwagk, kah attáhta8hkon; n8wagk, Babylon sohkomun, Bel chepshau, Merodach sokqshau, wuttinneukontunkoh chepsháoh, wuttinneukontunkanouh sokqsháoh.
50.3 Newutche wutch nanummiyeu ayeuuhkonittue kuhkuhquehtunk wutohtim[ô]in, nah piṣh touishitte[a]uohteauinit wutohke, kah matta howan na piṣh wutaiin: nag piṣh ontappuog, nag piṣh amaéog naneeswe wosketomp kah puppinashim.
50.4 Yeush ut kesukodtaṣh, kah na ahquompak wussin Jehovah, wunneechanoh Israel piṣh peyaoh, nag kah wunneechanoh Judah moeu, monchehettit, kah mauhettit, nag piṣh moncheog kah natinnewhaog Jehovah um-Manitt8m8uh.
50.5 Nag pish nat8tamuhteaog may ánshik Zion, ne nogque anaquosháhettit, n8wahettit, peyonk, weech8whuttitteuh en Jehovahut nashpe michemohtae wunn8waonk, ne matta wanhuwómun8g.
50.6 Nummissinninnúmog mahche wunneheáog shepsoh, wunnanaushepsaéneum8oh nanwushahukquog, nah wuttinn8hkauóuh wadchuuhkontu nag ahóntsadchuwâusháog, nag wanantamwog wutanwôsin8e ayeuongan8.
50.7 Wame neh nahnamheoncheg ummahchipwunneaóuh, kah a8kqhetticheh n8waoh matta nummatcheseumun: newutche nag matcheneheaog Jehovah, wutáyeuonk sampweusseonk, Jehovah wutannoósuongan8 8sh8oh.
50.8 Ontappek wutch nashauwe Babylon, kah sohham8k wutch wutohtuóut Caldeansog, kah tatuppéyeuk nomposhimwut ut anaquohtag flock.
50.9 Newutche kusseh, n8waábeh kah nukkuhkuhqueáh ayeuuhkonittue Babylon, mishe wutohtimóinne mukkinneunk, wutch nanumohkeit, kah nag piṣh, wutayeuuhkonittue wunappehtauóuh, nâ wutch piṣh amaunou: nag ukkôuhquodt8aṣh piṣh tatuppeyeu8aṣh noh pagwohteadt, matta piṣh tahn8che qushkemu8.
50.10 Kah Caldea piṣh matchehteauonganu8, wame neg magk8kinoncheg piṣh wamep8og, wussin Jehovah.
50.11 Newutche k8wekontamumwop, newutch kummuskouantamumwop, woi kenaau pagwatauógish wutohtóonk, newutche nano konohkumw8, onatuh heiferut maskuhkuhkontu, kah kutogque chequttumumw8 nomposhimwut.
50.12 K8kás8 piṣh mishe chepshau, noh nekhikqueóg piṣh akodchu, kusseh, aongkoue wutohtimoin piṣh touohkomuk88, kunkohteâadteáe ohke, kah touishinne ohke.
50.13 Newutche ummusquanittam8onk Jehovah matta piṣh ayeuonganinn8, qut piṣh mamusse touwushin: nishnoh pasuk noh kezqush[a]dt Babylon piṣh chepshau, kah pish quequssumau wame wuttininneaongoh.
50.14 Ayeuuhkonittue wunappéhtók Babylon waeenu: wame kenaau wonki[n]ógish ohtomp, pumók, wohquánittadteohk kounkquodtash, newutche matcheneheau Jehovahoh.
50.15 Mishont8wak waéenu: noh magou wunnutcheg, ukquenohtagómash penushaash, ukqussukqunneutunkaṣh penushaash: newutche ne wutann8taonk Jehovah; ann8tók, ne ásit, ne unnéheuk.
50.16 Tummehtoh8k ohkehteaénin wutch Babylon, kah noh nohtónuk sickle, kepenumuk: newutche wabesuóntamwog sunukkutchóh8wae togkodteg, nag piṣh quinnuppeog nishnoh pasuk en ummussinninnúmut, kah nag piṣh ushpuhh8waog nishnoh pasuk en nehenwonche wutohtuóut.
50.17 Israel naswáiyeue sheep, qunnon8og wutama8hkauóuh: negonne Assyriae ketass8t ummahchipwunneàpuh kah maumachish noh Nebuchadnezzar Babylone ketass8t uppohquétahhamauoh wuskonaṣh.
50.18 Newajeh yeu n8wadt Jehovah ayeuteaunit um-Manitt8moh Israel, kusseh, nussasametah Babilone ketass8t & wutohke, neane sasamatahwhogkup Assyriae ketass8t.
50.19 Kah wonk nuppas8 Israel ut wutáyeuonganit, kah noh piṣh nadtupp8wongam Carmel kah Bashan, kah ukketeahogkounoh piṣh taphéoneuh ut Ephraimme kah Gileade wadchuut.
50.20 Ut yeush kesukkodtash, kah na ahquompag, wussin Jehovah, ummatcheseonk Israel piṣh natinnehamun, kah piṣh wannehenn8: kah ummatcheseongash Judah, kah matta piṣh namehteauouunash; newutche nutahquontamauoog neg wadchanogeg.
50.21 Ayeuuhkonittue kuhkuhquéhtam8k wutohke Merathaim, ayeuuhkontamunat, kah ayeuuhkonittue wadohkitcheg Pekod, mahtupán8k kah papaquanne paguan8k asuhk8e nag, wussin Jehovah, kah ussish wame neanann8nun.
50.22 Mishont8wae mattompog ut ohkeit, kah mishe pagu[a]nuonk.
50.23 Uttoh en wut-hammerum mamusse ohke poskehthamun, kah pohquenumun? uttoh en Babilon tauishitteauun ut kenugke wutohtimóneat.
50.24 Kupponamoush ahpeh, kah kuppitham woi Babilon, kah matta k8wâun, kenamhetteap kah wonk kuppitham, newutche kutáyeuuhkon Jehovah.
50.25 Jehovah pohquánum ukkenauwameekommuk, kah sohh8wuttau ummusquanittam8e auwohteaongash, newutche yeu wutanakausuonk Lord Jehovah ayeuhteaunit, ut wutohtuóut Caldeansog.
50.26 Ayeuuhkon8k wutch aongkoue s[ù]ssippoiyeuut, wôshinum8k ummaumachiekommukquash; ogque unnúhteagk nomwunkquag; kah papaquanne paguanok: ahque teag sequnnum[ó]k.
50.27 Nehtók wame wutoxinumoh: womussehettich en ahhut nushit: missi wutonkapunnaongan8 newutche ukkesukkodtum peyom8, natauwaháe wutaquompiyeum8.
50.28 OOwadtauatonkqussuongan8 neg wasemwutcheg wutch Babilone ohkeit: wahteauwáhuónat ut Zion wuttann8taonk Jehovah num-Manitt8mun, wut-Templumme [á]nn8taonk.
50.29 Miyáe wehkomok pepummuwaenuog ayeuuhkonittue Babilon: wame kenaau w[o]o[n]kinogish ahtomp, weenuhkók: howán pohquohhogitch: ununkquodtok neaunak wutanakausuonk: neaunak wame wutusseonk ne unnéhúk: newutche noh pehtuanum8óneau Jehovah, ayeuuhkonittue 8neetupanatam8moh Israel.
50.30 Newaj piṣh 8skeneumoh penushónit ut mayit, kah wame wutayeúhteaenéumoh piṣh tummehtahwhóninneuh ne kesukok, wussin Jehovah.
50.31 Kusseh, kutayeuuhkonsh woi ken mahshe pittuanumweon wussin Lord Jehovah ayeuhteaunit: newutche kukkesukodtum peyom8, ahquompi neadt nátauwáhhun.
50.32 Kah mahshe pittuanumwit piṣh togkussittassun kah penushau, kah matta piṣh howan wutomohkinuh: kah piṣh nunnashqunnanum n8tau ut ukkeitotanahtu, kah piṣh mahchikussum8m8 wame waeenu.
50.33 Yeu wussin Jehovah ayeuteaunit, wunnaumonuh Israel, kah wunnaumonuh Judah, moeu sunnukkutchahwhoog, kah wame neg masinóuhteacheg, ummenuhkinóuh, sekenamwog ummoncheáhónaóont.
50.34 Uppohquohwussuaéneumoh menuhkesuoh, Jehovah ayeuhteaunit ussowesu, noh piṣh papannuppe ukken8tamwanshuh onk woh wutanwôhsiteauunat ohke, kah woh 8wogkouwéhheonat wadohkinitche Babilon.
50.35 Togkodteg nuhkuhkongquog Caldeansog, wussin Jehôvah, kah wadohkitcheg Babilon, ut wussontimomut kah 8waantam8mut.
50.36 Togkodteg nuhkuhkongquog pann8waenuog, kah nag piṣh as8ke usseog, togkodteg nuhkuhkauau ummenuhkesueneumoh, kah nag piṣh chepshaog.
50.37 Togkodteg nuhkuhkauau wut$horsesumoh[,] kah wut[-]chariotumash, kah ut wame kenukshae missinninnùut ut wunnash[ó]mut, kah nag piṣh tatuppeyeu8og mittamwossisut: togkodteg nuhkuhkom8m8 wunnompekouunash, kah piṣh mukk8kinnuwontamunash.
50.38 Nunohteau ut wunnippemut, kah niṣh piṣh nunnohtaash, newutche ne nunneukontunkanne ohke, kah nag kogkee ahchuánumaog wuttinneukontunkanóuh.
50.39 Newaj piṣh touohkomukque puppinashimwog kah munnahhanne puppinashimwog na pish 8tohkinneau, kah k8k8kh[â]usog na piṣh 8tohkinneau: & matta pish wonk wutohkei[n] micheme, kah matta piṣh wutohkein wutch pometuonganit onk yaan pometuonganit.
50.40 Neane God kepuhteop Sodom kah Gomorrah kah weetatteamunguh, wussin Lord? ne ne matta pish howan wutappein kah matta wosketompae wunnaumoniin pish 8tohkein[.]
50.41 Kusseh, missinninnuog pish 8mwog nannumiyeu, kah mishe wutohimoin, kah monaog ketass8tamwog pish tahshinon, wutch sussippoi ohkeit.
50.42 Nag pish kogkôunnaog ohtompe, kah qunuhtug, nag onkapunuhteaenu8og, kah matta monanetea8og: 8wadtauatonkqussuongan8 pish ogque mishont8wom8 keitahhannit, kah nag pish nayeumukquog horsesoh nish$noh pasuk ogquhhausu ayeuittimuk, ayeuuhkonittue ken woi Babylone wuttaunin.
50.43 Babylone ketass8t n8tam unaunchem8wonaongan8, kah wunnutchegash n8chumwiyeuash onkquommom8onk wuttohqunuh, kah ogque onkquommom8 mittamwossis neechadt.
50.44 Kusseh noh pish ogque kuhkuhqueu qunnon8ut wutch ummogquesuonganit Jordan, ut wut[a]yeuong[a]nit manuhkesit: qut nag teanuk n8semowaheaog: kah howan noh pepenaue wosketomp onk woh nah nanawunnumwaheonuh, newutche howan aniit, kah howan kohquttumiit ahquompi, kah howan noh nanaushipseaen noh neepauit anaquabeh?
50.45 Newut[c]he n8tam8k ukkogahqutteam8onk Jehovah, ne nemunuk ayeuuhkonittue Babylon, kah ukkesantam8ongash nish ayeuuhkonittue kesantogish wutohke Caldeansog: wunnamuhkut noh peississit ut flockut pish wussohwhunuh, wunnamuhkut pish touwishittea8 wutayeuonk weeche nahoh.
50.46 Ut 8wadtauatonkqussuonganit Babylone tohqunnumunat, ohke ontohteau, kah mauonk n8tunkquadt ut kenugke wutohtimoneat.
51.1 YEu wussin Lord, kusseh nutayéuuhkonittue waabenumau Babylon, kah nag nashaue ayitcheg, neg waabehtunkqueâneg, pagwohteae waban.
51.2 Kah nutann8n fanonuhsuenuog en Babylon nah pish fa[u]nonahetticheh, kah pish sequnnumwog wutohke: newutche wuttamehpunae kesukodtut pish waeenu wutayeuuhkonouh.
51.3 Ayeuuhkonittue noh wadtu[u]kinont ahtompe, pepummuwaenin wuttunkinonch wutohtompeh: kah ayeuuhkonittue noh waapinuk up-brigandineum: wohquanumuhkon 8skeneumoh, papaquane pagwohteau wame ukkenauwameumoh.
51.4 Yeu pish wuttinne penushoneau nashitcheg ut wutohtuout C[a]ldeansog, kah neg pannuppetawhutcheg ut wuttaumaogk8mut.
51.5 Newutche Israel matta ohquanumau[,] kah Judah um-Manitt8moh, kah nashpe Jehovaoh ayeuteaunittoh tohkonogque wutohk8 numwohteau ummatcheketeaongan8 8neetup[a]natam8moh Israel
51.6 Wusseemok wutch nashauwe Babylon, kah pohquohwhunonch, nishnoh pasuk ukketeahogkôunoh, tummetawhutteateok ut ummatcheseonganit: newutche yeu ahquompi wutann8táonk Jehovah; neh piṣh wutonkquatauoh.
51.7 Bablyon ne golde wuttattamwaitch ut wunnutcheganit Jehovah, ne kogkeissippamwáheont wame ohke: wutohtimoinneunk wuttattamwog 8wineum, newaj wutohtimoineash kogkey[ô]m8uk.
51.8 Babylon kenuppe penusheau, kah paguatauun: 8n8wansh8k, neemunum8k balme wutch wutonkquommom8onk, tohneit woh neetskéhit.
51.9 Nukkodneetskéheómun Babylon, qut noh matta neetskeheuh: ohquanumok, kah ontuh nishnoh pasuk wutohkit: newutche wussumáonk mussishin kesukqut, kah tohshinnumun wehque pohkuhqut.
51.10 Jehovah sohh8wuttau nussampweusseonganun: peyunk kah wahteauwáhuwadtuh ut Zion wutusseonk Jehovah um-Manitt8m.
51.11 Wôóhsuppánumok kôuhquodtaṣh: moenum8k ogqunnegash Jehovah tahshinau wuttahh8uh Medse ketass8tamwog: newutche ukkesantam8onk ayeuhkontam8m8 Babylon pagwatauunat, newutche ne wutann8taonk Jehovah, wut-templumme ann8taonk.
51.12 Neepattau8k muttaag ut Babylone hassunneutunkanit, menehketeau8k askuhwheteaonk: wunash8k askuhwheteaénin: quagwashwehtam8k tummushkôsuongash, newutche Lord kesantam kah mahche ussen, ne ayeuhkonittue [à]nomp Babylon.
51.13 Woi ken wadohkéan eiyáne nippekontu, monatash kenompak8unash, k8wohkukquossin8onk peyom8, kah numwohtae kutaháhchuwontam8onk.
51.14 Lord ayeuhteaunit chadchekeyeuau nashpe nehenwonche nagum, n8wau, wunnamuhkut kutogque numwohtoush wosketompaog m8paut, kah nag piṣh kussáshquónukquog.
51.15 Ayimup ohke nashpe ummenuhkesuonk, menehketeauop ohke nashpe 8waantamoonk, noh sepágenumup kesukquaṣh nashpe 8wohwohtam8onk.
51.16 Mishant8adt, móneau nippeash ut kesukqut, waabehteau ouwan, wutch weekqshik ohke, ukkutshámunáhteau nashpe sokanon, sohh8wunau wabanoh wutch wunnompak8unéhtu.
51.17 Nishnoh pasuk puppinashimweyeu8 ut wohwohtam8onganit: nishnoh pasuk noh sabahsausit chepshau nashpe wuttinneukontungok, newutche wussabassumwe wuttinneukontunkoh, pann8waongannù8oh, kah matta wunnashaonganéog.
51.18 Nag tahn8cheyeu8og, pann8wáe usseonk, natauwáhit piṣh pagwan[ù]og.
51.19 Wuchippiyeum Jakob matta tatuppéi[n]8, newutche noh kahkénauwéhteunk wame, kah Israel uppogkomungane ohtoonk: Jehovah ayeuhteaunit ne 8wesuonk.
51.20 Ken nummattompágwe togkunk, kah nummattompagwe auwohteaonk, newutche nashpe ken nuppohquetahham wutohtimóneash, kah nashpe ken nuppagwadtoh ass8tam8ongash.
51.21 Kah nashpe ken nussukquttoh horses kah neh na8moncheh, kah nashpe ken nuppohquttahham chariotsash, kah neh na8mukqut.
51.22 Nashpe ken wonk nussukquttoh wosketomp kah mittamwossis, kah n[a]shpe ken nussukquttoh kutchis kah wusken, kah nashpe ken nussukqutt[o]h wusken, kah|peaomp.
51.23 Nashpe ken wonk nussukquttoh nanáushepsaen kah uf-flockum, kah nashpe ken nussukquttoh ohkehteaen, kah we-yoke oxinumoh, kah nashpe ken nussoquetoh mugquompaog, kah nananuwaénuoh.
51.24 Kah nutonkquttau Babylon, kah wadohkitcheg Caldea, wame machuk ne asehettit ut Zion, anaquabeóg wussin Jehovah.
51.25 Kusseh, kutayeuhkonsh woi ken pagwohteae wadchu, wussin Lord, ken pagwatauan wame ohke, kah nussumagkinum nuhpit ut kuhhogkat, kah k8w8mhenuṣh wutch qussukquanóhtu, kah kutchikohtaé wadchukonsh.
51.26 Kah nag matta piṣh neemunumóog náshine qussuk wutch ken, asuh quenohtagane qussuk, qut piṣh kummicheme touwushin wussin Jehovah.
51.27 Neepatto8k muttaagk ut ohkeit, p8tantam8k monopuhpegk ut kenugke wutohtimóineash: ayeuhkonittue nanashwunnumok wutohtimóneash, ayeuhkonittue moeu wehquetumok Araratte ketass8tamwog, Minni kah Ashkenaz; ayeuhkonittue kukquttumok mugquompuh:
51.28 Ayeuhkonittue nanashwunnumok wutohtimóneash, weeche Medse ketass8tamwog, umummugquompomuh, kah wunnanauwunnuaéneumoh, kah wame wunnanauwunnumóe ohkeit.
51.29 Kah ohke piṣh nunnuksheau, kah neuantam: newutch nishnoh ukkesantam8onk Lord piṣh wutussen ayeuhkonittue Babylon, touishitteauunat Babylone ohke, matta wutohkeéinneat.
51.30 Babylone menuhkésuenuog ahquiyeuhteáog: nag appuog 8wonkon8sinn8óut: ummenuhkesuongan8 mahtsheau, tatuppeyeu8og mittamwussisut, nag chikossumwog wutáyeuongan8, up-barsumash pokqshaash.
51.31 Pasuk quogqueaenin pish quogqueu nogkishkauonat onkatogeh, kah pasuk ann8naen nogkushkauonat onkatuk, nahtinonat Babylone ketass8t, ukkeitotan sohkomun ut nequtchippaiyeuut.
51.32 Kah pomushaongash kuppuhhausuash, kah weekinaskquash chikohtaash n8taut, & ayeuhteaenuog t8weshaog.
51.33 Newutche yeu wussin Jehovah áyeuteaunit um-Manitt8moh Israel, wuttaunoh Babylon tatuppeyu8oh tanuppogguhham8onganit, utt8cheyeu8 ne adt woh pogguhwhut, qut pasweyeu8 kah kepenumwae ahquompi peyaum8.
51.34 Nebuchàdnezar Babylone ketass8t, nummahchipuk nussunukkuhhuk, nummachishquohkonuk: nutogque misheashquonuk dragonsut, wameechummehteau wunnogkus n8nummeechumash, nussohwhuhkonuk.
51.35 Chekee unnehettuonk, kah ut neyausut nuhkuhkaj Babylon, wadohkitcheg Zion ne pish n8waog; kah n8sqheonk nuhkuhkonkqhettich wadohkitcheg Caldea, ne Jerusalem n8wau.
51.36 Newutche yeu wussin Jehovah, kusseh nukken8tamwontam kuttinniyeuonk, kutann8tauwanshush, kah nunnanassum ukkethann8m, kah nunnunassum wuttuhkekomeumash.
51.37 Kah Babylon pish numwonkquaenu8, wutayeuongan8 Dragonsog, chepshaonk, kah quekqs[u]ontam8onk, matta ayeinat.
51.38 Nag pish moae ogque chequttumwog qunnon8ut, kah pish ogque 8nwog qunnonuemesit.
51.39 Kósobpishettit, nummishadtup, kah nukkogkeissippamwaheaog, onk woh weekontámwog, kah woh micheme koueog, kah matta t8hkeog, wussin Jehovah.
51.40 Nag nutogque womussuunoog Lambsut nushonaout, onatuh ramsog weeche nomposhimwe goatsut.
51.41 Uttoh en Sheshak tohqunau? kah uttoh en mamusse ohkee waéenoaonk sohkomun? uttoh en Babylon chépshontamun ut kenugke wutohtimoineat.
51.42 Keitoh kuhkuhquemo Babylon: noh puttogguhkunk nashpe monacheg tuhk8oh.
51.43 Ukkeitotan8mash touishineash, nunohtae ohke, kah touohkomuk, ohke ne matta howan ayek, kah matta wosketompae wunnaumoniin na pomushaun.
51.44 Kah nussasamatah Bel ut Babylon, kah nussohh8wauttau wutch wutt8nut, ne mase[a]shqut, kah wutohtimoinneash matta pish wonk moae miyaehtunk8h, nux Babylone hassunneutu[u]k pish penusheau.
51.45 Nummissinninnúmog sohham8k wutch wunnashómut, kah pohquohwhunok nishnoh ukketeahogkôunoh wutch ummishe musquantam8onganit Jehovah.
51.46 Kah ishkont kuttahhou nupp8m8, kah kukquehtamumw8 nashpe wadtaúatonkquodt ne piṣh n8tamuk ut ohkeit: wadtauatonkquodt piṣh peyaum8 nequt kodtumwae, kah ompetak onkatog kodtumm8 piṣh peyaum8 wadtauatonkquodt, kah chekeeusseonk ut ohkeit, nanawunnuwaén ayeuuhkóne nanawunnuaènúh.
51.47 Newutche kusseh, kesukodtaṣh peyaum8, n8sum kogoksumwe nunneukontunkanog ut Babylon, kah mamusse wutohke piṣh chepshaog, kah wame neh náhtaúutcheh piṣh penushauh ut wunnashómut.
51.48 Neit kesuk kah ohke, kah wame ne na ohtag piṣh ket8hamwóntamwog Babylon: newutche neg magk8kinoncheg piṣh uppeyaóunouh wutch nanummiyeu, wussin Jehovah.
51.49 Neane Babylon penusháheont adt nushitcheg Israel: ne piṣh wuttinne ut Babylon penushoneau nashitcheg ut wame ohkeit.
51.50 Kenaau pohquohhamógish togkodteg, monchegk, neepo8k, nôadtit en ne mehquánumok Lord, kah Jerusalem peyom8utch kummequontam8ongan8óut.
51.51 Nutchepshámun newutche n8tamumun kekont8onk, akodchuonk nukkuhkom nuskesukqunónash, newutche penuwohteaog petutteaog ut wunneetupanatamwe ayeuonganéhtu Jehovah wekit.
51.52 Newutche kusseh, kesukodtaṣh peyom8, wussin Jehovah, piṣh n8sum ukkogoksumwe nunnúkontunkoh, kah pannuppe wame wutohkeit n8chumwéhtahhamauitcheh piṣh ha[u]uhhóm8oh.
51.53 Tôkonoguqe Babylo[n] woh kuhkuhquem8ut en kesukqut, kah tôkô piṣh unogque ummenuhkehteauun ukqunuhqui menuhkesuonk, onch wutch nuhhogkat woskehuaénúh piṣh peyaónuk wussin Jehovah.
51.54 Maue wadtauatonkqussuonk 8m88 Babylon, kah mishe pagwanuonk wutch wutohtuout Caldeansog.
51.55 Newutche Jehovah matchehteo Babylon, kah pagwodtau mishe wadtauatonkqussuonk wutch wuhhogkat, wuttukk8moh agque mishont8ánit mishe nippéit, mishont8wae 8wadtauatonkqussuongan8 sohwhunumun.
51.56 Newutche woskehuwaen wunnuhkuhkauuh, ut Bablyon, kah ummenuhkesuéneumoh tohqunóneuh, nishnoh pasuk wutohtompeh pohquésuoh, newutche Jehovah ôadtehteáe Manit, piṣh wunnamuhkut wutonkquatauoh.
51.57 Kah nukkogkeissippamwáh wussontimomoh, kah 8waantam8moh, ummugquompomo[h], kah w[u]nnanawunn[u]énúh, kah ummenuhkesuénúmoh: kah nag piṣh micheme kouéog, kah matta t8hkeog, wussin ketass8t noh as8wénit Lord ut ayeuteaunit.
51.58 Yeu wussin Jehovah ayeuteaunit, Babylone mishe kishkinneutongash piṣh pokshaash kah ukqunuhkqui squontamash piṣh chikohtaash n8taut, kah missinninnúog piṣh tahn8tanakausuog, kah auwâog n8taut, kah piṣh sauunumwog.
51.59 Wuttinn8waonk ne Jeremiah quoshodtumwaen ann8nau Serajahoh wunnaumonuh Neriah, wunnaumonuh Maasejah, weechauont Zedechiahoh, Judae ketass8toh en Babylon, yaue kodtumwae nanauwinnuwadt, kah yeuoh Serajah manunnissue Sontimó8.
51.60 Neit Jeremiah wussukhum ut b8kut wame machuk ne piṣh nohkuhkom8m8uk Babylon: wame yeush kutt8wongash nish wasukkuhwhosikish ayeuhkonittue Babylon.
51.61 Kah Jeremiah unnau Serajahoh, pey[o]an Babylon, kah nauman, kah ogketaman wame yeush kutt8wongash.
51.62 Neit pish kussim, woi Jehovah, yeu kutayeuhkonittue ken8tamun ayeuonk, tummehthamunat, onk woh mo howan wutappein, wosketomp asuh puppinashim, kah ne piṣh touwushin micheme.
51.63 Kah piṣh nnih mahche ogketaman yeu b8k, piṣh k8wéenadtippinun qussuk, kah kuttinuhkon nashaue Euphrates.
51.64 Kah piṣh kussim, yeu pish wuttinne quttauwushun Babylon, kah matta piṣh omohku wutch machuk ne piṣh nohkinnumauog, kah nag pish sauunumwog, yeu wéhque ukkutt8wongaṣh Jeremiah.
52.1 ZEdechiah neesneechage kah nequtta kodtumwohkomup n8che nanauwunn[u]wadt, kah nabo nequtta kodtumwaeu nanawunnuau ut Jerusalem, kah ohkasoh ussowesuoh Hamutall wuttaunoh Jeremiah wul[-]Libnah.
52.2 Kah ussu ne machuk ut wuskesukqut Jehovah, neaunak wame wutusseonk Jehojakim.
52.3 Newutche nashpe ummusquantam8onk Jehovah n$niyeup ut Jerusalem, kah ut Judah, nô pajeh uppogkenónat wutch anaquabit, Zedechiah cheketauau Babylone ketass8toh.
52.4 Kah n$niyeup pasuk8gun adtahshe kodtumwae nanawunnuadt, piogqussit nepauz, piogquequinohhog nepauz, Nebuchadnezzar Babylone ketass8t peyau, nagum kah wame ukkenauwammúmoh, ayeuhkontamunat Jerusalem, kah ayeuuhkonittue wutappehtamun, kah 8wonkon8sinuhkontamun waéenu.
52.5 Neit keitotan wéenuhkomunáh, nô pajeh nabowunnukqutte kodtum8mit Zedechiah.
52.6 Kah ut yaue nepauzsaut, pasuk8gun adtahshikqunúhhog nepauz, mahshagquodt unkqueneunkquodt ut otanat, newaj matta petukqunneganinn8g wutche ohkee missinninnuog.
52.7 Neit keitotan sohqshau, kah wame ayeuhteaenuog wussem8og, kah sohhamwog wutch otanat nuhkonaeu, squontame mayut nashaue neutunkanit, ne kishkohtag ketass8t wuttittanohketeaonganit (kah Caldeansog weenuhkomog otan) kah auog mukoshquttae mayut.
52.8 Qut Caldeanse kenauwameonk n8swetahwhaog ketas8toh, kah mattanaog Zedechiahoh ut Jerichoe mukoshquttaut, kah wame ukkenauwamumoh seahsh[á]uh.
52.9 Neit tohqunaog ketass8t, kah wutuss8unouh en Babylone ketass8tamwut ut Riblah ut Hamathe ohkeit: uttoh ad wussumup.
52.10 Kah Babylone ketass8t, nushau wunnaumonuh Zedechiah ut anaquabenit: nushau wonk wame Judae Sontimuh ut Riblah
52.11 Neit kajkesukquanau Zedechiahoh, kah Babylone ketass8t wuttattogkuppinuh chainsash wutuss8unuh Babylon, kah ukkupshagkinuh, nó pajeh wunnupinat.
52.12 Kah napanna tahshe nepauz piogquequinohhog nepauz (ne nabo pasuk8gun tahshe ukkodtum8m Nebuchadnezzar Babylone ketass8t) Nebuzarradan askuhwheteae mugquomp, noh wadtininneumuhkauont Babylone ketass8t, petutteau Jerusalem.
52.13 Kah chikkossum wek Jehovah, kah ketass8t wek, kah wame Jerusalemme wetuomash, kah wame wekuoash masugkenukeg chikossumunash ut n8taut.
52.14 Kah wame Caldeanse kenauwameog, neg weetomoncheg askuhwheteae mugquompoh nag pohqshadtauog Jerusaleme hassunneutongash waeenu.
52.15 Neit Nebuzarradan askuhwhetae mugquomp, missinohteau matchekuoh, kah askqshoncheg missinninnuog neg apitcheg otanat kah neg amashoncheg en Babylone ketass8tamut, kah sekqshoncheg monacheg.
52.16 Qut Nebuzarradan askuhwhetae mugquomp sequnau machekinitcheh ut ne ohkeit, wanteunkeg weenominneash kah ohkehteaenuog.
52.17 Wonk brasse pillarsash wonk nish ohtagish wekit Jehovah, kah basesash kah brasse keitoh, nish ohtagish wekit Jehovah Caldeansog sohquttahhamunaash kah monchadtoog wame brasse en Babylon.
52.18 Cauldronsash wonk, kah shovelsash, kah snuffersash, kah wunnonkanash, kah kenamoog, kah brasse auwohteaongash, nish nashpe wowussumahetticheh, nash wunnemunnumunaoash.
52.19 Kah bas[i]nsash, kah n8taeponsash kah wu[sin]onkanash kah cauldronsash, kah wequananteganuhtugquash, kah kenamog, kah cupsash, nish goldu8hish, ut goldut, nish silvereu8gish, ut silverut, askuhwheteae mugquomp wutamaunumussash.
52.20 Neenash pillersash, pasuk keitoh, nabo nees8og brasse bulsog, neg agwapehcheg basesut, nish ketass8t Solomon ayikupash ut wekit Jehovah, ne brasse ut wame yeu auwohteaonganit, matta quttuhwhosin8.
52.21 Kah papaume pillarsash ne sohkunkqussit pasuk pillar nabo swosuk tashishquanogkut, kah pemuneat nabo neesihquanogog weenompósu, ne an8ke kishkag yauunash muttinwhunutcheash: puhpuhtiyeup.
52.22 Brasse muhpuhkuk quenahtop nesohkunkquok pasuk muhpuhkuk napanna tashishquanogok, hashabanakausuonk, kah pomgranatsash quenohtopash muhpuhkukqut waeenu, wame wompohshag: kah nahohtoeu wonk pillar, & pomgranatsash, neyaneyeu8.
52.23 Kah pask8gun tahshinchagkodtash kah nequtta pomgranatsash sussippoeu, kah wame Pomgranatsash ut hashabpae anakausuongánit nequt pasuk88ash quinnuppu.
52.24 Kah askuhwhetae Mugquomp tohqunau Serajah kehche sephausuenuh, kah Zephaniah nahohtôeu sephausuen, kah nishuog nanawehteunkig ushsquont.
52.25 Amaunau wonk wutch otanat Eunuch, noh nanawunont ayeuhteaenutcheh, kah nesausuk tahsuog neg kishkappehtauoncheg ketass8toh, neg namhetcheg ut keitotanat, kah kehche kenauwamee Scribe, maiyapheont ohkee missinninnuog, kah nequtta tahshinchagkodtog ohkee missinninnuog, neg namhetcheg ut nashaue otanat.
52.26 Neit Nebuzaradan askuhwheteae mugquomp nah wunneemunuh, kah nah uppas8uh ut Babylone ketass8tamwut ut Riblah.
52.27 Kah Bablyone ketass8t nah wutt[o]gkomuh, kah wunnush[u]h ut Riblah, ut Hamathe ohkeit, yeu unne Judah missinohkonuh wutch nehenwonche wutohkeit.
52.28 Yeug missinninnuog Nebuchadnezzar masinóhteapah ut nesausuk tahshe kodtum8ut, nishwudt muttannonganog kussuog Jewsog, kah neesneechagkodtog kah shuog.
52.29 Nabo shwosuk wutteashe kodtum8mut Nebuchadnezzar, missinóhteauup wutch Jerusalem shwosuk tahshe pasuk88oh, shwinchagkodtoh kah neesuoh.
52.30 Neesneechage kah nishwe kodtum8mut[,] Nebuchadnezzar, Nebuzaradan askuhwheteae mugquomp missinóhteau Jewsoh, nesausuk tahshe pasuk88oh yauunchag, kah napanna tahsuoh, wame missinninnúog yauut muttannonganog kussuog kah nequtta tahshit pasuk88og.
52.31 Kah n$nihyeup, shwinchage kah enatuh tahshe kodtum8 ummissinnoóonk Jehojakim Judae ketass8t, ut naboneese nepauzsaut, naboneesnechage kah napanna adtahshikquinok, Evil$merodach Babylone ketass8t, negonne kodtum8e nanawunnuadt, tahshinum uppuhkuk Jehojakim Judae ketass8t, kah wussohh8wunuh wutch kuppishagkinittuonganit.
52.32 Kah 8womoausuont8wanumauoh, kah wut[á]nuwonkquottauoh wutappuonk, wuttappuongan8 ketass8tamwog, neh weetomukqutcheh ut Babylon.
52.33 Kah ôs8wunum ukkuppishagkinae hogk8ongash: kah nagwutteae meechwoh petukqununk ut anaquabit, nisohke pomantog.
52.34 Kah wutch ummeetsuonk, nagwutteae wutchippiyeum aninnumauau nashpe Babylone ketass8t, pajeh kesukodte wunnupp8onganit, tohsohkepomantog.
